sanatkumāra saṃhitāyām śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ prapadyet evam ī śānam sarvajñam aparājitam saṃbhavam sarva bhūtānām anādi viśvatomukham veda ādau yaḥ svaraḥ proktaḥ oṃkāra ākhyaḥ maheśvaraḥ sṛjate sarva bhūtāni paṃcabhūtaiḥ sadāśivaḥ sāṃkhyānām paramam yogam vrataiḥ pāśupataiḥ tathā rakṣā artha sarva jaṃtūnām tridhā ātmānam sṛjati ajaḥ sa saṃjñayā tu bhagavān ekaḥ eva maheśvaraḥ prajvalantam mahā śūlam ghora rūpam mahā aśanim nānā krīḍanakaiḥ devaḥ krīḍate yoga māyayā dayitā ardha vapuḥ rutvā nṛtya āraṃbhe sthitaḥ haraḥ tad bhaktyā saṃpravakṣyāmi purāṇam śiva bhāṣitam parāśarasya dāyādaḥ śrīmān satyavatī sutaḥ brahmarṣiḥ saca dharma ātma akāla yoga vidām varaḥ ṛṣi saṃdhaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śrutaiḥ iva pitāmahaḥ bhārate śatasāhakhyām saṃhitāyām kavi īśvaraḥ caturdhā avyasya matimān iiśaṣyān ca adhyāpayat pṛthak teṣām sukha upaviṣṭānām kathām kathayatām parām tatra ca adhyātma dharma ātma abrahmaṇaḥ tanayaḥ śubhaḥ anugraha artham ṭaṣīṇām darśanam kṛtavān ṛṣiḥ sa dadarśa sukha āsīnān brahmarṣīn amita ojasaḥ arghyam ācamanīyam ca teṣām dattam ca dharma vid tatas saṃpūjayāmāsa valapīn saṃśi ta vratān anujñātaḥ ca taiḥ sarvaiḥ upaviṣṭaḥ kuśa āsane pṛṣṭaḥ tu ṛṣibhiḥ tatratra hma putraḥ mahā muniḥ prāsādasya acayat puṇyam devadevasya dhīmataḥ mūrtīnām tu vibhāgasya maṃtrasya paramam vidhim sthānān iti aṣṭau asya api rudrasya tu mahātmanaḥ upaviṣṭaiḥ tu bhagavān yogīśaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ tapaḥ veṣa anurūpeṣu āsaneṣu yathāyatham virājati adhikam brahmā taiḥ śva vahmarṣibhiḥ sadā satām madhye ca dharma ātmā bhagavān sūkṣma yoga vid kṛta aṃjali puṭāḥ sarve ṛṣayaḥ tam atha abruvan iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃhitāyām prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ śaivam purāṇam de vasya yat vṛttam tat bravīhinaḥ śaivam purāṇam bhavataḥ śṛṇudhvam dvijasattamāḥ yat śrutvā nirmalāḥ saṃtaḥ tad cittāḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ bhavanti bhāvitātmānaḥ kṛtakṛtya viśeṣataḥ sva rga kāma pradam puṇyam purāṇam veda saṃmitam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇīya sanatkumārasaṃhitā vivṛtau prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ om om namaḥ śivāya atha dvitīye ṛṣibhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ brahma sutaḥ bravīt pāvanam śraddadhānānām iha loke paratra ca prakṛtyā artha adhikāreṇa pradhāna purupa īśvara m kīrtayiṣyāmi iva u viprāḥ purāṇam śiva bhāpitam śrutam purā āmayā vyāsāt devadevasya dhīmataḥ yat aham tat pravakṣyāmi yathā pūrva śrutam mayā saṃkṣepāt ca eva vakṣyāmi pṛthivī ādi yathā tathā saptadvīpasya ca ākhyānam varṣāṇām ca tathā eva ca sanatkumāra vikāṃtam rudrasya vihitam kṛtam ārādhitam mahādevam brahmaṇaḥ tanayena tu vara dānena saṃbaṃdhaḥ muni śiṣya samāgamaḥ bhavanam meru śṛṃgasya brahma viṣṇu maheśvarān vibhīṣaṇasya saṃvādam rudrasya ca mahātmanaḥ sarva tīrtha phalam puṇyam śiva liṃgasya pūjanam liṃga arcana vidhim ca eva devasya pūjanam tathā prāsādasya ca yat puṇyam mahādevasya dhīmataḥ sthāna ādi jyaiṣṭhyam asya api rūpasya tu mahātmanaḥ liṃga saṃsthāpane puṇyam puṣpa dānasya yat phalam dhūpasya ca vidhim ca eva māsānām ca param phalam yathā dvādaśa jyotiḥ liga ādīnām caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām vidhāne vihite phalam nāma aṣṭamī vidhānam ca tathā vailakṣaṇya aṣṭamīm vibhūtim devadevasya īśvarasya ca dhīmataḥ yoganāḍyāḥ tathā ākhyānam mayā a proktam purātanam avimuktasya māhātmyam tathā coṃkāra varṇanam yajñeśvarasya māhātmyam tathā tīrtha anuvarṇanam bhagavat ārādhanam nandeḥ tathā anaṃya bhiṣe canam nīlakaṃṭhasya māhātmyam tripurasya tathā avadhaḥ vāsudevasya māhātmyam vidhānam ca eva tasya ca jñāna praśaṃsanam ca eva mokṣam parama saṃpadam idānīm vi staram citram vibhāgam rūpam aiśvaram āsīt tamaḥ mayam sarvam aprajñātam alakṣaṇam ātmanā sarvam ātmānam saṃciṃtya bhagavān haraḥ manaḥ saṃsṛjate pūrvam mahaṃkāram tu pṛṣṭhatas ahaṃkārāt prajātāni mahābhūtāni paṃca ca aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ proktāḥ vikārāḥ ca eva ṣoḍaśa śabdaḥ sparśaḥ ca rūpam ca rasaḥ gaṃdhaḥ tathā eva ca prāṇa upānaḥ samāna śvā audānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca satvam rajaḥ tamaḥ ca eva guṇāḥ proktāḥ tu te trayaḥ tasmāt bhagavataḥ brahmā a tasmāt viṣṇuḥ ajāyata tasmāt parataram na asti na asti tasmāt param śivam brahmā viṣṇu śrva dvau etau udbhūtau śaṃkarāḥ ttutau tapasā āharate ca eva nānā bhūtāni sarvaśas dina ekam brahmaṇaḥ proktam niśā kalpaḥ tathā ācyate evam māsam ca varṣam ca tathā varṣa śatam dvijāḥ evamādi parārdhī toharasi ani miṣaḥ smṛtaḥ brahma ādi staṃba paryaṃtam nimiṣaḥ ca maheśvaraḥ nimiṣaṃjīvitam sarva caṃdra ādīnām grahaiḥ saha pātālam sutalam tālam vitalam talam eva ca paṃcamam viddhi pātālam rukma sauvarṇikam smṛtam saptamam śarkarābhūmiḥ aṣṭamam vijayam smṛtam prakhyātāḥ aṣṭaupātālavāsinaḥ aṃte rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ evam prakurute lokān krīḍā artham tu maheśvaraḥ brahmaloka parīmāṇa gatiḥ ūrdhva vivarṇitā pṛthi samuccayaṃgirīṇām ca anukramaṇa saṃkhyayā samudrāṇām ca vistāram pramāṇam ca tathā śṭaṇu sthāvarāṇām carāṇām ca devānām ca divaukasām catuṣpāda dvipādānām dhārmikān karma mokṣakān sa hasraguṇam ākhyātam sthāvarāṇām prakīrtitam saha saṃpāda hīna aśvāḥ iti āha bhagavāśivaḥ maheśvaraḥ paraḥ teṣām sarveṣām deva mānuṣāt evam saṃkhyā atra saṃkhyātā sarvajñena svayaṃbhuvā eṣām māheśvaram jñānam bhakti maṃtraiḥ prakīrtitam ekam jñānam namasyaṃti abhūtam bhūta saṃjñakam nirguṇam nirmalam jñānam śaṃkareṇa pracoditam ṛṣīṇām śrotu kāmānām bhaktānām ca dṛḍha vrata śrāvitam jñāna sarvasvam purāṇeṣu ca gīyate tatas jñānam param śreṣṭha proktam īśena dhīmatā brāhmaṇānām hita arthāya sarva varṇe viśeṣataḥ yathā saṃbhavati jñānam tathā īśaḥ pravartate aham ādi śva madhyam ca aham ca te ca saṃsthitaḥ krīḍā rtham īhate vyāsaḥ utpannamatiḥ avyayaḥ tatas kālaḥ hi bhagavān saḥ abhidhyāya śiva ājñayā kurvan prakṛti nāma nāmataḥ tasmāt brahmā apraka utpannaḥ saha viṣṇunā pāda hīnān kān caturtha pāda hīna aṃśvaḥ ācāraiḥ avahiṣkṛtān pṛthivīṃcām diśaḥ ca eva makalpayat lokālokasya saṃkhyānam dvipadām uddheḥ tathā saritām sāgarāṇām ca tīrthāni āyatanāni ca ulkā nipātam ketum ca jyotiṣāṃpatanāni api evam sarva artha saṣṭāvai codyamānaḥ śivena vai utpannam ca eva tat sarvam bhūyas kālena pīḍyate vyāsauvā ca katham brahmā a samutpannaḥ katham sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate āsīt tamaḥ mayam ca etat na prājñāyata kiṃcana tatas śivaḥ mahādevaḥ yogadhṛk satu sarvaśas tasmāt pṛthvī tvam āpannam tasmāt āpaḥ tatobhuvaḥ tat tamaḥ udārayāmāsa āpaḥ bhūtvā tu śaṃkaraḥ tasmāt tuteja sā ca eva vāyunā ca sadā akṣipan tasmāt aṃḍa samutpattiḥ tatas nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ apām cāgneya asaṃyogāt agniḥ tejaḥ śva saṃbhavaḥ vāyoḥ apivikurvāṇāt ākāśam abhavat tadā saṃghātaśvā abhavat pṛthvī eṣām māheśvarī tanuḥ atra praviśya hi jalam nimiṣa ardha pramāṇataḥ tatas brahmā samutpannaḥ adbhiḥ nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ bhagavān uṣitvā a parivatsarān tatas vaibrāhmaṇaḥ jajñe kāle kālena coditaḥ atha vyoma diśa śva aṣṭau apām sthānam ca śāśvatam tatas sakālam adhyetu saḥ atha sṛṣṭim athā akarot iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃhitāyām tīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ mahataḥ tu tatas brahmā tasmāt rahmāṃḍa tām gataḥ samudrāḥ tasya rudhiram ākāśam udaram tathā pavanaḥ ca eva niḥśvāsaḥ tejas nirnimnagā rasaḥ ākāśa tamasī śrotre caṃdra arkau nayanau smṛ tau pṛthivī aṃte samudra aśva samudra aṃte tamaḥ smṛtam rasātala aṃte salilam tasyati pannaga adhipāḥ tad aṃte punar ākāśam tasya api aṃte punar jalam tejasā uṃtetadā aṃḍasya dhāraṇāt sadma mahataḥ śva mahātmanaḥ evam brahmāṃḍam iti uktam mahā dhāraṇam ucyate yaḥ yathā yasya yoni tva etam pravakṣyāmi aśeṣatas āpaḥ nareṇavaiḥ sṛṣṭāḥ āpaḥ u vai narasū navaḥ tāyat asya ayanam pūrvatena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ tad ālokāḥ tatojīvāḥ sattvāḥ paṃca ātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ jarāyu ja aṃḍa ja udbhid jāḥ sveda jāḥ ca caturvidhāḥ ṣṭavidhā devayoniḥ mānuṣāḥ tu ekavidhayā mānuṣyam ca ekavidham tu cāturvarṇyam anekadhā pṛthivī ca aṃtarikṣam ca tri divam bhuvanam smṛtam pṛthivyāḥ tu parīmāṇe bhūyas tulyaḥ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ekam tu koṭyā vikhyātam evam tribhuvanam matam rudrāṇām koṭiḥ ekātu pure ca antar vyavasthitā bahmā viṣṇu śrva dvau etau upāsāte maheśvaram pṛthivī ādi prasaṃkhyānam tapasā a samudāhṛtam tat idam saṃpravakṣyāmi puruṣān loka viśrutān śiva krīḍana saṃsthānam śive na parikalpitam kāma ārādhanakam śaṃbhoḥ pūjanam dvīpa vāsibhiḥ sārdhapaṃcā śīti śata yojana ādi visāriṣu jaṃbūdvīpa ādi dvīpa iṣu mayā vyāptam idam dvija jaṃbūddīpe mahādevaḥ gomedegirijeśvaraḥ śālmali dvīpa madhya sthā devaḥ paśupatiḥ svayam kuśadvīpe haraḥ bhūtvā krauṃce proktaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ śāka īśaṃkara nāmā yam puṣkara ibha alalocanaḥ tatra tatra mahādevam pūjayaṃtaḥ sthirān abahūn bhogān mahā auṣadhīḥ tebhyaḥ prāpnuvaṃti śiva ājñayā jaṃbūddīpaḥ ca gomedaḥ śālmaliḥ ca kuśaḥ tathā krauṃcadvīpaḥ tathā aśākaḥ puṣkaraḥ samamaḥ smṛtaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi ddīpāḥ nām tu pṛthak pṛthak parimāṇam ca saṃkhyām ca dvīpa pravaram eva ca jaṃbūdvīpe jaṃbu vṛkṣaḥ yojanaiḥ stam nibodhata sahasram śa tam ekam ca yojanānām samucchritaḥ tasya jaṃbū phala rasaḥ ca amṛta svāduḥ ucyate pramāṇādāḥ yatas dvīpa udviguṇaḥ pariṇāhataḥ dviguṇena samudreṇa lavaṇena samāvṛtaḥ tasya varṣāṇi sa meha kāmagāḥ ca yathārhataḥ bhāratasya varṣasi anava bhedāḥ prakī titāḥ sapta vargāḥ prasaṃkhyātāḥ samā eva kulaparvatāḥ dakṣiṇena visam khyātam ilāvattam prakīrtitam uttaram dakṣiṇam ca eva iṃdradhanva ākṛtiḥ yathā catvāraḥ droṇa saṃsthānām varṣāṇām ca pramāṇataḥ girivarṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣaḥ bhāratam da kṣiṇena tu pūrveṇa mālyavān ca eva paścime gaṃdhamādanaḥ nīlaḥ parvata rāja śva śvetaḥ śuklaḥ mahā giriḥ śṛṃgāt uttaratas pārśve samaṃtāt samupotthitau sahasrāṇām tasmin jaṃbūdaka iti eva kanakam deva bhūṣaṇam tasya jaṃbūttare pārśvameruḥ nāma mahā giriḥ merum pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā yojanānām sahasrāṇi caturaśītiḥ ucchrayaḥ adhastāt daśa sahasrāṇi viṃśaḥ ca eva pārśvataḥ merum pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā kailāsa ākhyaḥ tatas giriḥ caturaśītiḥ tatas vyāsaḥ giri iṃdrasya mahātmanaḥ tasya sānuṣu citreṣu kaṃdareṣu darīṣu ca tatra āyati jita krodha ajita lobha ajita iṃdriyāḥ ye gṛhasthāḥ svadharma jñāḥ gaḥ brāhmaṇa hite ratāḥ te yānti paramam sthānam prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ śatam śata sahasrāṇi yojanānām samaṃtataḥ niṣadhaḥ ca eva hemakūṭaḥ ca parvataḥ himavān dakṣiṇe pārśve tābat paramam ucchritaḥ paṃcaviṃśat sahasrāṇi vistareṇa sadā ucya te tathā eva vakṣa siṃdhu śvati srastā vaipratīcya gāḥ ca eva pūrvagāḥ jaṃgā yātu samaṃtā āsām jaṃbūddī pa sarit varā gaṃgā samāna rūpa aśrva puṇya tīrya śiloccayāḥ deva tīryāḥ su puṇya aśva pṛthivyām anukīrtitāḥ jaṃbūdvīpaḥ prasaṃkhyātaḥ yāthātathyena vai dvijāḥ paṇṇām itara dvīpānām śeṣam prāmāṇyataḥ śṛṇu jaṃbūdvīpa pramāṇena dviguṇa aṃtarataḥ smṛtaḥ uttareṇa smṛtāḥ sarve aṃtare svarga vāsinaḥ sarvaśas kṣāra ekṣuḥ surā sarpiḥ dadhi odān āma nāmataḥ maṃḍodaḥ ca prasaṃkhyātaḥ tatas svādaka uttaraḥ dvīpānām sahasrāṇi tu vyākhyātāni mayā dvijāḥ api varṣa śataiḥ viprān aśakyam kathitum mayā lakṣadvīpā ikṣa saḥ śālmale śālmaliḥ smṛtaḥ kuśa dvīpe kuśaḥ tam vaḥ krauṃca dvīpe mahā giriḥ jaṃbū vṛkṣa pramāṇena dviguṇa uttaratas smṛtāḥ sarveṣām eva vṛkṣāṇām amṛta svādā ucyate taṃtu pītvā amṭata rasam dīrgha āyuḥ stavam ca gacchati na anyam priyam vijānaṃti ca kravāka sadharmiṇaḥ sūkṣma kāṃcana vālukā sarva kālaphalā vṛkṣāḥ sva sva gaṃdha phala āśrayāḥ sarve pāṃca eva dvīpānām saptānām kulaparvatāḥ nadyaḥ teṣām tu samā eva kalpitāḥ śubhāḥ sahasraśas raṃjitāḥ śṛṃgavaṃtaḥ śva śobhate girayaḥ tathā tatas siddha aśva ṛṣayaḥ gaṃdharvāḥ dānavāḥ khagāḥ bhagavān aśivaḥ teṣām parvata jālāni dīpyanti prabhayā svayā vṛtāḥ parvata rājā samaṃtataḥ ṣaṣṭiṃgiri sahasrāṇi ete tasya samaṃtadā tatra te puruṣāḥ divyāḥ śukla daṃtāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ teṣām na duḥkham na glāniḥ na kaścid paribādhate teṣu dvīpeṣu jāyaṃte puruṣāḥ te tapodhanāḥ dīrgha āyuṣvaṃtam teṣām vidyate kāmagā gatiḥ jaṃbūdvīpasya paryāyam kathayiṣyāmi vai dvijāḥ mānuṣāṇām ca varṣāṇi yugānām ca eva saṃkhyayā kīrtayiṣyāmi iva a viprāḥ purāṇam yat vibhāvyate aṣṭa varṣa sahasra aṃtaka alaṃkṛta yugam viduḥ lakṣāḥ dvādaśa vaipra uktāḥ ṣaṣ sahasrāṇi vatsarāḥ tretā yugasya prāmāṇyam purāṇe parikīrtitam aṣṭa varṣa sahasra aṃtā lakṣa aśva aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ lakṣa aśva aṣṭau cala kṣaudyau ayuta idva tayā eva ca aṣṭa varṣa sahasrati kālaḥ evamādi ca varṣa ca tathā varṣa śatam dvijāḥ evam āyuḥ jita iṃdrasya harasya animiṣaḥ smṛtaḥ brahma ādi staṃba paryaṃtam nimiṣa utpattiḥ īśvaraḥ nimeṣa jīvinaḥ sarve caṃdra ādityau gṛhaiḥ saha mahākalpam ca vikhyātam śivasya nimiṣaḥ tathā dvīpānām ca eva varṣāṇām kathayāmi samāsatas anyeṣām ca eva dvīpānām dhā vihita āgatiḥ bhāratasya varṣasi anava bhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ iṃdradvīpaḥ kaśeruśva tāmraparṇaḥ gabhastimān nāgaddīpaḥ tathā asaumyaḥ gāṃdharva śrvāraṇaḥ tathā ayam tu navabhaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃgataḥ svādūdakaḥ nāma nāmnā sāgara uttaratas mahān tasya ca adya aparā pṛthvī dviguṇena pramāṇataḥ tasmāt paraṃca vailokaḥ lokālokaḥ ca nāmataḥ lokān viśati tat lokṛ pramāṇam loka vistarāt manasā asiddhi saṃpanna anīroga aśvira jīvinaḥ prākāra sthitayaḥ ca eva sauvarṇa aśva saha arṇavāḥ lokeśāḥ ca eva catvāraḥ lokālokesthitāḥ tathā evam sa bhuvi vistāraḥ triguṇaḥ parimāṇataḥ iti śrī śiva mahā purāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām saptadvīpavarṇanaṃnāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ vistāraḥ dīrgha tā tathā adhastāt yat pravakṣyāmi tāla tala vāsinām tatra bhogavatī ramyā nānā ratna upaśobhitā sarve ca nāga rājānām viśramaṃte mudā anvitāḥ tatra siddhā muni gaṇāḥ bharata ādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ kāliyaḥ pavanaḥ nāma nāgaḥ pūraṇaḥ eva ca maṇimālaḥ ca eva bhadraḥ nāgaḥ ca eva atha kauśikaḥ bala aśvatarau ubhau karavīra puṃḍarī kausaṃvataḥ atha mahoragaḥ anaṃtāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ purī bhogavatī ramyā nānā ratna upaśobhitā vicitrābhiḥ patākābhiḥ vimānaiḥ vasahasraśas dolā laṃbita vāsā aśva muktā dāmaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ hāsya nāṭya vicitrābhiḥ gāna vāditra niḥkhanaiḥ sarva kāma prasiddha arthāḥ striyaḥ śva apsarasā upamāḥ na eva teṣām bhavet glāniḥ na śokaḥ na jarā tathā īrṣyāyāḥ ca bhayam na asti sarva kāma hite ratāḥ puṣṭidānasyara hitāḥ sarva kāmeṣu pūjitāḥ tatra bhogavatī ramyāprabhālokā dvi śiṣyate tatra staṃbha saha khāṇi vajra vaiḍūrya kalpāni mahāratnāni śobhitā iṃdranīla mahānīlaiḥ sarvataśva abhimaṃḍitā sarva kālaphala anayaḥ sarva pāyasa kardamāḥ kulyā aśva ghṛta saṃpūrṇāḥ sadā vṛkṣa upaśobhitāḥ anna parvata kūṭāḥ ca śaṃkha kuṃda iṃdu pāṃḍurāḥ kalpitāḥ a brahmaṇā pūrṇāḥ śaṃkarasya ājñayā purā payasā anitya pūrṇāni bhājanāni samaṃtataḥ madhukulyāḥ ca saṃnyastāḥ ārakta daṃtāḥ ati śobhitāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ tathā ca anyā bhāryā yauvana saṃpadaḥ bhukta abhuktāḥ priyaiḥ tatra yoniḥ tāsām na cakṣatā prasūtāyāḥ tu kanyāyāḥ yau vanam na apihīyate ti sva dāra niratāḥ sadā iṣṭa bhuj sva jana ākīrṇa a nāga loke prakīrtitāḥ ūrdhva tirya ggatiḥ khyātā a tāsām taṣām anekaśas nāga lokasya vistāram dviguṇam parikīrtitam eka deśa pramāṇena mayā ākhyātam yathā ta thā yojanaiḥ koṭire kātunāga lokaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ūrdhva tiryak prasaṃkhyātam catur asram tathā dvijāḥ anantaram pravakṣyāmi hiraṇyapura vāsinām tatra api koṭiḥ saṃkhyātā ayojanaiḥ parimāṇataḥ tatra āsan sa phala avaṃkṣāḥ puṣpaiḥ ca eva sugaṃdhinaḥ nānā vicitra nirghoṣa niḥsvanaiḥ pūrṇa kaṃdaraiḥ yauvana sthāḥ striyaḥ tatra sukumāḥ rāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ puruṣa a rūpa saṃpannāḥ sva dāra nirata iṃdriyāḥ sauvarṇa aśva gṛhāḥ tatra vimāna cāriṇaḥ sarve sarve ca sthita yauvanāḥ akṣata pratimāḥ tatra striyaṃśu āpsarasā upamāḥ śukla daṃta ambara dharāḥ caṃdra aṃśu vimala prabhāḥ manoramāḥ su siddhārthāḥ cakravāka sadharmiṇaḥ na udvegaḥ ūna ca kopaḥ tu īrṣyā asūyā vivarjitāḥ varṣaiḥ anekaiḥ saṃkhyātā guṇāḥ tasmin pura uttame saṃtye te prahāda ādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām prasādāt jīvaṃti sarva lokān na saṃśayaḥ brahma ādyāḥ devatāḥ sarvā ādhāryate samanantaram para aparāṇām lokānām dhāraṇaiḥ loka dhāraṇaiḥ sarvān imān dhārayati surabhiḥ nāma nāmataḥ pṛthvīm dhārayati sarvān sudhanvā nāma nāmataḥ sarvāgaśvasusarvāgaḥ sulabhāca uttarām diśam dakṣiṇām caṣakānām adhārayanti diśam sadā teṣām prasādāt jī vaṃti brahma ādyāḥ tridivaukasaḥ tasmin adivyāni veśmāni citrāṇi ca laghūni ca patākā dhvaja citrāṇi prāsādānām ca paṃktayaḥ sarva kāmaphalā vṛkṣa aramya aśvitra aśca pādapāḥ svargāt atitarām ramyā sukhasparśā jalāśayāḥ kāmyā a purā utyeṣā a sadā a saṃpūrṇa mānasā brahmaṇā a vihita apūrva kāma rūpa guṇa anvitā ni sahasraśas sarvaiḥ ca eva sukha sparśāḥ śvāraṇasya api veśmani prāsādapam śubhāḥ prakīrtitāḥ pāyasena ca pūrṇāni bhājanāni saha sraśas aṃbu divya amṛta upamam bhaktāḥ nānāvidhāḥ tatra bhūṣaṇāḥ pūrṇa kalpitāḥ na śakyāḥ nāma mātreṇa ākhyātum su samāhitaiḥ uddeśa mātram kathitāḥ pātāle asmin guṇa āmayā teṣām vakṣyāmi vaivipra anāgapātāla vāsinām citra avicitrāḥ kurvāṇāḥ sūkṣmāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca dṛ śyaṃte tāni nityam hi avyakta avyakta saṃjñitāḥ purī gulyāḥ anaṃtasya pātāle parikīrtitā guṇāḥ saṃkhyāna rahitāḥ tasmin puravare tadā tu tattvataḥ anaṃtasya api anaṃtasya sarva kāma su pūjitā atas param tu vipra iṃdra śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ kathām nadī vaitariṇīyataḥ asipattravanam ca eva yamaśūlī bhaya āvahā bhairavāni ca rūpāṇi eka pāṣāṇam eva ca jalam śālmalī karṣaṇam śālmalinaḥ kaṃṭaki vṛkṣa viśeṣāt karṣaṇam atha pāpa viśeṣeṇa naraka viśeṣa saṃbaṃdham āha raurava iti kūṭa sākṣiṇām anṛta sākṣyam kurve ca tathā śūlam tathā vaitaraṇī nadī karaṃbha vālukā ca eva śṛṃgāṭaka vanam tathā thā na huśas proktā ayam asya viṣaye smṛtāḥ sarva ādhāraiḥ anekaiḥ akliśyaṃte ca punar punar āśībhiḥ takṣaṇaiḥ ca eva krakacaiḥ ca eva pāṭanam vaitaraṇyāḥ tathā ākṣāram śālmalī karṣaṇam tathā ādānam yaṃtra sūtrasya kuṃbhīpāka ica mardanam raurave kūṭa sākṣiṇām pātanam na atra saṃśayaḥ para hiṃsā niviṣṭānām bodha ke patanam bhavet brahma sva haraṇāt ca eva kuṃbhīpāka icapātanam varṣāṇām ca sahasrāṇi pīḍyate ca nara adhamaḥ varṣāṇām śata sāhasram pīḍyamānaḥ punar punar kṣiptaḥ pa cyate dhruvam dhana dhānya suvarṇāni hiraṇyam vā aviśeṣatas hṛtvā narakam āpnoti yama śūlam bhaya āvaham śatam varṣāṇi pīḍanam pitṛ haṃtā ati adhomukhe pīḍyaṃta ca su duḥkhitaḥ sarveṣu vaitariṇyām ca deva dravya vināśakaḥ cyate naraka ighāre varṣāṇām ekaviṃśatim mala apahasya mūla anihiṃsya mānaḥ himāḥ navaḥ bhairavāṇi ca rūpāṇi ghoram parama dāruṇam adhomukhena patati varṣāṇām ca sahasraśas mitra bhāryā abhilāṣiṇaḥ tathā ca asya abhayaṃda tvā abhayam utpādyate punar etāvatā apāpi puruṣaiḥ anubhūyamānān narakān abhidhāya idānīm idam aloka vartī niramya aṇi puṇya śāli jana gamyā nisthānāni āha eva para eteṣām upariṣṭāt tu bhānoḥ lokaḥ vibhāvyate tasmāt bhānoḥ mahā utsāha lokāḥ sura namaskṛtāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ ca eva sahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇām bhāvitātmanām upāsateḥ atha varaṃbhānoḥ akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ tatra teṣām mahātmānaḥ nāga gaṃdharva rākṣasāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ ca eva sahasrāṇi apsarāṇām prasaṃkhyayā gīta gaṃdharva ghoṣa śva hāhā hūhūḥ anekaśas na avidhā aiti śloka artha yojanā yena vai parjanyāḥ te āgneyāḥ iti jānaṃti vidvāṃsaḥ iti yojanā mahā utsāha lokāḥ vāyu rathāḥ vāyu rathaḥ gamana sādhanam yeṣām meghāḥ vāyavyāḥ gaṇa viśeṣāḥ sapta skaṃdheṣu sapta su gaṇeṣu vibhaktāḥ iti śeṣaḥ śata śotha vimānāni śata ghaṃṭā ayutāni ca nānā ratna vicitra āṇi patākaiḥ śobhitāni ca kiṃkiṇī jāla citrāṇi nānā ratna ujjvalāni ca sarva kāma samṛddhāni kāvya śabda anvitāni ca ete vāyu ratha aramya aṃtarikṣa carāḥ smṛtāḥ vāyavyāḥ śataśas te śrasa taskaṃdheṣu vā etathā evam gaṇāryāṃ āṃti tān svān bhāgān ākāśam eva ca svarga paṃthānam āśritya caranti vimala udakāḥ devaiḥ saha apsarobhiḥ siddhaiḥ śva apsarasā anvitaiḥ tatra divyāni veśmāni vicitrāṇi bahūni ca puṇya kṛdbhiḥ upetāni śas tatra devāḥ vimāna sthāra maṃte kelikārakāḥ su kṛtaḥ sarva saṃga jitaḥ narāḥ ādityasya mahātmanaḥ ā dityasya upariṣṭāt tu loka avaivasvatāḥ smṛtāḥ tatra divyāḥ śuci maya vimāna śata śobhitāḥ kṣatriyāḥ ca eva yajvānaḥ maṃtriṇaḥ soma pāyinaḥ tasmāt ūrdhvam bhāsva raḥ samavasthitaḥ viprāḥ bhavanti yajvānaḥ vimāna śata śobhitāḥ su mahātmanām divyām bara dharāḥ sarve upariṣṭāt vibhūṣitāḥ ākāśagaṃgā tatrasthā sarve ca eva grahāḥ tathā tasmāt ūrdhvam ṭaṣīṇām vailokaḥ parama pūji taḥ tatra śūra araṇe prāṇān parityajya mahā āhave eva ca na śakyam prāpyate gaṃtum varjayitvā śiva anugān anugrahāt vā ayaḥ gāt vā anaiṣṭhikāt vā atathā dvijāḥ etasmin antare devāḥ sarva aiṃdra purogamāḥ pādayoḥ patitāḥ sarve brahmāṇam ṛṣayaḥ tathā brahmaṇā ca api anujñātāḥ sarve sukha mayāḥ sthitāḥ svāgatam vaḥ mahā bhāgāḥ śṛṇudhvam kim iha icchatha yena kāryeṇa vā āyātāḥ tat urvaṃtu sura uttamāḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ sraṣṭā tvam paripṛ cchasi varāṇām vai sahasrāt tu darśanam deva śasyate mahān naḥ saṃśayaḥ atyaṃtam bhagavān vaktum arhati durlabham paramam gutyam praṣṭavyam praśnam uttamam yat aham pṛṣṭavān pūrvam rudrasya paramātmanaḥ tat idam saṃpravakṣyāmi itihāsam purātanam naimiṣeyāḥ tu ṛṣayaḥ jita krodha ajita iṃdriyāḥ icchā dveṣa vinirmuktāḥ dhyāna yoga parāyaṇāḥ īśvara jñāna saṃpa nna āgatāḥ brahma sabhām parām bhṛgu aṃgirasa vṛddhau ca purastāt kṛtavān śuciḥ parama bhāvinī paramam parama ātmānam bhāvayati iti sā yatas pāpa samācārāḥ sadācā om namaḥ śivāya tatra kāma mayā nāma sabhā parama bhāvinī puruṣāḥ tatra paśyaṃti parama ātma aikya tāṃgatāḥ varjayitvā aśivam devam kaḥ śaktaḥ tamasaḥ paraḥ sarve pāpa samācārāḥ sat ācāra vivarjitāḥ tamasā apihitam kṛtvāni rṇayam pāpa puṇyayoḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām bhuvana kośa varṇanam nāma paṃcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtau uvāca nayāt āgataḥ vyāsaḥ sadbhāvam bhaktim āśritaḥ sanatkumāram sarvajñam saṃdeham atha pṛṣṭavān eṣa mā asaṃśayaḥ brahman brūhi me tvam mahā mune bhagavan bhūta bhavya īśa śaktyā āśrāvayitum kṣamaḥ ākhyā ahirudra māhātmyam śṛṇumaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ idam sarva purābhūtam sarvam āsīt mahā arṇavam na agniḥ na vāyuḥ ādityaḥ na bhūmiḥ na diśaḥ daśa kṣatram muhūrta karaṇe tathā na deva asura gaṃdharvān a piśācān arākṣasāḥ dṛṣṭvā aham moham āpannaḥ niśveṣṭaḥ ciram āsthitaḥ koṭi sahasrāṇām lokānām hita kāmyayā mukha padmam su śobhanam samam āyāṃti saṃmūḍhāḥ kimartha pariśuṣyatha śrūyatām vaḥ mahābhāgāḥ upadeśaḥ ya thākramam yathā avasthā nibhūta anisthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca prājāpatyam bhavet annam anne prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ annāt bhavanti bhū tāni annam vaiyajña saṃbhavam ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni kalpa upaniṣadaḥ tathā maṃtrāṇi āraṇyakam ca eva rahasya ātharvaṇam tathā ekākṣaram param brahma oṃkāraḥ parā ucyate ṣaḍaṃgaiḥ saha saṃproktaḥ sāṃkhya yoga viśāradaiḥ sāvitrī saṃbhava ūti eṣa brahma akṣara mayaḥ mahān mayā aśaktyā ava hmaṇā ca viṣṇunā api saḥ ījyate yajña lokaḥ tadā sāmnām pratipattiḥ svayaṃbhuvā upadeśam tatas kṛtvā mahādevaḥ maheśvaraḥ uktvā vacanam īśānaḥ tatra eva aṃtaradhīyata ekā bhagavataḥ mūrtiḥ ūrdhva roma abhaya āvahā dvitīyā tasya vaimūrtiḥ sūrya jyotiḥ sama prabhā tṛtīyā bhagavataḥ mūrtiḥ śaśinaḥ paramātmanaḥ sūkṣma dhyāna viciṃtakāḥ loke pṛthak pṛthak krīḍate prathamā mṛrtiḥ dvitīyā tapyate tapaḥ tṛtīyā harate lokān caturthīḥ sṛjate prajāḥ paṃcamī jñāna sadbhāvam sarva mā āhatya tiṣṭhati saḥ eṣa sarva bhūtānām gomān īśānaḥ ucyate utpattim pralayam ca eva bhūtāḥ nām saṃgatim gatim mahān ca mahataḥ yasmāt mahadbhiḥ śva mahīyate yasmai didam mahat nityam mahādeva eti smṛtaḥ yasmāt nāśayate pūrṇa trailokyam sacarācaram paśūnām pāśanam ca eva tasmāt paśupatiḥ smṛ taḥ svayam mātā asvayam bhūtvā apriyaḥ lokaiḥ anuttamaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ lokeṣu ca svayaṃbhūtvā svayaṃbhūḥ iti hi smṛtaḥ yasmāt ekam śiraḥ chitvā tat kapālam adhārayat kapālī iti tatas yaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ tathā yasmāt kṣaya aṃte trailokyam śaṃkareya ati saṃkṣayam tasmāt saṃvarta kodhāta aśaṃkara iti abhidhīyate yasmāt imāni bhūtāni paśyan tena adhikam tatas sarvam viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ tasmāt īśānataḥ bhavat bṛhat tvā ahaṇa mā avatam brahma yāvat prāṇam ayaḥ dhuvaḥ akṣarā dvāparaḥ rudra akṣara āśu avayam purā asmākam devatā rudraḥ vai yam deveṣu devatāḥ deva a deva a dvijātīnām dvijāḥ śeṣasya devatāḥ āpad bhāvaḥ samāpannaḥ mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām trahmagītopākhyānam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ etat kāraṇa saṃjātam niścalam kevalam dhruvam viṣṇuḥ pārśvāt tu saṃbhūtaḥ liṃge bhūtāḥ surāḥ tathā liṃgāyasa vadharmeṇa jagat sthāḥ vara jaṃgamam liṃga mūrtiḥ ca bhagavān anādinidhanaḥ śivaḥ alpa akṣaram idaṃgutyam mama ekānteniśamyatām aham viṣṇuḥ purā śakraḥ anye vā asura puṃgavāḥ virūpākṣasya netrābhyām nimiṣa unmeṣaṇe sthitāḥ tat ca vakṣyāmi vipra iṃdra īśvaram saṃpracakṣate rudreṇa sadṛśam devam na anyam paśyāmahe vayam sarvathā āvarttamāna āśvaye bhaktāḥ parameśvare tevaśyavāsinām tulya munīnām bhāvitātmanām bhava pāpam na viṃdanti teḥ yāti paramām gatim na deva asura gaṃdharvān ayakṣān acarākṣasāḥ viṣṇu tvam vāsava tvam ca amara tvam suraiḥ saha rudra bhaktāḥ tu vipra iṃdrāḥ prāpnuvaṃti śiva ālayam aśubhāḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ yena rāj kalmaṣīkṛtāḥ īśvaraṃpratipaśyam dvija a bhāvita bhāvanāḥ ādidevam mahādevam prabhum prabhavatām api ye smaraṃti sadā rudra bhayam teṣām na vidyate suraiḥ sahavāsam iti śeṣaḥ śivālayam śivakalyāṇam ca tad ālaya sthānam mokṣam iti arthaḥ prabhavatām alaukika śaktimatām devānām pāpa yonayaḥ śvapaca ādayaḥ nīlakaṃṭhasya nīlaḥ kaṃṭhaḥ viṣa bhakṣaṇena yaṃsyasaḥ sarva lakṣaṇa hīnaḥ sarvaiḥ nija varṇa āśrama ucita dharma ihi naḥ tam devadevam maheśvaram rudra rudra iti tri saṃdhyam yaḥ būyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ kīrtanāt nīlakaṃṭhasya sa rva pāpaiḥ pramucyate sarva lakṣaṇa hīnaḥ api yuktaḥ vā a sarva pātakaiḥ śivam āsthitaḥ saṃsāreḥ bhramamāṇānām pāpa yoniṣu yat bhavet mahādeva prapannānām bhayam teṣām na vidyate manasā api śirva devam ye prapayaṃti mānavāḥ vidhūtāḥ sarva pāpebhyaḥ devaiḥ saha ramanti te agnihotram cayet nityam yajñān ca eva su dakṣiṇān rudra bhaktasya vipra iṃdrāḥ kalām nāḥ īti ṣoḍaśīm sarveṣām dhyāna yogānām ye ca anye mokṣa kāṃkṣiṇaḥ mahādeva prasādena prāpnuvaṃti parām gatim a prāpya cavi rūpa akṣaṃkaḥ pumān siddhim arhati tīrthānām ca mahā tīrtham maṃgalā nāṃca maṃgalam yat pavicam pavitrāṇām saṃprapadyetam īśvaram sarva bhūta patiḥ bhavaḥ thṛdisthaḥ sarva bhūtāḥ nāma oṃkāram adhigacchati karam katham tad phalam vidmahe yathā ghṛtam ca payasi yayā agniḥ ca eva dāruṇi yathā vayam tathā ca anye tathā asana tkumāra ādayaḥ ādhyātmikaiḥ sura varaiḥ brahmaṇaḥ sva ātma saṃbhavaiḥ tad kāraṇakāḥ aiti bhāvaḥ om namaḥ prakṛtya jāpyam stuti homa liṃgam nataḥ bravīmi atra mahā maheśvaram punar tu tatra api dadarśa liṃgam anāmaya liṃgam alakṣaṇam ca na deva gaṃdharva na bhūta saṃgha ana siddha yakṣa adhipa pannaga adhipāḥ vibhum prapaśyaṃti maheśvaram param mahā viṣam yojarayat kṣaṇena mānuṣa nāgānām na bhayam vidyate kvacid kāmageṣu vimāneṣu vicaranti hi mānavāḥ arcayanti virūpākṣa liṃga mūrti maheśvaram iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sa natkumārasaṃhitāyām saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭi varṣa śatāni ca thṛṣīkeśena vipra iṃdraiḥ varṣa koṭim prasāditaḥ ārādhitaḥ mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ maheśvaraḥ tuṣṭena ca tathā viṣṇuḥ varaiḥ śveṣṭhaiḥ tu yojitaḥ śit nāma mahācakradhara uvalī īśvarasya prasādena viṣṇuḥ parama taijasaḥ rakṣate pṛthivīm sarvām ajeya śva balī tataḥ prasāditaḥ virūpākṣaḥ puṣkarākṣaḥ maheśvaraḥ iṣṭābhiḥ stuti pūjābhiḥ vividhaiḥ karmabhiḥ stathā ārādhitaḥ mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ hiraṇmayaḥ tuṣṭena cakṛtaḥ brahmā saṃhartā viśvatomukhaḥ dātā āhartā ca goptā ca saṃhartā ca yuge yuge pitāmaha tvam ca sura asurāṇām brahma ādhipatyam param avyayam ca anāgatam vartamānam śvam sarveṣu lokeṣu cara acara tvam sarve ca vedāḥ saha ṣatiḥ aṃgaiḥ sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca sa pāribhāṣam śakreṇa ācīrṇe divyam pāśupatam mahat vāyubhakṣaḥ abukṣavat urvāsā śvarma saṃvṛtaḥ evam āsīt virūpākṣaḥ rudraḥ śṛṃgādṛha asataḥ tuṣṭaḥ vai kṛttivāsāḥ pinākadhṛk gaṇeśaḥ vaikṛtaḥ śakraḥ ma hā vajradharaḥ balī bhūyas cakratuḥ rājena dattam ca eva triviṣṭapam sanatkumāraḥputra ume vyākhyātaḥ mānasa uddijāḥ sahasram ca vimānānām sapta saṃkhyāsu yat purā caṃdra sūrya prakāśeṣu vibhāneṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ strī sahasra samākīrṇaḥ dīpyamānaḥ su tejasā gāyadbhiḥ nṛtyamānaiḥ a vādayadbhiḥ a sarvaśas puruṣaiḥ sūrya saṃkāśaiḥ dīpyamānaiḥ sva tejasā upaviṣṭaḥ sthitaḥ tatragi riṃ pādena pīḍayan yajamāna āśvaye dṛṣṭa āloka yātrā kara āśvaye pārthivāḥ te itam āsādya sarva dhiṣṇyeṣu adhiṣṭhitāḥ udyoginām ca tarji tvam bhīruṇām ca nivāraṇam puṣpa kāle ca puṣyaṃti phala kāle phala pradāḥ pāka kāle saṃvṛtāḥ śaila iṣu nirata ayeca pātāleca samāśritāḥ aṃtarikṣe carāye ca carantiṃdivisaṃśritāḥ ye ca nakṣatra mārgeṣu nakṣatrāṇi samāśritāḥ caṃdra sūrya ogra saṃtiye sva sthāne prasthita aśvāḥ anye sāṃkhya yogam anuvratāḥ asaṃkhyāta atyaneka aśva jaṃgama ajaṃgamāḥ sthitāḥ te samāśritāḥ divyāḥ pārśva gatāḥ sarve gṛhāḥ tu pādapāḥ tathā kunda iṃdu kumuda prakhyām māla padma sugaṃdhinīm jighaṃti cai vadha avaṃti rudra pārśva gatā gaṇāḥ teṣām varṇa viśeṣaḥ asti pramāṇam ca eva dṛśyate ekaikasya gaṇa īśasya śarīram pratitiṣṭhati meru maṃdara śailānām gaṇānām parimāṇataḥ teṣām parivṛtaḥ udevaḥ grahāṇām iva bhāskaraḥ sanatkumāraḥ deveśaḥ gaṇeśāya mahātmane evam dṛṣṭam mayā ākhyātam bhīmasya amita tejasaḥ śṛṇuyāt gaṇa saṃkhyānam manasā api sadā smaret prayatna mānasaḥ bhūtvā paṭhet parvaṇi parvaṇi sarvān kāmān avāpnoti amṛta tvaṃca viṃdati śatam śata sahasrāṇi rudra loke mahīyate tathā eva samudāharet āhāra kāle tu paṭhet rāhmaṇānām ca saṃnidhau nityam evam paṭhati yaḥ śraddhāna ujita iṃdriyaḥ śata rudra phalam tasya labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ paṭhataḥ tu tatas puṇyam gaṇa saṃkhyām ca nityaśas śṛṇuyāt vā piyaḥ bhaktyā sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate prabhāta samaye kāle samutthāya mahā manāḥ brahmāṇam deva kartāram sarva śāstra viśāradam siddhāḥ te garvitāḥ purā sya śiva syavā ukta gaṇa varṇa nasya pāṭha śravaṇa ādiṣu phala viśeṣam āhaṃ śṛṇuyāt ityādi śata śata sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām iti śeṣaḥ a mogha retāḥ sa phala śukraḥ anaṃta pāpa yuktaḥ vā ūrdhva ca nayanam dṛṣṭvā deva tejaḥ mayam sthitam pitāca pitaraḥ me dya dṛṣṭvā apātram upāgatāḥ evam dṛṣṭvā āsa mām putraḥ vyājahāra sa saṃbhramaḥ nigṛhītaḥ asmi bhadram te bālena akṛtakarmaṇā vi mānāni ca ratnāni ajasram ca su saṃskṛtam tena aham duḥkha saṃtāpāt deham tyakṣye na saṃśayaḥ ātmānam gamayāmāsa dhyāna yogena dṛṣṭavān sa pāraiti tam jñātvā atatodṛṣṭa naraḥ bhavat utthāya ca āsa na a brahmā a prāṃjaliḥ praṇataḥ sthitaḥ namaskṛtvā mahādevam īśvaram sarvatomukham idam āha mahā tejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ yogānām adhikaḥ yogī devānām aṃbikāpatiḥ dṛṣṭvā purā nandi mukha deva devena bhāṣitam anugraham mahādevaḥ kartu kāmaḥ maheśvaraḥ su durlabhaḥ tu ete viṣṇunā ca prakīrtitāḥ na kiṃcid rahmacārīca paśyati akṛtabuddhyaḥ aikāntena ca saukhyā iva anāsti tatra vicāraṇā vṛṇīṣva ātmam mahādevam gāṇapatyam su durlabham gāṇapatyam ca bhadram te viṣṇunā āsāditam purā brahmaṇaḥ vacanam śrutvā aprayata amāna saṃjapan prasanna śva mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ maheśvaraḥ tuṣṭaḥ prasannaḥ deveśaḥ karmabhiḥ śva amita ojasaḥ sthitaḥ pradakṣiṇaḥ rutvā devadevasya dhīmataḥ dhāraṇam sarva bhūtānām dharādhara patiḥ yamaḥ daśeśvaraḥ śata sūrya agni netra śva cāru netra vibhūṣitaḥ catur mukhaḥ catur daṃṣṭraḥ catuḥ bahuḥ catur yugaḥ mahā īśvaraḥ śrīkaṃṭhaḥ kalināśanaḥ viṣṇu prasāda daḥ ca eva samudrevaḍavāmukhaḥ deva sura vinirjetā adeva asura parāyaṇaḥ kapardī śūla hastaḥ ca ajātaḥ parama āgatiḥ tāpasānām param tattvam tathā ca paramam padam parāvara jñaḥ lokānām sarvadā harivāhanaḥ asitāṃgaḥ sitāṃgaḥ ca asitāyatalocanaḥ brahmaṇā adhīyate brahma asaṃsthitaḥ nābhi paṃkaje nīla ugra jaṭilaḥ śrīmān śaṃkha cakra gadā dharaḥ ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni kalpa upaniṣadaḥ tathā maṃtrāṇām bhavanam ca eva parasya ātharvaṇasya ca sahasra vāh paśupatiḥ sahasra śata yojanaḥ bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca bhagavān eva sarvaśas tvad gātrebhyaḥ yaḥ lokāḥ sa nātanāḥ evam saṃstūyamānaḥ sa vyaktī bhūtaḥ maheśvaraḥ upagamyam udāyuktaḥ tadā adṛṣṭaḥ sa dṛṣṭimān kamaṃḍalu dhara udaṃḍī śaśāṃka kṛta śekharaḥ siṃha camaṃcara chadaḥ nāga yajñopavītī ca akṣamālā vibhūṣitaḥ śūladhṛk puras śara dharaḥ devaḥ śakti cāpa sa mudgaraiḥ śaṃkha cakra gadā pāṇiḥ padma śūka hala āyudhaḥ śaśiḥ uṣṇa ajina dharaḥ pālī ghora cāpa dhṛk vṛṣa ārūḍha ūr̤hīpyamānaḥ gaṇaiḥ parivataḥ haraḥ nandinā aśūla hastena purastāt darśitaḥ prabhuḥ dadṛśe bhagavān devaḥ sūrya agni śaśinā dṛśā tathā ca sarva prāṇi rūpā eti bhāvaḥ brahmaṇā akathitam pūrvam yathāgatyam yathodbhavam manasaḥ kāma lobhau melobhāt meha ṛṣaṇam ca yat iṃdriyāṇām ca sarveṣām indriyāṇi manāṃsi ca māneṣu udāna udāna me kālena sarva bhūtānām niṣpattiḥ samudāhṛtā na aśnaṃti tarpitāḥ devāḥ sadā viśada mānasaḥ tvam eva uraga gaṃdharva piśāca yakṣa rākṣasāḥ tvat ṛte na anya bhaktaḥ asmi manasā karmaṇā a girā tasya evam vacanam śrutvā umāpatiḥ maheśvaraḥ mama nāmāni sarvāṇi gocarāṇi bhavaṃtu te su saṃgrahāṇi sarvāṇi na asti kācid vicāraṇā pārāśarya aiti khyātaḥ utpatsyati mahā tapāḥ vedavyā saḥ sa dharma ātmā ajñānavān dīrghadarśanaḥ vyāsaḥ kamala patra akṣaḥ sate śiṣyaḥ bhaviṣyati nirmalam vimalam śuddham jñānam candra sama prabham rathaṃkāma gamam divyam sāra ratna vibhūṣitam muktā jāla paricchanna hema jāla samāvṛtam patākaiḥ ramaṇam tatra sevyamānam sura asuraiḥ vimānam sūrya saṃkāśam sarva lokaḥ jva lam śubham sura asuraiḥ akṣaram tatra aiśvaryam bhaviṣyati mama ājñayā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitā āryāḥ aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sasaṃcacāra lokān trīn brahma putraḥ abikāsutaḥ eṣa ḍhātāca kartāca saṃha rtāca yugeyuge etasya trividham sarvam īśānasya mahātmanaḥ eṣa yajñapatiḥ devaḥ kṛtāṃtaḥ saumāpatiḥ eṣa hotā ācahomi aśvaḥ evam yajña vidaḥ viduḥ iṃdriyāṇi iṃdriya artheṣu sarvaḥ eva maheśvaraḥ evam jñāna param brahma praśāṃtam nirmalam śivam avyaktam ca avyaktam ca jñānam ca ajñānam eva ca sāṃkhya yogam param sāṃkhyayaḥ paśyati sa paśyati tatas jñānena śuddhāḥ tu prāṇāyāma jita iṃdriyāḥ dhyāyaṃti parama oṃkāram yoginām paramam padam tapasām ca prasādena labhaṃte yoga ci takāḥ śrutiḥ iyam saḥ evam śrutvā tatas sarve ṛṣayaḥ dharma vatsalāḥ abhyanujñāpyatām deva gacchāmaḥ vigata eṣaṇāḥ japyaiḥ dhūpaiḥ alaṃkāraiḥ stūyate vividhaiḥ śivaḥ oṃkāra ādi namaskāraiḥ sahitaiḥ gīta vādanaiḥ athasavya apasavya aiśva vāmadevam tu suvratāḥ na jñānena na tapa sā ciṃtanāt bhāvitātmanām sāṃkhyāt eva param mokṣam yat ca anyaiḥ vividhaiḥ tathā ṛṣibhiḥ viprayuktān vaiṛṣīṇām pradadauva rān teṣām api yathākāmam manasā īpsitam dadet sarva varṇa anukaṃpī ca sarva tīrtha mayaḥ vyayaḥ yeṣām tu kalaṣa abuddhiḥ narāṇām bhāvitātmanām janāḥ niṣkala avirajāḥ khyātāḥ bhaviṣyanti śiva āśritāḥ yatīnām brahma gītā ca brahmaṇā samudāhṛtā yaḥ ca enām tyaṃ yaḥ ca enām śṭaṇuyāt sadā devāgāre paṭhet nityam sadā brāhmaṇa sannidhau dhyāya phala śrutiḥ āsīt asti viṣkaṃbheṇa argala rūpeṇa āyāma taitiyāvat iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām bahmagītā nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tat aham jñātum icchāḥ mi vistareṇa mahā mune āsīt giri varaḥ vyāsa yojanānām samaṃtataḥ aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi nadī pra sravaṇaiḥ yutaḥ viṣkaṃbheṇa sthitaḥ brahman tāvān eva ucchritaḥ smṛtaḥ ri śreṣṭha śvāmīkara sama prabhaḥ tasya kuṃbhepu kuṃbheṣu kaṃdareṣu darīṣu ca nānā kusuma citra ipu śikhinām madhurā giraḥ bheruṃḍaiḥ svarṇa yūthaiḥ śva cakāraiḥ anviteṣu ca kīrṇeṣu vyāghrāṇām ca eva kakṣāṇām khagānām bhavaneṣu ca harmya staṃbheṣu kīrṇe pusiṃhānām rūpa śālinām śobhita giri varye ca devānām ca surā gaṇāḥ kubera pramukhāḥ yakṣāḥ krīḍaṃti ca samaṃtataḥ vicaranti mudā yuktā vidyādhara gaṇa anvitāḥ hāhā hūhū śva gaṃdharvāḥ staṃburu pramukhāḥ tathā mudā anvitāḥ yaṃtra dhārā nighāteṣu ninadaṃti śikhaṃḍinaḥ tāḥ tucam drāṃśubhāḥ kāmaṃjyotsnāyāḥ sarit uttamāḥ yatrasā patate gaṃgā devatānām kulāni vai tatas tam prāpya sarva bhūtāni sauvarṇāni mahānti vai na ca api sama ṛṣayoḥ vāti vai mārutāḥ śubhāḥ paśyaṃtidevatāḥ grāmaha ṛṣayaḥ bhuvanam kāṃcana śrīman vijayam vijayā nadī yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśa ca aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ tāpanīyena mahatā prākāreṇa samāvṛtāḥ gṛhāḥ taṃtra su ramya aśva patākā śobhi māli kāḥ divākara kara ābhāḥ ca su prabhāḥ amita ojasaḥ tatra dvāra sahasrāṇi tāvam taśva dvijottamāḥ sarva aṇi puṇya karmāṇi taru ṇa arka sama prabhāḥ vinyastaiḥ pūrṇa kuṃbhaiḥ ca śobhitāni yathā tathā muktā dāmaiḥ su vipulaiḥ bhūṣitāni samaṃtataḥ puṣpa upahāraiḥ vividhaiḥ dhūpaiḥ vā agaru saṃbhavaiḥ rakṣibhiḥ śva samāguptam vipula aiśvarya śālibhiḥ prākāra pratisaṃchanna prāsādaiḥ gṛha paṃktibhiḥ kailāsa śikhara prakhyā virājata sahasraśas anyāḥ jāṃbūnada mayāḥ prāsādānām ca paṃktayaḥ pāvakāḥ iva dīpyate jvālā vipula mālinaḥ kecid maṇi mayāḥ tatra prāsāda ābhavana uttamāḥ prerayan nidiśaḥ sarvāḥ śaradi iva uditāḥ grahāḥ bhūmikābhiḥ paricchinnam kānanaiḥ ca samaṃtataḥ gavākṣa mālā kalitam muktā dāmaiḥ vibhūṣitam vicitraiḥ bhūṣitaiḥ naddham sākṛtam dvāraiḥ su vipulaiḥ śvitraiḥ śobhita aṃsa paricchadaiḥ nānā ratna śataiḥ śvitraiḥ patākā śata śobhitaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phala ādyaiḥ ca phalānām ca suvarṇitaiḥ kadalī vanaiḥ nadībhiḥ śva taḍāgaiḥ śva palvalaiḥ asamaṃtataḥ vāpī bhiḥ dīrghikābhiḥ śvanhadaiḥ kūpaiḥ ca śobhitaiḥ kadaṃba pallavaiḥ śva api balākānām capam ktibhiḥ mayūraiḥ cakravākaiḥ śva tathā eva śuka sārikaiḥ tasmin advāra purāṇi aṣṭau pura śreṣṭhe dvijottama śrīdvāram prathamam tatra mahā asi yaḥ vyavasthitaḥ pūrvasyām diśi vaiśaivaḥ padma mālā vibhūṣitaḥ kṣmīdvāram tatas tasya yatra aṃbuda sama prabhaḥ mahākālaḥ mahā kāyaḥ sthitaḥ śūlaḥ mahā balaḥ śivam nāma puram tatra dakṣiṇena vya vasthitam gaṃḍakarṇaḥ sthitaḥ tatra mahā vīryaḥ śiva ājñayā sannidhāna itathā ca anya etasyām eva diśi ddijāḥ pālitam bhīma nādena gaṇeśena mahātmanā paścimam vāruṇam dvāram tatra naṃdīśvaraḥ śrutaḥ jivhena gaṇanāthena dhīmatā kīrtidvāram tathā udīcyām tasyām eva diśi dvijāḥ yatra arka varuṇa prakhyaḥ dvāra adhyakṣaḥ maheśvaraḥ upakrīḍanakaiḥ śvitraiḥ krīḍate bhagavān prabhuḥ yatra yānti jita krodha ajita lobha ajita iṃdriyāḥ śrūyaṃte paśupateḥ bhaktyā a rudra bhakti parāḥ dvijāḥ ye ca eva āgama saṃyuktāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca śrutabuddhayaḥ ye gṛhastha aśva dharma stha a rudra bhakta a jita klamāḥ nyāyataḥ yudhyamā na aśva saṃgrāma abhimukha īhatāḥ kṣatriya ugo grahasya artha imitra artha airāṣṭra pālane vaiśya aśva nirata adharme satya vācaḥ jita iṃdriyāḥ rujā iṃdra viṣṇu hṛdayāya iva ala ye suvarṇasya dātāraḥ tathā sarva priyaṃvadāḥ veda adhyayana saṃpannāḥ dhyāyinaḥ vrata cāriṇaḥ yaja̭ti vidhinā ayajñaiḥ kratubhiḥ śvāru dakṣiṇaiḥ te tatra gatvā adṛṣṭāḥ tu nivasaṃti yathāsukham kalpa ayuta sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi caturdaśa jāyaṃte śreṣṭha varṇe parame jagatīm ca abhinaṃdaṃti ciram pramuditāḥ tathā tatas param pravakṣyāmi raupya bhṛṃga nivāsitam rājataṃgiri rājasya śṛṃgam śrīsāgaram mahat yojanānām sahasrāṇi trīṇi evam tu param hitam prākāreṇa atha mahatā rāja tena samāvṛtam alaṃkṛtena divyena patākā dhvaja mālinā rājata dvāra sāhasaiḥ maṇi citraiḥ śva citritam yatra staṃbha sahasrābhyām dvābhyām prāsādam uttamam pura madhye tam rājatam dhātu bhūṣitam nānā viṣṇu padam nāma tat suraiḥ api kīrtitam catur dvāram catur śṛṃga kailāsa śikhara prabham nānā ratna samākīrṇa nānā druma latā āvṛtam tasya mūrdhni sthite dvāre kṛṣṇa rūpaḥ pratāpavān dvārādhyakṣaḥ sthitaḥ tatra hṛd yajña karaḥ balī pratīhāraḥ mahākāyaḥ hariprāṇa samaḥ jave tasmin madhumatī nāma nadī sva artha prakāśakā kāṃcanaiḥ kamalaiḥ śvāpi nānā pakṣi nināditā tatra atha su ciraṃkālaṃbhaya śoka vivarjitāḥ taiḥ taiḥ karmabhiḥ ādiṣṭāḥ śaktitaḥ samanuṣṭhitaiḥ prājāpatyam pravakṣyāmi tat meni gadataḥ śṛṇu tṛtīyam su sthiram śṛṃgam ma ṇi ratna maya prabham yojanānām sahasre dve viśokam nāma nāmataḥ caṃdra arka graha saṃkāśam prabhākaram anuttamam tribhiḥ śvitraiḥ su vipulaiḥ śikharaiḥ śva api alaṃkṛtam sthitam staṃbha sahasreṇa prāsāda pura mālinam harmya aṭṭālaka saṃyuktam valabhīnām śate na ca gavākṣāṇām sahasreṇa śobhitam paṃkti mālayā dvāraiḥ caturbhiḥ saṃyuktam sva pramāṇaiḥ su śobhitam alaṃkāraiḥ viśiṣṭa advyaiḥ sarvatas parivistṛtaḥ nāmnā advāra adhipaḥ śrīmān jvalana arka sama prabhaḥ dvāra adhyakṣaḥ dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sa jala aṃbuda sannibhaḥ nāmnā apara mayaḥ tasmin sthitaḥ saṃdhyā aruṇa prabhaḥ prajāpatiḥ sura śreṣṭhaḥ veda sāṃkhya viśāradaḥ amṛtā nāma vikhyātā nadī tasmin pura uttame padma nīlotpala yutā śubha kāṃcana vālukā su saṃdṛṣṭāḥ tad toyaṃpura vāsinaḥ tat pītvā ācajara anaivana śoka ūna pariśramaḥ prāsāda pura mālinam prāsādānām purāṇām ca mālābhiḥ paritas veṣṭitam vala bhīvaka dārū parivaṣṭi vāraṇa arthaṃkṛtā śataśas su prabhāḥ śubha karmāṇaḥ satya siddha ajita iṃdriyāḥ kratu dāna prasakta aśva gurū ye ca bhikṣām upāsaṃte tīrtha āyatana vāsinaḥ dharma iṣu niratāya ica viprāḥ krodha vivarjitāḥ ye ca dhyāna parāḥ nityam yoge ca niratāḥ sadā sāṃkhya dhyāna parāḥ viprāḥ teṣām vaipratyayaḥ mahān viśuddhāni ca karmāṇi ye caraṃti tad arthinaḥ te yāṃti paramam sthānam śoka moha vivarjitāḥ kalpa ayuta sahasrāṇi vartayanti sukha anvitāḥ śauca ācāra samāyuktāḥ bhaṃte param sukham jñānena eva ca tat sthānam prayāṃti parama arcitam sa tu ayukta a mahātmānaḥ jita krodha ajita iṃdriyāḥ prājāpatyam idam sthānam kīrtitam ca sanātanam evam etāni vipra ṛṣe bhūdhara iṃdra sya dhīmataḥ trīṇi tribhiḥ śva bhuvanaiḥ ātma sthānīkṛtāni vai te vai bhadra ādika yuta ayāvat bhānti sura īśvarāḥ meghā bhūtvā anu garjati vidyut mālāḥ iva aṃbare graha nakṣatra tārā aśvatebhavanti maheśvarāḥ kāmagāḥ sarva siddhārthāḥ ramaṃte bhavane surāḥ idam sva yaṃbhuvā ākhyātam paṭhet parvaṇi parvaṇi labhate abhīpsitān kāmān moha śoka vivarjitaḥ idam paramam pavitram śubham tat ca kathitam vipulam mayā muni iṃdra iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām śivapuravarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ idaṃparam iti viṣama chaṃdaḥ iti daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan śrotum icchāmi māhātmyam puṇya karmaṇaḥ yāni sthānāni rudrasya yathāvat anupūrvaśas bhūḥ āyā brahma loka aṃtāḥ satya lokāḥ prakīrtitāḥ evam śata sahasrāṇi yaḥ janānām pramāṇataḥ vaiṣṇavāt koṭi vijñeyam yojanānām pramāṇataḥ aṣṭamam rudra lokam tu etat uktam triviṣṭapam evam triviṣṭapam tatra devānām amita ojasām brahma viṣṇu maheśānām manubhiḥ ca samanvitam tasmāt triviṣṭapasya eva dvija ardhena pra māṇataḥ śatam rudra sahasrāṇi viṣṇu koṭi śatāni ca śiva prasādāt kīḍam sarve kusuma gaṃdhāvyāḥ khaḍga yaṣṭi dharāḥ api śūlinaḥ daṃṣṭriṇaḥ ca eva sarve vigata matsarāḥ caṃdra ardha maulinaḥ sarve sarve vṛṣabha gāminaḥ amalāḥ te mahātmāna trailokya su viśāra dāḥ sarvāmaṇi mayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣma kāṃcana vālukā natatra caṃdrāka vāyuḥ śva prakāśa tena vāti ca drāṃkita vibhūṣaṇāḥ svayam pratyakṣa vara dāḥ sarve eva prakāśante prāsāda harmya mālāni gopure lakṣaṇāni ca tatra vai brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdhaiḥ gṛhasthāḥ sat pathe sthitāḥ gaṃdha dhūpa ādibhiḥ ca eva jaṃtiśū linam sarva pāpa vinirmuktāḥ a gṛhasthāḥ sūrya varcasaḥ sarve lokāḥ adhastāt tu dviguṇena pramāṇataḥ bhuvanānām prabhu syānam dvitīyam samudā hṛtam tṛtīye tu mahā yogī bhūtaiḥ parivṛtaḥ ramat tatra api bhavanam divyam māyeśa vasatiḥ smṛtā gṛhāṇi ca eva divyāni pracurā ṇi mahāṃti ca agni sthānam param divyam paṃcamam samudāhṛtam agni sthānāt para tvena ugra nāma prabhu sthānam ṣaṣṭham tat samudāhṛtam tatra pāśupataiḥ sārdham yogibhiḥ parameśvaraḥ anugraha arthaiḥ lokānām sma guṃṭhitaḥ dama praśama saṃyuktāḥ bhūtānām abhaya pradāḥ yathā ukta kāriṇaḥ udānta ayoginaḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ bhaikṣa caryā vrata anityam dhyāna tatpara pūjakāḥ yāṃti pāśupatam sthānam punarāvṛtti durlabham tasmāt pāśupatāt sthānāt viguṇenapramāṇa taḥ māheśvaram param sthānam saptamam samudāhṛtam māheśvaraiḥ parivṛtaḥ vasate bhūta bhās vanaḥ tatra vai sarva loka īśaḥ īśvaraḥ kāma rūpadhṛk āviśya sarva bhūtāni loka ānaṃdam karoti vai na teṣām parisaṃkhyā na pramāṇam vā api vidyate īpsitān tu sṛjati eṣa bhūtānām īśvaraḥ yatas atas param dvijaśreṣṭha sthira sthānam iti smṛtam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ sanatkumāraḥ uvāca śṛṇu viprāḥ idam sthānam śivasya paramātmanaḥ yat na paśyaṃti durvṛttāḥ brahma ādyāḥ deva sattamāḥ sāṃkhya avāpi athavā ayogān avi duḥ tad vidaḥ janāḥ naca viṃdaṃti gṛtyāḥ tu umā naca gaṇa īśvaraḥ na viṣṇuḥ na ca rudra śva na ca anye dijasattamāḥ tasya eva ca prasādena yathājñānam tathā śṛṇu śatam koṭi sahasrāṇām yojanānām pramāṇataḥ umā devī ca suvratā vāma pārśva upaviṣṭā ca tasmāt vā eva vāma locanā dakṣiṇāt nayanāt muktaḥ jala biṃduḥ sita prabhā sā sarveṣu ca lokeṣu gatā vaibhūrbhu vādikam upasthāya imām aṃgām prāptā tasmāt gaṃgā iti ca ucyate netrābhyām prathamāt jātā gaṃgā iti dvijasattamāḥ brahmaṇaḥ yatna śīlasya īśvareṇa mahātmanā tat tṛtīyam tu vijñeyam kapāla vadanam mayā viṣṇu cakraṃ caturtha tu paṃcamaṃ dakṣa saṃbhavaḥ ṣaṣṭhakam tu yadā devaḥ himavaṃtam mahā mune taruṇa āditya saṃkāśaiḥ udraiḥ parivṛtā uvasat āha dṛṣṭānta iti dṛṣṭa nāśe jagati viśeṣa jñāna janikā vicāraṇā pravartate itas alīkam eva idam iti yathārtha jñānam ca saṃbhavati agocara nāśaka parivāra viṣaye tu katham viśeṣa dvitīyam tu parīvāram tatas dviguṇa vistarāt rudrāṇām prakīrtitāḥ apara āhṛṣṭa varṇānām koṭyā uśī niḥ dvijottamam paṃcamam tu parīvāram tatā dviguṇa vistaram ṣaṣṭham tu saptamam ca evam ye rudrāḥ tān nibodhata sadā evam aṣṭa parīvāram mānasam tu mahātmanaḥ na śakyam tasya vijñānam dṛṣṭāṃte tad vicāraṇā sarve viṣṇu puraḥsarāḥ evam yaḥ vadati sthānam śuddham parama nāmayam saḥ api gacchet param sthānam liṃgam śivam anāmayam kim punar śucayaḥ dāntāmaha īśvara parāyaṇāḥ evam brahma kriyā yogī lokānām bhūti vādinām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām śivamāhātmyam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca māhātmyam sarva bhūtānām prabhu tvam vartate śive vidhinā ātuṣyeta kena kapardī vṛṣavāhanaḥ vinīta veśana praveṣaḥ avimuktam vārāṇasī oṃkāram mahākāla sthānam ujjayinī etat ḻāgala ādi śṛṇu vyāsa emām vāṇīm sarva pāpa bhaya apahām tuṣyeta lokānām bhuvana īśvaraḥ tam aham kīrtayiṣyāmi śṛṇu tattvena me dvija meru parva tam āsādya deva yakṣa mahā uragāḥ śrotu kāmāḥ sthitāḥ purā namaskṛtvā pravakṣyāmi purāṇam brahma nirmitam tasmin vibhīṣaṇa aṃga tva asatya śāṃta ujita iṃdriyaḥ vinīta veśaḥ bhava namī śānam paripṛcchati etat me saṃśayam deva brūhi tvam vṛṣabhadhvaja īśvarā uvāca sa tyam śṭaṇu mahā bāho yasmāt tvam paripṛcchasi vibhīṣaṇa mahā rāja śṛṇu gutyam param mama karṇa gokarṇa ca viśe ṣataḥ avimuktam ca oṃkāram paṃcāyatanam uttamam etān dṛṣṭvā ālabhet mokṣam gulyam etat udāhṛtam oṃkāram cita yānasya tasya tuṣṭaḥ asmi aham sadā yatra sā kṣāt sthitaḥ devā rudrāḥ vā setu mukti daḥ agni prākāra saṃyuktam parikṣitam samaṃtataḥ yogīśvare suvarṇa ākhye tathā eva vātikeśavaḥ bhadradaṃḍī mahākālaḥ devaḥ taruvanesadā ugra ca gutya sthāna pavitrāṇi mamai tāni vibhīṣaṇa yetu vrajaṃti mad citta amad bhakta amat parāyaṇāḥ te śreṣṭhāḥ sarva bhūtānām bhavaṃti iha vibhīṣaṇa ayutāni arbudān koṭīḥ tathā padma ayutāni ca krīḍanti rudra lokān tān sadharmaḥ yaiḥ tu rādhyate teṣām samasta yuktānām puru ṣāṇām vibhīṣaṇa mleccha strī napuṃsakānām tu krūrāṇām pāpa karmaṇām yatra tatra mṛtānām tu dhruvam māheśvarī gatiḥ aṣṭau gu tya pavitrāṇi ye yajaṃti kṣitau narāḥ teṣām tuṣṭaḥ prayacchāmi gāṇapatyam vibhīṣaṇa mad bhakta a mad parāya ṇāḥ kim teṣām yajña dānena kriyābhiḥ śva vibhīṣaṇa tat phalam vyāsa sakalam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ ahorātra śatam trātvā yat phalam labhate naraḥ cāṃdrāyaṇa śatam kṛtvā yat phalam labhate naraḥ hiraṇyānām sahasreṇa yat phalam go mūtra yāvaka āhāra śāka bhikṣā aśanaiḥ tathā brahma ghnaḥ pitṛ hā gonaḥ surā paḥ gurutalpa gaḥ nityam liṃga arcanā dvi bhīṣaṇa ahaṃkartā ācahartā ācasraṣṭā ca api yuge yuge prabhavaḥ sarva bhūtānām mahātmā anā atra saṃśayaḥ aham bahmā ca viṣṇuśva somaśva aham mahā mune ti pada ādi ama aṃtam tathā eva pāsa kāse māyām upoṣaṇena bhavati lavaṇaḥ kṣārasamudraḥ lohitaḥ śoṇa bhadraḥ nāmanadaḥ śiva arcanena abhilaṣita siddhim āha śiva uddeśe yat kicid dṛśyate loke sarva ca aham vibhīṣaṇa kāmaḥ ca eva atha vāyuḥ vanānā ṛṣayaḥ eva ca ahaṃkṛtiḥ a saṃśayaḥ ca aham vibhīṣaṇa mataḥ śiśiraḥ tathā prāvṛṣ kālaḥ śva vijñeyaḥ śarad kālaḥ mahānadī anaṃtanāgarāj tathā pa rvataḥ maṃdaraḥ meruḥ kailāsaḥ gaṃdhamādanaḥ meruśva ahaṃtrikūṭa śvapāriyātraḥ ca parvataḥ maināka śva vibhīṣa kṣīroda isuramaḥ tathā lavaṇaḥ ca eva vijñeyaḥ lohita śva vibhīṣaṇa sthāvaram jaṃgamam ca eva kaḥ ūna saṃśayaḥ varṣe māsāḥ aśvapakṣaḥ ca ahorātram vibhīṣaṇa dīpa pradānam yaḥ dadyāt viprāya śuddha mānasaḥ tena dīpa pradānena mad puram yāti mānavaḥ svarṇa dānam tuyodadyāt gāṇapatyena yāmi aham dāsyāmi ca gatim puṇyām gāṇapatyam ca durlabham yajñaiḥ ṣahu viśiṣṭa annaiḥ yat phalam labhatet dija yathā abhilaṣitam puṇyam tatas sat phalavān ubhavet evam prakṣālya doṣām stunā ipya āmi paramām gatim karmaṇā a manasā a vācā dehena api cayat kṛtam mama arcana ratānām ca teṣām pāpam na vidyate yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram puṇyam pūjayet ekaliṃga ke tasya tuṣṭaḥ prayacchāmi gāṇapatyam na saṃśa yaḥ prabhāsam ca prayāgam ca naimipam puṣkaram tathā kadā cit nara adhamāḥ mama arcana gatam puṇyam labhaṃte ca vibhīṣaṇa hāyātrā iti teṣām mad bhaktānām puṇya kṣaya ādi doṣa śūnyam mā iti bhāvaḥ namām paśyaṃti te mṛḍhā manasā yemlīkṛtāḥ agnipraveśanam rutvā attha amāsopavāsakam kaṃdareṣu athavā araṇye gṛhe vā api samāhitaḥ yaḥ mām arcayate nityam tasya gāṇeśvarī gatiḥ yaḥ ca enam paṭhate nityam vā enam kīrtayet naraḥ yaḥ ca evam niyataḥ bhūtvā māhātmyam dhārayiṣyati caṃdra arkau na prakāśete yasmin deśe purā sadā prakāśaṃte hi manujāḥ tasmin deśe sute jasā māhātmyam tu suraśreṣṭha sarva bhūta namaskṛtam māhātmyam me tatas puṇyam paṭhi śuci dhārayiṣyaṃti ye ca anye khaḍga dhāra sudhā śuci na tepām kilbiṣam kiṃcid mayi tuṣṭe bhaviṣyati vibhī paṇau uvāca tvam vāyuḥ tvam hutāśaḥ ca tvam śivaḥ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ tvam śuciḥ sāgaraḥ ca eva bhaktānām ca sureśvaraḥ sarva bhūta namaskṛta tvam gatiḥ sarva bhūtānām śaraṇam tvam na saṃśayaḥ bhavān mokṣaḥ bhavān iṃdraḥ bhavān agniḥ sanātanaḥ bhavān dharma iṣu puṇya iṣu saṃkalpa śva manīṣiṇām tvaṃ catuṣṭiḥ vai puḥ medhā buddhiḥ kāmye manaḥ tathā śivam puṇyam ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tathā bhavān mokṣa śva śāṃtiḥ ca bhavān kṣetrajñaḥ ātmanaḥ bhavān stu sarva lokānām nityam harṣa vivardhanaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pāda aṃta sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukha yaḥ ca enam paṭhate nityam śiva proktam aniṃditaḥ vibhīṣaṇa yathānyāyam nityam devena pūjitam paṭhet vā a śṛṇuyāt ca eva caturdaśī aṣṭamīṣu ca tasya deyam idam śāstram anyathā na prakāśayet maheśvara stavam śrutvā svarga gacchet na saṃśayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca deva yajña phalāni iha dāna tīrtha phalāni ca upavāsa phalam ca eva dānānām tapasaḥ phalam a kṛtvā phalam eteṣām katham yatra vā kauśikī gaṃgā devī kāma artha mokṣa dā kurukṣetram prayāgam ca naimiṣam puṣkaram tathā trisrotā ca payoṣṇīca tṛtīyā gaṃḍakī tathā brahmāvartā nidīśvā yamunā ca atipāvanī gaṃgādvāram sa bhadrakarṇa hṛdaḥ tathā dṛṣadvatī karatoyā lohitā ca mahā nadī sarayū gaṃḍakī ca eva sāgaraḥ saritāṃpatiḥ kokā nadyāru ṇā tāmrā ramyaḥ śoṇaḥ mahān hadaḥ godāvarī narmadā canadī vetravatī tathā kāverī kṛṣṇavarṇā ca vitastā ca mahānadī om namaḥ śivāya caturdaśe jaga liṅgāt jātam
