pitṝṇām makṣayyam sthāneṣu eteṣu yonaraḥ śrāddham dayāt mahābhāgā udadyāt vā api tila udakam darbha āstaraṇa saṃkīrṇe piṃḍam sthāne nive bhyaca vaṃti parām gatim tasmāt vidvān adhīyīta śrāvayet ca samāhitaḥ na apraśāṃtāya dātavyam na ca anya ahita kāriṇe karkaśāya viśuddhāya piśunāya śaṭhāya ca capalāya nṛśaṃsa ayana deyam syāt kathaṃcana idam tu śreṣṭha putrāya śiṣyāya vahitāya ca ślāghine ślāghamānāya praśāṃtāya tapasvine priyaṃvadāya śrotriyāya bhaktāya ca maheśituḥ tathā ājñā sma adbhutyam iti smṛtam gatvā tapasyataḥ nityam mānasam vi malam śivam tatra aham niyataḥ vipra gaṃgādvāre ca nityaśas ādya sthāneṣu eteṣu pūjayaṃti sadāśivam gacchanti vimalāḥ śuddhāḥ padam māheśvaraṃhite na teṣām punarāvṛttiḥ bhavam mṛtyuḥ mahātmanām eṣa īśvara sadbhāvaḥ kathitaḥ te samāsatas yam sya upatiṣṭhati etat te kathitam puṇyam gutyānām ca eva kīrtanam satyena eva mahā mune iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām māheśvaravarṇanam nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ iti saptadaśaḥ udhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca hi suvrata prabhāvaiḥ karmaṇām ca eva kodhikaḥ vada īśvaraḥ etat me saṃśayam tāta brūhi buddhimatām vara atra api udāharaṃti imam itihāsam purā tanam purā trailokya vijaya īviṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā baliḥ baddhaḥ mahā rāja trailokyam prāptavān tadā athā ājagmuḥ prabhum draṣṭum devadevam sanātanam yatra asau viśvarūpākṣaḥ kṣīrodasi asamīpatas siddhāḥ vidyādharāḥ nāgāḥ nadyaḥ sarva aśva parvatāḥ dṛṣṭavām bara gatā viṣṇum devadevam sanātana jasi prabho tvad prasādāt ca kalyāṇam prāptam trailokyam avyayam asurāḥ ca hatāḥ sarve baddhaḥ ca eva baliḥ tathā sthāpitam ca tvayā apūrvam jagat sthāvara jaṃgamam tvam gatiḥ sarva devānām tvam yogī prabhuḥ avyayaḥ evam uktaḥ suraiḥ viṣṇuḥ siddha aiśva parama ṛṣibhiḥ pratyuvāca tatas viṣṇuḥ sarva gaḥ puruṣottamaḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi kāraṇam sura puṃgavāḥ yaḥ tuṣṭaḥ sarva bhū tānām khaṣṭṛ tvam adadāt śivaḥ sṛṣṭa aśva brahmaṇā ca eva sapta loka aśva māyayā tasya eva ca prabhāvena aham śreṣṭha tvam āgataḥ tad avastheṣu bhūteṣu ekaḥ han śayitaḥ tathā sahasra śīrṣaḥ vai bhūtvā sahasra akṣaḥ sahasra pād śaṃkha cakra gadā pāṇiḥ māyayā avimala aṃbhasi etasmin antare dūrāt paśyāmi vimalam prabhum kṛṣṇa ajina dharam devam kamaṃḍalu vibhūṣitam dāt iti asura aśva iti gatiḥ śaraṇam kāraṇam sarvasya brahmāṃḍasya iti śeṣaḥ grasitam nigīrṇa nimiṣa aṃtara mātreṇa prāptavān puruṣottamaḥ kaḥ tvam kutas vā kim śeṣa itattvataḥ vada kiṃciram ahaṃkartā asmi lokānām svayaṃbhūḥ viśvatomukhaḥ mayā api udāhṛtam trahman a nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ dhātā akartā acalokānām saṃhartā aca jagatprabhuḥ evam saṃbhāṣamāṇau parasparam iti tadā uttarāṃdiśam āsthāya jvālām paśyāmi tiṣṭhatīm tatas tām jvālām ālokya vismaya āviṣṭa mānasaḥ tat dṛṣṭvā aparam āśvaryam ubhau vismita mānasau divam bhuvam ca viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhate jvāla maṃḍalam prādeśa mātram duḥprekṣyam durnirūpyam ca duḥsaham mahā kāyam mahā tejaḥ vardhamānam nam iva ojasā jvāla mālā ādibhiḥ vyāmam sarva bhūta bhayaṃkaram tatas umām prābravīt brahmā api aham tvad samanvitaḥ atyaṃtam ca vijānīyāt liṃgasya asya mahātmanaḥ tvam ca adhastāt vijānīhi antam tasya mahātmanaḥ evam ca samayam kṛtvā āgataḥ varṣāṇām parasparam na ca paśyāmi tasyām tam tatas śrama vaśāt aham tayā eva brahma asaṃśrāṃtaḥ aṃtam ca eva na paśyati māyayā a mohitī tena naṣṭa saṃjñau ubhau tathā dhyānāt rudhvā mahādevam īśvaram sarvatomukham prabhavam nidhanam ca eva bhūtāḥ nām bhṛtam avyayam rodasī dyāvābhūmī atyantam sīmām paśyāmi apaśyam lakāraḥ brahma aṃjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā tasmai śarvāya śūline parameṣṭhi param brahma paramātmā aparam padam tvam yajñaḥ tvam vaṣaṭkāraḥ tvam oṃkāraḥ param padam svāhākāraḥ namaskāraḥ sarva karmasu sūktavān svāhākāra śva jāpi aśva vratāni niyamāni ca kāmaḥ krodha udbhavam duḥkham icchā dveṣaḥ damaḥ śamaḥ tvam paścāt sukha duḥkhayoḥ ṛtavaḥ vatsaṃrāḥ ca eva tathā iṃdriyāṇām sarveṣām iṃdriya arthāḥ smṛtāḥ sthaviṣṭhāḥ ca eva sūkṣmāḥ ca bhagavān eva sarvaśas viśvarūpaḥ mahārūpaḥ sarvarūpaḥ tathā eva ca te jasate iparam tejaḥ sparśānām sparśam eva ca rūpa gaṃdha rasāḥ āpaḥ dhi paśca bhuvana īśvaraḥ ākāśaḥ tvam ca vai chaṃdaḥ bhūtānām prabhuḥ avya yaḥ tvam kartā sarva bhūtānām lokeṣu pralaya aṃta kṛt tvam dhārayasi lokān trīn tvam eva sṛjasi prabho paścimena tuvatreṇa varuṇaḥ tvam prakāśase ādityāvasa vā rudrāvaruṇa śva tathā aśvinau siddha a vidyādharāḥ nāgāḥ apsaraḥ yakṣa rākṣasāḥ siddhāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ ca eva cāraṇa aśva tapodhanāḥ vālakhilya aśva ṛṣayaḥ tapaḥ siddhāḥ sahasraśas tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśa akṣarāśva mahā balāḥ sahasraśīrṣā nantaḥ ca vai sukiḥ eva ca arthaḥ dharma śva kāma śva yaśaḥ mohaḥ samīraṇaḥ agniḥ ca evam a hau viśva prajātāḥ te maheśvara ramā sītā tathā kālī devī gāyatrī eva ca pāṭha aṃtaram paśvāt iti akṣara ajara amaraṇa śūnyāḥ lakṣmīḥ kīrtiḥ dhṛtiḥ siddhiḥ medhā lajjā vapuḥ smṛtiḥ tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ tathā ānaṃdā ja yā devī sarasvatī tvattaḥ jātāḥ mahābhāga mahā balāḥ ṛtuḥ saṃvatsaraḥ māsaḥ pakṣaḥ ahorātraḥ eva ca kalā kāṣṭhāḥ nimeṣa aśva muhūrtāḥ cala vāḥ tathā nakṣatrāḥ ṇigrahāḥ ca eva aśvāgāvaḥ ajāvikāḥ rajobhiḥ māyayā āchannam na tvām paśyaṃti kevalam yoginaḥ nitya muktāḥ ye paśyaṃti tvām budhāḥ tathā māyayā āmohitam lokam tvat padam ca sanātanam na tvāṃ paśyaṃti saṃmūḍhāḥ ādau madhye tathā ca antena vidaṃti kadācana parātparaḥ tvam paramam ca śāśvatam namaḥ stute bhasma vibhūti śīla namaḥ stute kāma śarīra nāśin namaḥ naga iṃdra ātmaka deva nityam namaḥ astu te śaṃkara nīlakaṃṭha paṭṭiśam asi jātīyam kṣepaṇīyam śastram saḥ eva hetuḥ bhūtvā jagat kāraṇam bhūtvā sarva jit bhavati iti śeṣaḥ iti aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ evam saṃstūyamānaḥ hi kīrtyamānaḥ maheśvaraḥ babhāṣe ca tathā tuṣṭaḥ īśānaḥ vara daḥ prabhuḥ eka grīvaḥ su jaṭharaḥ nānā ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ nānā maṇi vicitra aṅgaḥ nānā gaṃdha anulepanaḥ pināka dīpita karaḥ paṭṭiśa aśani śūladhṛk yajña upavītī bhayaṃkaraḥ muktaḥ hāsaḥ tadā tena lokāḥ tatra prakaṃpitāḥ tatas provāca bhagavān prītaḥ utha api āvayoḥ tathā ayam me dakṣiṇaḥ bā huḥ brahmā tvam hi mama ātmajaḥ vāma bāhu śva meviṣṇu saṃyuge parājitaḥ munayaḥ sadṛśam samyak varam vṛṇuta suvratau tatas prahṛṣṭa manasau pādayoḥ patitau ubhau evam uktaḥ suraśreṣṭhaḥ sṛjadhvam vipulāḥ prajāḥ evam saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ prabhāvaḥ tasya yoginaḥ tena sarvam idam dṛṣṭa hetuḥ bhūtvā tu sarva jit idam ca svargyam āyuṣyam idam śāṃtikaram tathā tasya vighnam kurvati dānava agraha rākṣasāḥ piśāca ayātudhāna aśva gulya kāḥ bhuja gāḥ tathā yaḥ paṭhet aśuciḥ prātar brahmacārī jita iṃdriyaḥ iti śrī śi va mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām liṃgodbhavanāmā aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca abhyaṃge ca eva kim proktam kim phalam saptānām soma saṃsthānām yat phalam samudāhṛtam phalam vai sarva kāmyānām phalam bahu suvarṇakam ayuta arbuda koṭīnām teṣām aṣṭau yutāni ca tāḥ striyā uvā puruṣā uvā api yat iva atha napuṃsakaḥ māse māsetuyaḥ strāyāt yāvat jīvaṃrutī śuciḥ gaṃdha dānena tat puṇyam prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ gaṃdhāt abhyaṃga dānena ṣaṣṭi koṭyaḥ tathā eva ca catuḥ ṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi gavām vā hema mālinām yaḥ dadyāt kapilānām tu kṣīra snānasya yat phalam māse māse triṣavaṇam yaḥ strāyāt muni puṃgavaḥ pakṣe pakṣe cayaḥ snāyāt yāvajjīvam dvijaḥ śuciḥ aparādha śatam devaḥ kṣamate na atra saṃśayaḥ puṣpa dānena tat puṇyam prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ utpalam karavīram ca arka pallavakān tathā āghāti ājighrati nāgapuṣpam nāgacampaka puṣpam caṃpakam bilva patram ca devedeyam sadā naraiḥ kāla śva teṣām saṃproktaḥ tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu apāmārga kuśān ca eva āśu ayuktena nivedayet sadā asitāni puṣpāṇi yāvatkālam nivedayet caturṇām puṣpa jātīnām gaṃdham āghrāti śaṃkaraḥ utpalānām sahasreṇa arka me kam viśiṣyate caṃpakānām sahasreṇa dhattūram ca viśiṣyate dhattūra ka sahasreṇa nāgapuṣpam viśiṣyate siṃdhu puppa sahasreṇa punnāgaṃtu viśiṣyate punnāgānām sahasreṇa karṇikāram viśiṣyate siṃdhupuṣpa sahasaiḥ tu bṛhatīnām viśiṣyate bilva patrāt param na asti yena tuṣyati śaṃkaraḥ sarve śuddhāḥ sugaṃdhāḍhyā kṛṣṇanā eva nivedayet yatra ekam bilva patrasya catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ udāhṛtam yathālābham yathāpakṣam puṣpāṇi nivedayet alābhena tu puṣpāṇām parṇāni tu nivedayet viśeṣeṇa tu yaḥ bhaktyā teṣām eka phalam śṛṇu saviṃdati mahā puṇyam rudra sāyujyam āvrajet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām puṣpasāra samuddeśaḥ nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca bhūyas eva aham icchāmi īśvara ārādhanam katham jana prakāram abhidhāya jñāninām phala saṃsarga vimukhānām pūjā prakāram āha iti ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ su lopa abhāve ārpaḥ śiva prītaye kāñcana dānasya phalam āha gaṇeśvara patiḥ nadī sūrya ayuta sama prabhaḥ īśvarasya tu māhātmyam pṛcchate naṃdikeśvaraḥ yathoktam pṛcchate devyā īśvareṇa mahātmanā naṃdikeśvarā uvāca śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi tava snehāt mahā mune maheśvareṇa pārvatyāḥ puratas bhi hitam purā yatra aham tatra saḥ nityam bhavet aṣṭaguṇa anvitaḥ tasya haimavate śṛṃge gṛhaṃbāla arka sannibham yaḥ tu gāvaḥ hiraṇyam vāsam uddiśya pradāpayet tasya kāmadughām pṛthvīm dadāmi nirupadravām upahāra aiśva jāpya aiśva bhāvita aiśva āpi nityaśas agniṣṭoma ādibhiḥ yajñaiḥ yomā arcayati śobhane kasya ardhāsanam prāpya sura loke mahīyate sa yakṣāṇām guruḥ bhūtvā a yakṣaḥ bhava ti vīryavān sthāpanā abhyarcana mālyaiḥ dhūpa gaṃdha anulepanaiḥ arcayanti sureśvaram liṃge pūjām tu yā devī karoti ma maśobhane abhyaṃgena paṃcaśatam bhavet kṣīram paṃcaśatam deviḥ trāpa netu caturguṇam mālyepaṃcaśatam devi gīta vādya vara priye agarum śatasāhasam daśaguṇam caṃdanam bhavet gaṃdham daśaguṇam sarva yathoktam tat anaṃtaram mālyam paṃcaśatam devi nirmālyam tat anantaram kṛṣṇa aguruḥ smṛtaḥ aparādha sahasram ca kṣamate dubhāṣiṇi yat idam kṛṣṇa sāram dahet ca akṣa bhakta samānam tu devam sarva haram śi vam ghṛta abhiṣekam yaḥ kuryāt saṃvatsaram ataṃdritaḥ na asau mṭatyu vaśam gacchet gāṇapatyam tu bhokṣyate rudrāṇām sadṛśaḥ bhūtvā āraṣeṇa vicaret bhuvi tejaḥ maṃḍala saṃkāśam devam vrajati śakra vat caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām ubhau pakṣau vidhānataḥ bhāvāt bhakteḥ viṣa ādine śivāya taḥ jāti kāla ityādinā a niṣṭhā para nipātaḥ śiva dhyāne antarāyān āha bhāvanām dhyānam vinā api vidhinā ācitaḥ bhaktyā yathā bhāvitā eva phalam dāsyāmi anyathā abhābakānām arcanam vinā na iti anvayaḥ arcāyām pratimāyām acitaḥ ūna tathā tuṣya mi yathā lage acitaḥ tu tasya puṇya phalam devimat prasādāt idam śṛṇu śruti mātreṇa ye devi mama bhakti parāyaṇāḥ gāṇapatyam hiteṣām vai dadāmi kamala ānane yathāsthānāni yābhiḥ racitāni ivai maheśvarī tathā ta iṣu mṛtyu taḥ na kadā abhayam yaḥ tu kāma kṛtam tyaktvā ekabhakti kṛtaḥ naraḥ kāya vāc manaḥ saṃyuktaḥ yāvat jīvan tu gacchati yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam aneka vighna saṃbhūta atamasā bahulīkṛtāḥ vyādhita anitya yoga sthāḥ satya saṃdhā ajita iṃdriyāḥ ekāgra manasaḥ nityam paśyaṃti niścita āśvaye narāṇām alpa vittānām vidhinā abhāvanām vinā arcanam ca yathā uktam vaigutyam vā api matam śṛṇu liṃga arcitaḥ yayātasya tuṣyāmi hariṇa īkṣaṇe arcitaḥ aham varārāhe pūjitaḥ sarva daivataiḥ dhūpaiḥ gedhaiḥ aiśvamālyaiḥ ca rakta kāṃcana vāsasaiḥ martyaḥ puṃḍarīka phalam labhet bhaktyā aparamayā ayuktāḥ sakhyi yoga viśāradāḥ gacchanti mama lokān tu bhinnaḥ mattaḥ su dāruṇaḥ tapasā atuna śaknoti draṣṭum mām devatā api dhyānena eva niyuktā amām paśyaṃtidevinā anyathā sarva lokeṣu sarveṣām sāṃkhyā nārāyaṇī stutiḥ mad bhaktānām tu sarveṣām saṃkhyādevina vidyate kṣīyam sarva bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca vināśaḥ mama abhaktānām saṃhāre pina vidyate yaḥ bhūyas devatā yuktaḥ śraddhayā ācaya te naraḥ tasya tām mūrtim āsthāya prasīdāmi na saṃśayaḥ tasya aham na praṇaśyāmi sacamena praṇaśyati sarva āraṃbha itu yaḥ nityam satatam dhyāna karmaṇā samām praviśate devinā asti tatra vicāraṇā dhattūrakaiḥ ca puṣpaiḥ ca vilva patraiḥ śva śobhanaiḥ karavīra sahasram vā āyām me dadyāt viśeṣataḥ yat phalam śṛṇu sāṃpratam arkāṇām tu sahasreṇa padma me kam viśiṣyate caṃpakasya mahābhāge puṣpam dhattūrakaiḥ smṛtam tathā a parvasu suśroṇi tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu saṃvatsareṇa ca ekena puṣpāṇām yat phalam labhet śobhanaiḥ divya gaṃdha āṭyaiḥ bhṭaṇutasya api yat phalam baka puṣpa pradānena aśīti svarṇa jam phalam kāmena abhyarcamāna phalam mahat mama tulyaḥ naraḥ bhūtvā triśūlī vṛṣa vāhanaḥ yaḥ tu śaṃkara nirmālyam pādena ākramate naraḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi tiryagyoniṣu jāyate māsana ādinā yama niyamayoḥ sādhāraṇyāt iti bhāvaḥ padma arcitaiḥ praśasta pāḥ samam iti śeṣaḥ aśīti svarṇa jaṃtāvat dāna jam bhūtvā ācarati iti śeṣaḥ akāmāt vā a kāmāt api iti viṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ traya triṃśat sahasrāṇi deva dānava rākṣasāḥ pūjayaṃtiṃ tumān nityam dharma kāma artha siddhaye akāmāt paṭhate nityam yaḥ ca evam śṛṇu yān naraḥ rudra lokam avāpnoti tuṣṭaḥ tasya vṛṣadhvajaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām puppasa muddeśaḥ nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca śrotum icchāmi bhagavan yena tuṣyati śaṃkaraḥ puṣpam ca kīdṛśam proktam puṣpa mūlyam tu kīdṛśam kena puṣpeṇa kim puṇyam parimāṇam prakīrtitam tepām ca kīdṛśam yogam upayuktam mahat phalam yena kena prakāreṇa ā rya pūryaśva śaṃkaraḥ mahātmānam mahādevam svayam devī tapaḥ sthitā vijñāpayati deveśam bhūtānām ādim avyayam tvam nātha devadeveśayena tuṣyasi śaṃkara etat praśna varam brūhi yathā spṛṣṭa mahā ṛṣibhiḥ śaṃkaraḥ uvāca puṣpāṇi rakta pītāni asitāni tathā apare sugaṃdhinaḥ sugaṃdhāḥ cana anāgaṃdhāḥ tathā eva ca teṣām tra saṃkhyām vakṣyāmi devi ekamanāḥ śṛṇu devānām śukla puppetu durgaṃdhā dānaveṣu ca karkaśāḥ lomaśāḥ ca eva rākṣasānām chaṃṃti caye martyāḥ puṣpāṇi vividhāni ca tepām kīdṛśaḥ dharmaḥ saṃmārjana upalepane śaṃkaraḥ uvāca śṛṇu devi yathātathyam kīrtyamānam idam śṛṇu śaktitaḥ asya pradānena bhaktimān īśvare dvijaḥ daśa ca eva sahasrāṇi apsarobhiḥ cakrīḍate karṣa aśītikā vijñeyāḥ māṣāḥ ekādaśā api atha etat devi pramāṇena suvarṇa āśīrti bhaktimān droṇa puṣpam ca kuṃdam ca kurute śaṃkara arcanam ca sauvarṇikāḥ smṛtāḥ varṣa koṭiṃśataguṇam mamaloke mahīyate tailena api priya udāhṛta abhāve tu mānavaḥ tena dīpa pradānena śaśi vat rājate dvijaḥ puṣpa upahāra dhūpaiḥ ca śatam yoginam uttamam mālā śata sahasrasya japyam śataguṇam smṛtam agarum gaṃdha dhūpam ca caṃdanam ca vilepanam ekaviṃśat suvarṇāni mayāte tam pṛthak kṣīreṇa strāpayet liṃgam ghṛta abhyaṃgam ca kārayet pitṛ gaṃdharva yakṣāṇām nāgānām rāsām tathā sarva loka hita arthāya mayā ate kīrtitam tathā eṣa puṣpa vidhiḥ pro ktaḥ svayam īśena vai dvija puṣpa ādibhiḥ yoginam sevamānam śataguṇam phalam āmoti iti arthaḥ iti ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om namaḥ śivāya dvāviṃśe anāśaka vidhiḥ nānā aśubha phala āvahaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃhitāyām ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tīrthānām ca eva māsānām vidhānam paramam tathā upaviṣṭāḥ tu deva ādi ākhya ṛkṣa tripura śāsanam deva gaṃdharva sahitā muni saṃgha samākulāḥ praṣṭum ca parameśānam paramam ṛṣi pūjitam pareśaḥ bhagavān iṃdraḥ bhavān agniḥ sanātanaḥ bhavān dharmaśva kāmaśva saṃkalpaśva manīṣiṇaḥ tvam tuṣṭiḥ tvam dhṛtiḥ medhā śraddhā kāmaḥ manaḥ tathā caṃdra arkau na prakāśete yasmin deśe gatā mama prakāśante ca mad bhaktāḥ tasmin deśe su tejasā japya śva havya kavye manīṣibhiḥ māhātmyam te sura śreṣṭhayaḥ paṭhet niyataḥ naraḥ dhārayiṣyaṃti ye ca anye śraddadhāna aśva mānavāḥ na tepa kilviṣam kiṃcid tvayi tuṣṭe bhaviṣyati akṣayaśva aprameyaśva purāṇapuruṣaḥ ttam tvam vāyuḥ analaḥ ca evam tvam jalam tvam mahī smṛtaḥ jāti mallika yūthī aśva paṃca sauvarṇikāḥ smṛtaḥ raktotpalam tathā ca anye sapta sauvaṇikāḥ smṛtāḥ daśa sauvaṇikā jñeyā bilva aśokam iti smṛtāḥ kesara vṛkṣotpalam tu vijñeyam suvarṇāni tu dvādaśa dvātriṃśat suvarṇāni padma puṣpam tra kīrtitam śiva āha jāti ityādi paṃca sauvarṇikāḥ suvarṇapaṃcaka dāna phala kārpaṇāḥ evam api bhavati iti śeṣaḥ yān iti prābhuvanti iti śeṣaḥ vyāpakam cira sthāyi phalam upabhogam āchiāyāḥ aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi kuśapuṣpam prakīrtitam dvi sahasam tu vijñeyam śaṃkaram vai nigadyate sahasra aśīti vijñeyam bakapuṣpam nigadyate śatasāhasikaḥ jñeyaḥ dhattūrakaḥ iti smṛtaḥ etāvat puṣpa jātīnām gaṃdham āghrāmi aham sadā aṣṭa mīca aparān hetu tathā kṛṣṇa caturdaśī etaiḥ puṣpa viśeṣaiḥ akuryāt nāma arcanam sadā āya mārga siṃha ārūḍha māṃcchataḥ vyāpakam phalam śaivāt taranti eka manāḥ pūjayet māṃtuyonaraḥ kiṃvrataiḥ kiṃtapobhiḥ vā mahāsāṃkhyaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ ākāśena eva pāśena badhyate brahma vādinaḥ dhāroṣṇena tu kṣīreṇa pūjayitvā amama agratas nivedayet yathākāmam tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu koṭi śata sahasrāḥ tuhimālaye kṛṣṇāṣṭamīm arcayitvā yatra tatra yathā tathā sarveṣām ca eva puṣpāṇām viśeṣeṇa upalabhyate sa balā devadārum vā abhaktyā dhūpam pradāpayet śiva arcanam praśaṃsati mahātmānaḥ api muni yātanaiḥ munīnām api yātanā tad sthānī sadṛśam devi liṃgānām tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu dvātriṃśat tu suvarṇāni sārddha aśīti punar punar mālaye kāladīpaṃtamaḥ dadyāt saṃvatsaram mama apicam hṛdaya stham śivaḥ ca eva bhaktānām tu sureśvaraḥ yavaḥ haste suraśreṣṭha sarva bhūta namaskṛtaḥ aṣṭau kāmān prayacchasva akṣayāni mahāmate tvam gatiḥ sarva bhūtānām śaraṇam tvam na saṃśayaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ strāpayet ha maṃlabhate mahatīm śriyam bhava pārśvam upāgamya prāṃjaliḥ prayata ākaraiḥ upavāsam param dharma spṛśaṃti manasā a smṛtāḥ sarveṣām eva varṇān na kim phalam labhate naraḥ śrī mahādevaḥ uvāca śṭaṇude vi yathānyāyam upavāsa phalam śubham yathā ca vālakhilyānām naimiṣa araṇya vāsinām upavāsa phalam divyam samṛddhānām daridrāṇām jaṃtūnām duḥkha jīvinām śṛṇu vakṣyāḥ mita tvena mama vatrāt viśeṣataḥ upavāsa phala ca eva mokṣam vā api viśeṣataḥ sarvam etat aśeṣeṇa pravakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas yathā api devi saṃproktāḥ tathā tu ekamanāḥ śṛṇu paṃcamī ca eva ṣaṣṭhī ca paurṇamāsī tathā eva ca upoṣya āmama bhaktena śṛṇutasyā piyat phalam subhagā udarśanīya śva jñāna bhāgībhaviṣyati kṛṣṇāyām ca caturdaśyām tathā eva ca aṣṭamī bhavet upoṣyā eka yat phalam vasu āḍhyaḥ bahu putra śva vidyā bhāgī ca jāyate śuklām caturdaśīm ca eva yāvat śukla aṣṭamī bhavet upoṣyāḥ eka rātreṇa syā api yat phalam subhaga udarśanīya śva jñāṃna bhāgībhavet naraḥ nāṭyaḥ ca bahu putraḥ bhavet naraḥ dvādaśyām tu sadā vyāsaḥ eka bhaktena pūjayet vidyā bhāgī dhana avyaśca dhana bhāgī tu nirdiśet saṃvatsaram kṣipet śatam varṣa sahasrāṇi svarga loke mahīyate māse māse trirātreṇa yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram kṣipet apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃghṛṣṭā ivi mānedivī rājate yaḥ dīpaḥ udīpyamānaḥ tu kārtike ca vicakṣaṇaḥ apaḥ ca eva pivet māsam nivṛttaḥ bhojana aṃtare pauṣa māsam mahābhāge tasya api tvam vidhim śṛṇu vidhinā tena pānena tarpayitvā ca brāhmaṇān śaktyā tu dakṣi ṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam mahātmānaḥ śubhān lokān sarvadevena vaṃditāḥ śata varṣa sahasrāṇām sukham saṃti ca tri rātram kṣapayet yaḥ tu māgha imā setu yonaraḥ vividhena anna pānena tarpayitvā tu brāhmaṇān śaktitas dakṣiṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi triṃśat varṣa śatāni ca bhāgaśas sarveṣām eva saṃmānam rājarājena pūjitaḥ phālgunam tu yadā māsam eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet śaktitaḥ dakṣiṇām dayāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam jñāna vijñāna saṃpanna avinīta aśva bhavanti te dharma jñāḥ ca su bhāryā aśva aneka kratu yājakāḥ caitra māsam mahābhāge eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet tasmin māse samāpte tu pūjayitvā tumāṃpriye vidhinā annena pānena tarpayitvā tu brāhmaṇān śaktyā tu dakṣiṇām dayāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam aśītiṃtu sahasrāṇi śata varṣāṇi paṃca ya vāruṇam lokam āpnoti yā nena mama tejasā vaiśākham tu yadā māsam eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet tasmin māse samāpte tu pūjayitvā tumāṃpriye vidhinā annena pānena tarpayitvā tu brāhmaṇān śaktyā tu dakṣiṇām dayāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam triṃśat varṣa sahasrāṇi svarga loke mahīyate tatas śvāpi cyutaḥ bhūyas gavām koṭi pradaḥ bhavet jyeṣṭha māse ca eka bhaktaṃmad bhaktena aṃtarātmanā tasmin māse samāpte tu pūjayitvā tumāṃpriye vidhinā anne na pānena tarpayitvā ca brāhmaṇān na teṣām punarāvṛttiḥ vidyate tu mahātmanām epaḥ īśvara saṃbhāvaḥ kathitaḥ te samāsatas upavāsasya yat puṇyam sāṃvatsaram yathā uditam sārvakāmikam akṣayyam pitṛbhyaḥ vā upatiṣṭhati gām ca eva kapilām yaśva dadyāt ekasya brāhmaṇaḥ mad prabhāvāt saṃbhāvaḥ prabhāvaḥ sām vimānam labhate śubhraṃsa naraḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ ekaviṃśati kalpāni jātim evam na na āpnuyāt na jahāti ca tam dharma rāja dharma samāśritaḥ āṣāḍha māse saptamyām eka bhakta upoṣitaḥ śṛṃgāṭakam tadā āpārśva dakṣiṇām mūrtim āsthitaḥ labhate bahuśas dharma yoti upoṣati ca aṣṭamīm śrāvaṇam tu yadā vyāsa eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet vividha annena pānena tarpayitvā ca brāhmaṇān śaktyā tu dakṣiṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yatkam pitaraḥ tasya tuṣyaṃti viṃśat varṣa śatāni ca vividhena anna pānena tarpayitvā ca brāhmaṇān śaktyā tu dakṣiṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam śata varṣa sahasrāṇi vāyu loke mahīyate pramāṇena catur veda adhyāpanīya śvayaḥ bhavet āśvinam tu yadā vyāsaḥ eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet śaktyā tu dakṣi yat phalam ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi sūra loke mahīyate medhāvī vīrya saṃpannaḥ dhanībhavati mānavaḥ anukūlena kīrtitam aṣṭa varṣasya kālasya paṃcadhā sa bhavet naraḥ mama bhakti ratānām ca ekānta ra upavāsinām pakṣa upavāsinām ca eva tathā māsa upavāsinām śāka bha sa aṃbu bhakṣāṇām vaset tu jala śāyinām brahmacāri vratānām ca phala mūla āśinām tathā evaṃvidham pravakṣyāmi śṛṇutasya api yat phalam yaḥ tu kalyam ca sāyam ca bhuṃjānaḥ na antaram pivet ahiṃsā nirataḥ ca eva śṛṇutasya api yat phalam pauṃḍarīkasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ ahiṃsā nirataḥ ca eva śṭaṇutasya api yat phalam avyādhita ūniroga śvadī rgha āyuḥ ca eva jāyate yaḥ tu dvādaśa varṣāṇi eka āhāraḥ bhavet naraḥ ahiṃsā nirataḥ ca eva śṛṇutasya api yat phalam śata varṣa sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭi varṣa śatāni ca pade pade yajña phalam labhate ca anupūrvaśas kām cīnūpura śabde vasutaḥ saṃpratibuddhyate mṛdaṃga veṇu śabdena vaṃśaiḥ adhruvam utthitaḥ kalyaṃprātar vīrāsanam araṇya cāri tva ādikam divasam paṃcaśatikam rātrau sāhasikam japet balavān rūpa saṃpannaḥ labhate vipulām śriyam dīpa pradānam yaḥ udayāt daivate trāhmaṇeṣu ca atas rdhva pravakṣyāmi śṛṇutasya api yat phalam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dadāti iha pānīyam śraddhayā anvitaḥ caṃdra pradānam yaḥ dadyāt dijāya jvalitāni ca gṛha āṇi harmya yūthāni labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ dhenu pradānam yaḥ dayāt rāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ yāvanti romakūpāni tasya ā gātreṣu tiṣṭhati rūpavān śīla saṃpannaḥ vidyāvān śru abhavet naraḥ vastra dānam ca yaḥ dadyāt rāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ kapilā dānam yaḥ dadyāt rāhmaṇeṣu vi śeṣataḥ syāḥ gātreṣu vai dvija kanyā dānam tu yaḥ udayāt rāhmaṇebhyaḥ viśeṣataḥ brāhmaṇānām vivāhe ca vidhinā dvijasattama śayyā pradānam yaḥ udayāt rāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi svarga loke mahīyate yat tudānam mayā a vyāsa tavastre hāt udīritam upavāsasya yat puṇyam sāram ca eva sanātanam ti iti arthaḥ iti dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om namaḥśivāya trayoviṃśe śiva prīti kārakaḥ dharma auttamaḥ bahu dharma samāśritya ahiṃsāḥ satya vādinaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām upa vāsavidhiḥ nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tryakṣa tribhuvana śreṣṭha tryaṃbaka tridaśeśvara yakṣarakṣaḥ pramathana śūlapāṇeḥ ripuṃjaya ca eva anāśakaḥ paricaryā niyamāḥ yamāḥ katham puṣpāṇi gaṃdhāni phalāni kim svid syāt prabrūhi deveśvara śūlapāṇe śrī mahādevaḥ uvāca caturdaśīm aṣṭamī camadbhakta uyaḥ kṣipet naraḥ aṣṭamyām tuvarāraḥ hegavām snāpayet ca nirāhāraḥ prasanna ātmā ajita iṃdriyaḥ devasya utpādanam kṛtvā amunā avividhāḥ kriyāḥ siddha maṃtram sādhayeta śāka mūla phalāni ca sthaṃḍila iva ciṃtayet jānubhyām jānunā avāpi mahīm gatvā samāśritaḥ yathā āśri ta upaviṣṭaḥ uvā aśraddhayā aparayā ayutaḥ gṛhṇāti bhaktānām bhakti vatsale śraddhayā īdṛśī ceṣṭā bhakti saṃbodha lakṣaṇā khaṃḍa khādya vicitrāṇi divyāni annāni yāni ca śakti hīnāni adeyāni sa dya udbhūta rasāṃni ca tasya aham na eva tuṣya abhivimukhaḥ aham varānane maṃtram ca eva pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva āyata locane tam aham puṃḍarīkākṣam rudram om kārayāmi aham āyāṃtu devāḥ sa gaṇāḥ umā devī maheśvarī bhagavate mahādevāya pārśva gatāya anucarāya svāhā āmalakam sūkṣmam a yam śivaḥ trānam punar bhajasvāhā pradakṣiṇam taiḥ sarvam eva umā yute svāhā imāḥ āpaḥ śāṃtāḥ śatitamāḥ aṣṭatāḥ amṛtatamāḥ āpaḥpūtāḥ brahma pavitreṇa pūtāḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ āṃ hāraḥ sarva davānām gaṃdhaḥ ayam pratigṛhyatām svāhā su gaṃdham sumanaḥ divyaiḥ sarva gaṃdhaiḥ alaṃkṛtam pūtam brahma pavitreṇa pūtam sūryasya raśmibhiḥ puṣpam dattam mayā bhaktyā pratigṛhṇa namaḥ astu te namaḥ prajānāṃpataye namaḥ bhakta gaṇa ācita pratigṛhla emam dhūpam śiva liṃga namaḥ stute svāhā āpaḥ jyotiśva tejaśva devāḥ nām prabhavaḥ smṛtaḥ pūtaḥ brahma pavitreṇa pūtaḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ namaḥ stute nivedya manasā yuktam devānām gaṃdham uttamam pūtaḥ trahma pavitreṇa pūtaḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ āhāraḥ svāhā arcitaḥ pūjitaḥ ca eva mayā abhaktyā aniveditāḥ gaṃdha puṣpa upahāreṇa tad kṛpām kartum arhasi caturdaśīm pravakṣyāmi raktacaṃdana gaṃdhaiḥ śva haritāla anulepanaiḥ kadaṃbaiḥ kiṃśuka aśokaiḥ gaṃdha puṣpa atimuktakaiḥ patraiḥ śvamam asānnidhyam phalaiḥ puṣpaiḥ tṛṇaiḥ tathā maṃtreṇa ca dahet dhūpam ghṛtena saha guggulam namaḥ śrīvatsa dhārāya namaḥ jyeṣṭhabhujāya ca namaḥ pināka dhārin te namaḥ cakra gadā dhara umāpatim namasyāmi jaṃbūdvīpa pate prabho dvau etau deva saṃghātau prasīdetām ane kadhā śṭaṇuyāt kutsitaḥ uvā api yatra vā amṛta sūtakam tasya aham satatam prītaḥ bhaviṣyāmi yaśasvini etat te kathitam devi caturdaśī aṣṭamīṣu ca vyāsaḥ uvāca nāma aṣṭamī katham ca eva kartavyā mānuṣeṇa vai tat aham śrotum icchāmi tvad prasādāt mahā mune śrutam pūrvam mayā avyāsa rudrasya tu mahātmanaḥ devyā ca saṃśayam pṛṣṭaḥ himavati naga uttame yathā śrutam mayā avyāsa kathayāmi ca suvrata nāma aṣṭamīm pravakṣyāmi devasya vidhim uttamam yān śrutvā nirmalam yāti rudrasya ca mahātmanaḥ mārgaśīrṣe tu vai māse aṣṭamyām śaṃkaram naraḥ yamba kaṃca sanātana iti pāṭha antaram go mūtra prāśanam kṛtvā sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate labhate ca akṣayam puṇyam yaḥ upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm pauṣa māse tathā aṣṭamyām devadevam prapūjayet akṣayam labhate puṇyam yadi upa upyati ca aṣṭamīm māgha māse tathā aṣṭamyām maheśvaram prapūjayet ca eva dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ labhate bahu śaḥ puṇyam yaḥ upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm phālgune ca tathā aṣṭamyām tryaṃbakam ca eva pūjayet tilasya prāśanam rutvā dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśri taḥ labhate bahuśas dharmayā upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm caitre māse tathā aṣṭamyām sanātanam tu pūjayet yavān ca prāśayet tatra dakṣiṇā mūrtim āśritaḥ labhate bahuśas dharmayā upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm vaiśākhe ca tathā aṣṭamyām sadāśiva iti pūjanam jalasya prāśanam kuryāt dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ labhate vaḍuśaḥ dharmayā upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm jyeṣṭha māse tathā aṣṭamyām bhagavān iti pū jayet gomaya prāśanam kuryāt dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ labhate bahuśas dharmayā upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm āṣāḍhe tu tathā aṣṭamyām nīlakaṃṭham prapūjayet śṛṃgāṭaka prāśanam ca dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ eva ca labhate bahuśas dharmayā upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm aṣṭamyām sthāṇum eva ca pūjām ca mahatīm kṛtvā atra āśayet lavaṇa udakam dakṣiṇāmūrtim āsthāya prāśayet ca vicakṣaṇaḥ labhate bahuśas dharmayā upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm bhādrapade yadā vyāsa aṣṭamyām śaṃbhum eva ca daghna śvaprāśanam rutvā dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ labhate bahuśas dharmayā upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm aṣṭamyām īśvara iti ca taṃdula udakam aśnīyāt dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ labhate bahuśas dharma yadi upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm dadhi ca eva iha prāśnīyāt dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ śṛṅgāṭakam phala viśeṣaḥ evam aṣṭamī mātra pūjanam abhidhāya nitya pūjanam āha sārūpyam teṣām bhavati iti āha mahātmanā śivena saha iti trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ labhate bahuśas dharmam yaḥ upoṣyati ca aṣṭamīm arcayet satatam rudram prasanna ātmā samāḥ hitaḥ gaṃdhaiḥ mālyaiḥ śva dhūpaiḥ śva puṣpaiḥ ca eva viśeṣataḥ samāpte bhojayet viprān dadyāt sauvarṇa dakṣiṇām bhakṣayet ca yathāśaktyā śiva yogī viśeṣataḥ tatas mṭatyu vaśam prāpya śiva lokam sa gacchati saṃgacchanti śivam lokam svacchaṃdaḥ gatim uttamām divya apsaraḥ samākīrṇa krīḍate ca mahātmanā vṛṣa yuktena yānena svacchaṃdaḥ lalitaḥ sadā prārthitam labhate rājyam prajñā yuktaḥ bahu śrutaḥ śṛṇu mānī tu dharma jñaḥ mithyā daṃbha vivarjitaḥ pūjām ca smarate nityam devam pūjayate punar iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām nāma aṣṭamīvidhi kathanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca yena mānavāḥ sarva lakṣaṇa sam pannāḥ saubhāgya aśiva darśanāḥ jāyate apūrva lakṣaṇāḥ brūhi tattvena kathaya pramāṇa lakṣaṇa aṣṭamīm śrutam pūrvam mayā a vyāsa yat devyai proktavān haraḥ śṛṇu devi param divyam upavāsam param mama lakṣaṇāṣṭamīm pravakṣyāmi tat śṛṇutvam trilocane kārtikasya tathā aṣṭamyām upoṣya mama bhaktimān ahar rātra uṣitaḥ bhūtvā śivā iti ca prapūjayet sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyuktaḥ jāyate mānava uttamaḥ nai vaṃ buddhyā āmi śūla aṃka nikhilaṃ tat dravīhi me nāma nāma tathā aṣṭamyām vistareṇa bravīhi me vistaram te pravakṣyāmi śṭaṇu devi naga ātmaje nātham śirasi vaidevi pāda īśaṃkaram eva ca jaṃghe ati rudra medevi īśānaṃkaṭiḥ ucyate tryaṃbakam ca tatas devika paryaṣṭa aṃgam eva ca śūlapāṇiḥ tu vakṣaḥ gaḥ skaṃdha itu vṛṣabhadhvajam umāpati śvamede vināsā paśupatiḥ tathā pura hā karṇayoḥ de vi tri pu ra ghna śva cakṣuṣī śmaśānavāsi īś bhū madhye bhūteśa iti kapolayoḥ dakṣa yajña vināśī tudaṃta sevanam eva ca jaṭilam jivhayā devi śiraḥ paśupati iti ca śaśāṃka aṃka iti ca mūrdhni lalāṭe tu umāpriyaḥ gaṃgādhara iti keśeṣu sarva aṃge śivam eva ca ahani ahani yaḥ bhaktyā upoṣya vidhinā aṣṭamīm arcayet mām tatas rudra prayata ātmā samāhitaḥ gaṃdha dīpaiḥ va mālyaiḥ ca dhūpaiḥ ca eva viśeṣataḥ dadyāt tāmra ghaṭān pūrṇān brāhmaṇāya viśeṣataḥ dakṣiṇām ca yathā śaktyā suvarṇānām yathāmati mṛd mayam bhājanam tatas kāla kṣayam prāpya jāyate capu naḥ kramāt sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannaḥ jāyate mānava uttamaḥ na kaścid lakṣaṇaiḥ hīnaḥ bhavate puruṣa uttamaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām nāmalakṣaṇāṣṭamīkathanam nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ kathayiṣyāmi aham dharmam yathāvat anupūrva śas anna dānāt param dānam na eva kiṃcid viśiṣyate annāt bhavanti bhūtāni tasmāt tat adhikam smṛtam mayūra haṃsa saṃyuktam sarva kāma samṛddhimat vimānam sūrya saṃkāśam anna daḥ labhate śubham yat imā anu syamāyāti kadācid puruṣottamaḥ dhana dhānya samākīrṇe kuleya ati su rūpavān yathāśakti ātuya udayāt viprāya annam varaḥ naraḥ kadācid api yaḥ dadyāt annam viprāya saṃskṛtam tasya śataguṇam puṇyam sahasraguṇam eva ca avaghātam avajñātam asaṃskṛtam atha api vā annaṃpradayā gro devi yādṛśam tādṛśam śubhe tasya api nara ke ghore pātyamānasya rākṣasaiḥ yaḥ di mānuṣyam āyāti kadācid sa naraḥ punar annam eva viśiṣṭam hi tasmāt parataram na hi annam prajāpatiḥ proktam saca saṃvatsaraḥ punar tasmāt bhavanti bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca tasmāt annam viśiṣṭam vai sarvebhyaḥ eti viśrutiḥ anna dānāt param dānam na eva kim cit viśiṣyate annāt bhavanti bhūtāni tasmāt tat vai viśiṣyate sugaṃdhāḥ śītalāḥ ca aporasaiḥ divyaiḥ samanvitāḥ vimānam sūrya saṃkāśam apsaraḥ gaṇa nāditam tatra asau ayutāni aṣṭau uṣitvā deva vat sukhī kule mahati saṃkīrṇe jāyate dhana dhānyavān tayā anna pūrṇayā ubhām ḍam brāhmaṇāya prayacchati rasāḥ tasya upatiṣṭanti pūjyate ca divaṃgataḥ bhājana anicayā udadyāt anna pūrṇa śubha ānane bho janasya artha bhogānām tārayet ca pitṝn bhayāt taḍāgam yaḥ tu kurvīta vāpikāṃca samṛddhimān tārayitvā ca sa pitṝn tathā eva ca pitāmahān prapitāmaha lokeṣu kāmaga iṣu vihaṃgamaḥ bhogī bhavati bhogyānām rājā amātya śva jāyate dātāya śuci smite dadyāt ca brāhmaṇebhyaḥ tu bhojayitvā yathā rthavat aṣṭabhiḥ su vicitrābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam hiraṇyam hema bhūmim ca tilān ratnān iva apiyaḥ dāne phalam āha bhājanāni iti sa pitṝn bhojanasya artha bhogānām ca bhayāt tārayet iti yojanā tat pitṝṇām bhojana ādi alābha jaṃbhayam na bhavati iti arthaḥ pradadyāt sarva bhūtebhyaḥ tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu tata yuta śva dharma ātmā sarva kāma samṛddhimān yaḥ tu vṛkṣam cakurute chāyā puṣpa phala anvitam yat phalam samavāpnoti tat śṛṇuṣva mahāmate yāvat ṛkṣasya patrāṇi upayuṃjati dehinaḥ tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi tārayitvā pitṝn api samṛddham phalam āpnuyāt phalānām rūpavān subhaga vaha saḥ a psaraḥ śata saṃkīrṇe vimāne divi modate tāmrayaḥ bhājanam dadyāt rāhmaṇebhyaḥ viśeṣataḥ sa lokaṃbrahmaṇaḥ prāpya sarva kāma aiśva saṃvṛtaḥ varṣa koṭi śatam ca eva tad praśastena karmaṇā gṛhamedhī sadā dātā ābhogavān ca eva jāyate oṣadhīḥ yaḥ prayaccheta bāhmaṇāya mahātmane bahu varṣa sahasrāṇi carate kāmarūpavān hemnā acitram bhūṣitam su lakṣaṇam ca iti arthaḥ ratham aśvam gajam iti pāṭha antaram yadi mānuṣyam āyāti sa naraḥ kāla paryayāt paśum yaḥ tu prayaccheta brāhmaṇāyasa māhitaḥ annaṃ yaḥ tu prayaccheta saṃskṛtam brāhmaṇāya ca yaḥ tu śayyām prayaccheta trāhmaṇāya su alaṃkṛtām sa gatvā pitṛlākā iva varṣa ayuta śatam vasat bhāryā prāpnoti bhadrāṃgīm prajāvān śca upajāyate ratham aśvayujam dāsīm kanyām gṛham atha api vā jaladhenum cayaḥ dadyāt tasya dāna phalam śṛṇu tasya su puṣkalam rutvā kuṃbhān ca saṃpūrṇān mālyaiḥ śva samalaṃkṛtāḥ bhakṣya bhojyaiḥ su saṃvṛta antala pātrāṇi dāpayet dakṣiṇām puṣkalām dayāt tebhyaḥ tān darśayet budhaḥ āpaḥ śiva aśva saumya aśva tarpayaṃti pitṛn yathā kāma dāḥ kāma dātāraḥ bhavaṃti ca pade pade evam da tvā ca vā etadā tila pātrāṇi yaḥ udayāt ta thā vastra yugam naraḥ vṛtaṃgāḥ vaḥ prasūyate ghṛtam bhūmyām pratiṣṭhitam ghṛtam agni śvadeva aśva ghṛtam me saṃpradīyatām brāhmaṇān tarpayitvā tu gaṃdha mālyaiḥ tān dāna kāle tatas tasyām surā gātrāṇi saṃśritāḥ brahmātasya āḥśritaḥ mūrdhniśakaḥ bhālaṃsam āśritaḥ caṃdra āditya one deśe prāṇa iva āyuḥ prabhaṃjanaḥ mukham tasya āśritaḥ vanhiḥ jivhām somaḥ svayaṃbhavaḥ karṇayoḥ ca aśvinau devau śiraḥ rudrāḥ samāśritāḥ pādayoḥ lokapāla aśva sarvaiḥ ca eva tu pannagāḥ samudrāḥ sama jaṭhare grīvāyām tapanāḥ śritāḥ stane gaṃgāsarit śreṣṭhā pārśvatuvasa vaḥ tathā upastham ca gudam tīrthāḥ prajāpati samāśritaḥ purīṣam śrīḥ babhūva asya a nāgāḥ śvāsa anila āśritāḥ sādhyāḥ viśve atha loka aśvapuccham eva tu saṃsthitāḥ maṃtra a yajña aśva dāna niyama aśva ṛṣibhiḥ saha nakṣatrāṇi grahāḥ ca eva tārā rūpā gāyatrī ca eva viṣṇu śva jagatī paṃktiḥ eva ca anuṣṭubh ca eva yajña śva sāmāni ātharvaṇaḥ tathā dharmaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca eva bhūta anisaritaḥ tathā romakūpāṇi saṃśritya tasya divyām vyavasthitāḥ yakṣa aśva rākṣasāḥ ca eva piśācāḥ ca eva pakṣiṇaḥ yajñaḥ tathā dakṣiṇā aśva tathā apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ gaṃdharvāḥ ca anye pi evamādayaḥ tasya a viṣāṇayoḥ vyāsa sarve eva samāśritāḥ phalāni sarva dānānām patayaḥ śva pṛthagvidhāḥ kuśāḥ suvarṇa bīja ani tilāḥ siddhārthakāḥ ta thā sarva deva mayīm dogdhrīm sarva loka mayī tathā prayacchāmi mahā mūrtim akṣayām me śubhām iti evam tatra tatra gatā sā tathā tārayet tu bhayāt tathā sarvān kāmān saṃṭaṇoti goṃdānena yathā amaraḥ ihajātaḥ catām eva kāmagām pratipadyate yā iti śeṣaḥ vā pṛthivī phalam tad dāna phalam āvāsam nivāsa sthānam puṇḍarīkam pauṇḍarīka yāga phalam uddharet ciki manasā mānuṣaḥ bhūtvā go sahasrī mahā balaḥ rūpavān balavān ca eva prasūyamānām yogān tu dadyāt ubhayatas mukhīm hema śṛṃgī raupya khurīṃsa jāti smara tām labhet ruṣṇājinam tu yaḥ dadyāt vatine brahmacāriṇe prāpnuyāt puṃḍarīkaṃtu gosa hasaṃtu viṃdati sa smṛtim ca parām labdhvā yogam āpnoti suvrate kamaṃḍalam ca yaḥ dadyāt rāhmaṇāya nara uttamaḥ vyādhitam yaḥ tu viprarṣe dīnam mūḍham acetanam daśānām aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ yaḥ ca eva etāni ramyāṇi dānā nyuktāni kṛtsraśas sarvāṇi yugapad ca eva pṛthivyām ekarāṅga vet idam yaḥ śṛṇuyāt nityam dadyāt ca eva sva śaktitaḥ paśyati ca mahābhāgaḥ saḥ api gacchet triviṣṭapam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām dānadharmavidhinirūpaṇanāmapam caviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ īśvarā uvāca devi śṛṇuṣva bhūyas upi yathā dānam vinā aśubham satena karmaṇā adevi mām bhajan iva nityaśas māgha māse tu kurvāṇaḥ śriyam āpnoti vaipriye iti pañjaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om namaḥ śivāya mahā phalam pūrvatra mārgaśīrṣa upavāsa phala abhidhāne bhajan iva iti iva pada dya atyam phalam sphorayati śakra lokatā aṃśaka sālokyam eka ekaḥ eka bhaktam tu kurvāṇaḥ phālgune māsi nityaśas strīṣu saubhāgyam āpnoti striyaḥ śva parama śriyam vaiśākham yaḥ kṣipet māsam eka bhaktena mānavaḥ jñāti saṃśreṣṭha tāṃtrā pya pūjitaḥ dhanavān api jyeṣṭham āsam kṣipet yaḥ vai eka bhaktam samācaran jyeṣṭhaḥ bhavatiḥ bhrātṝṇām bhogān āpnoti puṣkalān āṣāḍha vāpī yaḥ māsam eka bhaktam samācaret sa rājñaḥ mānya tām prāpya kāmān āpnoti puṣkalān śrāvaṇe deviyomāse bhaktam samācaret saināpatyam ca saṃprāpya balavān apijāyate yā api ca āśvayujam māsam eka bhaktena tiṣṭhati vāṇijyam labhate tasya kṛṣiḥ paśu gaṇāḥ tathā kārtikam vā api yaḥ māsam eka bhaktena tiṣṭhati yaḥ kṣipet eka bhaktena mārgaśīrṣa na saṃśayaḥ pūrṇam eka bhaktena tiṣṭhati sa pārthiva samobhū tvā mahīṃpāti maheṃdra vat daśā anāṃsa suvarṇānām phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ māse māse ahorātram sarva pāpa vivarjitaḥ māse māse cayaḥkuryā tri rātram kṣepayet naraḥ yaḥ bhum kte divase ṣaṣṭhe nityam niyamam āsthitaḥ vāruṇam lokam āsādya saca viṃdet mahā padam aṣṭame ahani yaḥ bhuṃkte pratimāsam ataṃdritaḥ vāruṇam lokam āsthāya saca viṃdet mahat phalam sadā mānuṣyam ca punar prāpya daśa bhāryā labheta saḥ ekādaśe tu yoḥ bhukte divase mānavaḥ śuciḥ ekādaśyāḥ phalam prāpya yajñavān iha jāyate atha iha mānuṣaḥ bhūtvā sana raḥ jāyate śuciḥ iha rājā mahān bhūmau yatra tatra abhijāyate pūjyamānaḥ yathā devaḥ stūyamānaḥ atha sarvaśas jvalana ādi tya saṃkāśaḥ sa nityaṃmukham aśnute tatas padmāsanam prāpya daśa bhāryā labhetasaḥ athavā apunarāvṛttiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhavati īśvaraḥ snātaḥ ca śuciḥ athavā a hutvā anīṃśu asamāhitaḥ dīkṣayitvā tathā ātmānam upavāsam caret dijaḥ tam yāṃti śaraṇam ca eva durgam pāla agniḥ eva ca yaḥ japan deva gāyatrīm pavitrāṇi ca nityaśas rudra nāma guṇān vāpī rātrau ca sthaṃḍileśayaḥ kuśān āstīrya vidhivat strī śūdra parivarjitaḥ samaśnīyāt tu vairātra vīta rāgaḥ vimatsaraḥ yāvati ahāni saṃtiṣṭhet tāvat viprān tu bhojayet tatas pūrṇe tu kāle vai brāhmaṇānām śataṃgavām sahasram athavā aśaktyā pūjayitvā tu sarvaśas haviṣyam bhojanam dadyāt gāvaḥ vāsāṃsi cakra māt vṛṣabham yaḥ tu nīla aṃgaṃgām dadyāt ca payasvinīm yāvat roma sahasrāṇi varṣāṇa divi modate tila pātrāṇi yaḥ dadyāt viprebhyaḥ śraddhayā naraḥ amāvā syāṃsa māsa agra kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī samāhitaḥ yaḥ tu cāṃdrāyaṇam kuryāt yathā ukta mu samāhitaḥ sa pitṝn tarpayitvā tu akṣayam nara puṃga vaḥ pavitrāṇām vidhim bhū yaḥ ekacittā avadhāya mahā sāṃtapanam yaḥ tu karoti su mahā manāḥ tulāpuruṣa kaṃyaśva ati dvijasattame rudh śrātikṛcchreṇa tathā a gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt yaśrva sarvāṇi dānāni kurute nara sattamaḥ yam yam prārthayate kāmam tam tam eva samaśnute kaṃca upayuñjānaḥ go mūtreṇa apisaṃskṛtam piṇyāka mātra bhakṣaḥ vā vāyubhakṣaḥ yava apunar yā vat uktam samāsena mahātmā anaṣṭa kilviṣaḥ sālokyam vā mahā śabdam yatheṣṭam mokṣam eva ca aiśvaryam ca mahat prāpya dīpyamānaḥ a vatiṣṭhati varam prāpya ca sarvāṇi dānāni ca yathepsitam vinā amaṃtreṇa satatam śūdrāṇām iha sarvaśas amaṃtrāḥ te sṣṭatāḥ sarve śūdrā vigata kalmaṣāḥ strīṇām ca daivatam bharttā atatas nā anyaḥ vidhīyate sāgatiḥ paramaḥ dharmaḥ sa dhām paramam smṛtam tena sā abhyanujñātā idam dharma samācaret yātutena ananujñātā adharmam kuryāt śuci smitā su puṣkalam dadyāt ca paṭhate nārī tasya anaṃtam hi tat phalam vaśyaḥ śvā asyāḥ bhavet bhartā apriyā tasya ca sā tathā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇa iṣaviśaḥ adhyāyaḥ lokakartāram īśānam sarvajñam aparājitam praṇamāmi trinayanam bhavantam śūlapāṇinam bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca yat ca vedyam paraṃhara yat pṛcchāmi mahāde vata me brūhi yayā tathā yān ca vainiyamān cakuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā viśaḥ kecid teṣām vai brūhi yat phalam samṛddhāḥ phala vṛddhayaḥ dṛśyate niyamānām ca yoga dhyāna tapaḥ layāḥ eṣa me saṃśayaḥ deva citta vyākula kā rakaḥ śamayasva mahābuddhe nīhāram iva bhāskaraḥ śrī maheśvaraḥ uvāca niyamam tu naraḥ kṛtvā niyamāt niyata indriyaḥ duṣkaram niyamam kartu manuṣyeṇa viśeṣataḥ mahiṃsakāḥ deva tva devatāḥ prāptāḥ aniyamāt niyama anvite niṣkalmapa ātapaḥ maṃca yathā tathā mama patnī tvam āyāsi tvam śubhena atra saṃśayaḥ niyamam yaḥ ca kurute niyamān tatas dvijātīnām priyam tat me niśāmaya naga ātmaje vārāṇasyām abhūt vipraḥ kevalam nāma dhārakaḥ vikṛtaḥ karma mūḍhaḥ ca para dravya apahārakaḥ niṣṭhuraḥ karuṇaḥ devi jātikarma vighaṭṭakaḥ tyāṃdhrajaḥ pāpaḥ aviśuddhaḥ bhāti matsaraḥ mithyā vinītaḥ durmedhā deva dānava dhikkṛtaḥ para dravyeṇa saṃtuṣṭaḥ para dravya a vicārakaḥ uddejanīyaḥ sarvasya duṣṭa ahiḥ iva pārvati mithyā vinītaḥ durmedhāḥ veda vāda vahiṣkṛtaḥ chinna daṃṣṭraḥ yathā sarpaḥ śṛṃga hīnaḥ yathā vṛṣaḥ nunna pakṣaḥ yathā pakṣī vipuṣpā eva pādapaḥ vārāṇasyām sarvaiḥ vipraḥ vipra koṭi śata ardanaḥ āste artha hārakaḥ saḥ asti iha puruṣaḥ pramadā uttame yasya iṣṭaḥ sa bhavet bhīruḥ duṣṭa ahiḥ iva duḥkha daḥ tam rucira ānane tasya varṣa śatāni eva vaṇij āpaṇagasya vai pārvati atha aṃbu japa daḥ siddhaḥ siddha gaṃdharva pūjitaḥ vārāṇasīm gataḥ draṣṭum oṃkāram siddha vaṃditam vratam āsthāya tkṛtaḥ ārta bhūtāḥ kalā vāsa sarve tam praṇamaṃti ca pradakṣiṇam prakurvati janma pāpa kṣaya āvaham rudra āvāse tu pānīyam pibaṃti viharaṃti ca vārāḥ satatras śramamāṇa śvasiddhaḥ vikṛta rūpadhṛk satam vikṛta māyām tam siddha rūpam svam āgatam bujapada nāmā paṃcāyatana saṃsthitam oṃkāra īśvaram gṛhṇāt agṛhṇāt apūrva darśanam tvām tuṣpṛcchāmi aham ayobhavān kutas katham tu prāptaḥ si śaṃkesva gat samāgataḥ nahi dijānāsi kathyatām abhijñām svarga saṃsthānām apsarāṇām na saṃśayaḥ bā hmaṇā uvāca du sannibhām svarga kadācid rāhmaṇa ṛṣabha raṃbhām anāmayam pṛccha vacanāt mama sattama apakrāman divam kāṃtām vāyuḥ avyāhataḥ yathā caṃdralekhām yayā aṃbarāt apaśyat suka tīram bhām bhraṣṭa padmām iva śriyam pūrṇa caṃdra ābha vadanām madana aṃga mayīm iva gaja kuṃbha niśābhyām ca stanābhyām tu upaśobhitām pīna nivasati rāṃgane sa tvām pṛcchati suśroṇi yadi jānāsi kathyatām raṃbhā uvāca svam eva avasayaṃtūrṇam ābhiveśa anna locane vārāṇasīm anuprāptaḥ paṃcāyatanam āsthitaḥ dvijātinā āca saṃpṛṣṭaḥ śvireṇa punar āgataḥ sa tam prahasya provāca vārāṇasyām niketanaḥ katham brāhmaṇa dṛṣṭā asā tvayā āraṃbhā vara apsarāḥ kānisā avadate dṛṣṭā āpṛcchatā iva asura aṃganā raṃbhā dṛṣṭā tatas tubhyam prahasya vacanāt mama vyaśālinī siddhaḥ svargāt punar kāśyāṃsam āgataḥ te ciram viciṃtya mām āha na eva jānāmi kopi asau brāhmaṇā uvāca brāhmaṇaḥ asmi punar svargam yadā anāma mahā dyute svarge sukṛtinām vāse kila icchasi niyamam kuru vijñānam tatas svarge bhaviṣyasi iti uktvā asiddha māmaṃtrya namaskṛtvā atusa apsarāḥ naṃdanam vanam āgatya saṃgatā tatra ca apsarāḥ rudra āvāsam anuprāpya taṃ trāhmaṇam
