upahāraiḥ śubhaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ mahāgaṇapatiḥ bhavet yaḥ tu paryuṣitam yate naraḥ bhūtvā liṃgam eva arcayet punar mayā tava ākhyātam aniṃdite kṣaṇe manaḥ hara praśna kutūhalam ca iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitā āryā triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ aṣṭaṣaṣṭiḥ tu yā proktā śiva sya paramātmanaḥ maṃdara stham sukha āsīnam bahmā āpṛcchati śaṃkaram keṣu keṣu ca bhāveṣu draṣṭavya ūsi mayā prabho vārāṇasyām getu maheśvaram vyāsaḥ uvāca om om namaḥ śivāya kurukṣetre tu kāleśam prabhāseśa śibhūṣaṇam puṣkare tu ayaḥ gaṃdham viśvam ca vimaleśvare aṭṭahāse mahā nādam maru koṭe mahā utka ṭam śaṃku karṇe mahā tejaṃgo karṇe tu mahā balam rudrakoṭyām mahāyogī mahāliṃgam sthaleśvare avantyām tu mahākālam śarva madhyamakeśvare kedāredevam īśānam rudram ca eva himālaye suvarṇākṣe sahasrākṣam setu vṛṣabhadhvajam caṃḍaṃcaka bhijaṃgala galāṃḍe kapardinam kṛttivāsa itu varadam sūkṣma māghāḍika īśvare kālaṃjare nīlakaṃṭham śrīkaṃṭha maṃḍaleśvare vijayam ca eva kāśmīrejayam camaruka īśvare yamasya aṃge viduḥ sthāṇu kāpilaṃkaravīrake kāya avatāra ilaguḍim devikāyām umāpatim hariścaṃdra īśvaram ca eva pura caṃdra itu śaṃkaram jaṭiṃ kāleśvare vidyāt saumyam kukkuṭa keśvare jaleśvare triśūlam tu śrīśaila tripurāṃtakam lepane vai paśupa niṃdīta maṃgeśvare viduḥ gaṃgāsāgara iti amaram oṃkāram amarakaṃṭake karṇikāre gaṇādhyakṣa kailāsa tripurāṃtakam hemakūṭe virūpākṣam bhūrbhuvam gaṃdhamādane diḍīśvare analam prāhuḥ jvalalliṃgam sthaleśvare bhūtaśvare gaṇādhyakṣam kairātam ca kirātake dānavānām vināśāya vārāham viṃdhya parvate gaṃgā āha vaṃ vaḍavāmukhe śreṣṭhikoṭīśvaram tīrthe viśiṣṭa ceṣṭa kāpathe aṣṭaṣaṣṭistu nāmā nitatradevasya ca āśrayāt mahātmanā yaḥ śuciḥ prayataḥ bhūtvā ubhe saṃdhye paṭhet naraḥ daśānām aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca āsīnam maṃdarasya agre nānā ratna vibhūṣite tatra naṃdīśvarāḥ devam vibhūrti paryapṛcchata naṃdīśvarā uvāca śṛṇu naṃdīśvara mattaḥ vibhūtiḥ yādṛśam ama ekāgra mānasaḥ bhūtvā niśāmaya samāhitaḥ agni prākāra koṭi sthaḥ āvatoḥ hana saṃśayaḥ carāmi pṛthivīm sarva amā samudram sura amuram tiṣṭhāmi catvara iṣu dhuva sthitaḥ parvata iṣu sadā hṛṣṭaḥ devyā saha vasāmi aham pradakṣiṇam sadā kuryāt go śa tasya phalam labhet gavām śata sahasrasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ caṃdraḥ asmi varuṇaḥ ca aham vasāmi pṛthivīm aham dinam kṣapā ca saṃdhyā ca saha iṃdriyāṇi iṃdriya artha iṣu kṣayam ca eva ahamā yam vṛttīnām vṛttiḥ eva aham jayaḥ ham sarva bhūtiṣu vināśa śvasurā daityāḥ pavanoḍhahanaḥ tathā māruta ūham jalam ca aham kṣipām iba lavat sadā aham sṛjāmi bhūtāni saṃkṣipāmi yuge yuge yoni śata sahasreṣu bhrāmyata iti ātma līlayā mayā ate nihatāḥ daityāḥ tāraka ādyāḥ mahā balāḥ yeṣām niḥśvāsa vātena trayaḥ lokāḥ prakaṃpitāḥ sarva bhūta kṣayam ti evam kṛtavān na atra saṃśayaḥ sarva bhūteṣu vai muditaḥ sadā itihāsa purāṇa iṣu vede m natam deśam vijānāmi mayā śūnyam hi yat bhavet bhaktānām sarva bhūtānām yat camām śaraṇa āgatāḥ an anya mānasaḥ bhūtvā yaḥ mām pūjayate naraḥ saṃtuṣṭā uham pradāsyāmi gāṇapatyam su durlabham vasāmi aham puṣpiteṣu vṛkṣeṣu ca latāsu ca naṃdikeśvara nārīṇām sthita uham rūpa yauvane samaṃjīvaḥ ca dāsa śva sarveṣām niyamaiḥ saha sarva tīrtha abhigamanam kṛtam bhavati bhārata mahātmā asa jana śreṣṭhaḥ jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ bhaktānām ityādi sārdham eka anvayi jīvaḥ svāmī sukha āsīnā yathāśāṃti krīḍate ca yathāsukham prāpnuvanti śubhān loka antaiḥ vai karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ karī pakṣi poṣakāḥ mad prapanna aśva kravyādāḥ sarpa daṃśa upajīvanaḥ tat vākyam śrutvā ānaṃdī gaṇādhipaḥ pratyuvāca śubham vākyam yathāpūja yathāvidhi sidhyaṃti mānavāḥ mānavāḥ teṣu tatva iṣu tulya karma vaśa anugāḥ tāvat bhamaṃti saṃsāre yāvat dhyānam na viṃdati asurāḥ ca eva deva aśvaka payaḥ pitaraḥ tathā yathā brahma ādayaḥ om devāḥ dīpyate dhyāna tejasā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ yā varṇa saṃkarāḥ cāṃḍāla aśva antyaja aśva sarve te pāpa karmaṇaḥ te caram ti śubhān lokān dhyānam dahati kilbiṣam sarva pāpeṣu saktāyeta ica siddhyam dhyāna yoga vidhitsam mokṣa dvāra vidhi śṛṇu agamyā gāmī brahmanaḥ surā paḥ gurutalpa gaḥ śatam śakaṭa bhārāṇām jaṃtūnām yena hiṃsitam tad pāpam harate dhyānī kāṣṭha rāśim iva analaḥ kumārī dūṣaṇam kṛtvā mātaṃgī gamanam tathā abhakṣya bhakṣaṇam kṛtvā apeyam pītam eva ca tat viśodhayate idhyānī dīpta agniḥ iva kāṃcanam tattva jñāna aṃtaram prāpya sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate pāpa karmaṇaḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ pītam kṛtvā iti anvayaḥ yadi mokṣam na gacchati bhoga vāsanāyāḥ satyāt iti bhāvaḥ brahma loke pi vā vāsaḥ viṣṇu loke yadṛcchayā soma sūrya agni deva iṃdra a viśeṣam sthānam āpnuyāt yama loke pivā vāsaḥ pū jyamānasya daivataiḥ yathā uktena vidhānena viśuddhena antarātmanā sadā evam dhyāna yuktasya śivam prāpnoti na anyathā adhītya caturaḥ vedān sāṃga upaniṣadaḥ dvijaḥ gulyasya kalām na arhati ṣoḍaśīm vinā deva varam dhyānam śauca ācāra sama nvitam na tat śakyam phalam prātum ṛtu koṭi śataiḥ api adhītya catur āve dān dhyāna yogam viśiṣyate yaḥ sahasram sahasrāṇām bhojayet vai dvijān tathā yaḥ sahasram sahasrāṇām bhojayet satya vādinām saṃkalpinām sahasreṇa strā takānām śatena ca gṛhasthānām sahasreṇa trahmacāri śatena ca sāṃkhya yoga viśuddhānām bhuṃjānaḥ yasya yoga vid pratigraheṇa mūḍha ātmā an vimucyeta kilviṣam punāti dhyā ninaḥ teṣām iti jñāna parigrahe yathā parvatam āsādya āśrayaṃti mṛgādhipāḥ tatva viśva vidaḥ yogam āśrayanti dvijottamāḥ viśva vid sarva karmāṇi tathā kṛtvā na lipyate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tat aham śrotum icchāmi kena maṃtreṇa dhyāyate dhyānam katividham deva pratigṛhṇaṃti tat tathā akṣara aśva katham deva rudra viṣṇu pitāmahāḥ naṃdi īśvarau vāca keśavaḥ ubhābhyām madhyatas rudraḥ tiṣṭhata iti ekavigrahāḥ ca janārdanaḥ trailokyam devadevasya rudra viṣṇu pitāmahāḥ anugraha artha lokānām bhaktānām anukaṃpayā ātma deham tridhā devaḥ sakaroti pṛthak pṛthak bhagavant śivaḥ na tān saṃkramate pāpam mriyate ced divam ga taḥ akāraḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ ukāraḥ ca pitāmahaḥ makāraḥ ca svayam rudraḥ vijñeyā dhyāna tatparaiḥ akāram ca tu adhas kṛtvā oṃkāram ca prayojayet ukāraṃcam akāraṃcam ātra yā saha yojayet makāram tu śanais rutvā yojayet trividham tathā oṃkāram hṛdaye kṛtvā dhyānam yuṃjīta yoga vid oṃkāram vaidikānām tu yoginām ca tathā eva ca oṃkāram dhyāyamānasya janma sūtram na vidyate akṣarāt akṣaram bhavet nigṛtya sarva iṃdriyāṇi dhyānam yuṃjīta yoga vid aṃguṣṭha mātram puruṣam hṛdi kṛtvā śivam prabhum lalāṭa madhye caṃdra ābham acyutam loka pāvanam avyayam sūkṣma bhāvam tam mūrdhni kṛtvā aśivam prabhum om iti brahmayuṃjī triguṇam ca eva tri sthānam dhyakṣaram tathā uccāryamāṇam api ced saṃyamya ātmānam ā tma vid prāṇāyāme ciram prāṇasaṃyamī a ca punar punar nimeṣa mātram api ced dhyānam yuṃjīta yoga vid oṃkāre prathamam yogam nityam dhyāyīta mānavaḥ kūrma ogāni iva saṃhatya iṃdriyāṇi sukhāni ca prakāśayet tat ātmānam nirvāte dīpa vat dudhaḥ oṃkāram dhyāyate dhīraḥ ūvi śuddhena antarātmanā dhārayitvā yathāśaktyā tatas pratyāharet punar prāṇāyāmaiḥ vaśam ru tvām anaśva sthiram eva ca akāra śvaukāra śvamakāraḥ ca eva te trayaḥ ekaikaśas trayaḥ devāḥ viṣṇu rudra api tāmahāḥ naṃdīśvaram pariṣvajyat dṛṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ tapodhanaḥ śrutvā sthāneṣu ca yathātatham iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām naṃdīśvarayogākhyānam nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca prāṇāyāmam yathādhyānam pratyāhāram ca dhāraṇām teṣām krama viśeṣeṇa yogānām lakṣaṇam param pravakṣyāmi yathātattvam svayam rudreṇa bhāṣitam prāṇāyāmaḥ tathā ca api prāṇasyāyāmaḥ ucyate prāṇa apāna nirodhaiḥ tu maṃtraiḥ mātrāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ iti eṣa vividhaḥ proktaḥ prāṇāyāmasya lakṣaṇaḥ go vane jāyate yogam niviśamānaḥ tu na doṣam prāpnuyāt kvacid kāla aṃtara vaśāt yogāt abhīkṣṇam parimardanāt paricī yamāna yogasya tathā jāyeta mārutaḥ vaśi tvam ca tathā ca api gacchate yogam āsthitaḥ yathā siṃhaḥ mṭa go vāpī nīyamānaḥ vyavasthitaḥ abhayam ca manuṣyāṇām mṭagebhyaḥ saṃpravartate mārutaḥ yoginaḥ vaśyaḥ bhavati iti bhāvaḥ vyavasthitaḥ vaṃśe sthitaḥ bhavati iti śeṣaḥ viṣaya aṃtaram bhāvaḥ sīvanyāḥ vṛṣaṇa madhya ga rekhāyāḥ tathā a paricīyamānaḥ śarīra kilbiṣam dehat prāṇāyāmena yuktasya viprasya niyata ātmanaḥ sarva doṣāḥ praṇaśyaṃti sattva sthaḥ ca eva jāyate tīrthāni yāni paṭhyaṃte niyamāni tratāni ca prāṇāyāmaiḥ da het doṣān dhāraṇābhiḥ sva kilbiṣam pratyāhāreṇa viṣayān dhyānena anaśvarān guṇān tasmāt yuktaḥ sadā yogī prāṇāyāḥ mām samācaret atas param pravakṣyāmi prāṇāyāmasya lakṣaṇam āsanam svastikam kuryāt padyam bhadrāsanam tathā sama jānum eka pāda pāṇya uttānam ca saṃsthitaḥ tya caraṇau ubhau jānṛ varaṃtare vipra kṛtvā pāda tale aṃguṣṭhau api gṛhṇīyāt hastābhyām vyutkrameṇa tu pārśvayoḥ kṣiṣet pārśva pāda ca pāṇibhyām dṛḍha badhvā su niśvalaḥ saṃvṛta āsyaḥ umīlita akṣa aupaviṣṭa śva vāgyataḥ pāṇibhyām dapaṇam rakṣet tathā śephena nityaśas kiṃcid u saṃspṛśet jivhām na cālayet kvāpi pāṣāṇa eva niśvalaḥ sthiraḥ yogī saṃyuktaḥ su samāhitaḥ iṃdriyāṇi iṃdriya arthaḥ ca manaḥ paṃcama vāyavaḥ nirudhyase ma bhāvena kūrma ūgāni iva sarvaśas nivṛtti viṣayāṇām tu pratyāhāram upakramet tathā dvādaśa mātraḥ tu prāṇāyāmaḥ vidhīyate dhāraṇā dvādaśāyām ā īsevet ca dhāraṇātyayam daśa dvādaśa viṃśatyā catu viṃśati dhāraṇāḥ dhāraṇā ādhārayet yogī nityam adhyātma citakaḥ paśyate paramātmānam divyam evam kutas janiḥ dhārayitvā a yathāśaktyā aśanaiḥ pratyāharet punar jitvā a jitvā aśanaiḥ bhūyas ārabhet ca sadā muniḥ vivardhayati saṃmūḍham tasmāt eva jitā amahī prāṇāyāmasya saṃrodhāt dhārayet ca api yat vāyuṃdhāraṇām iti nirdiśet nivatta viṣayāṇām tu pratyāhāram na saṃśayaḥ sarveṣām samavāyena siddhiḥ syāt yoga lakṣaṇā dhyāna yuktāḥ tu paśyaṃti ātmānam jala caṃdra vat tathā a saṃdarśanam prāpte kṣema prāpti vinirdiśet deśa kāla videśaḥ tam vijñeyam tattva lakṣaṇam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām yo gavidhiḥ nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca sukha upaviṣṭam āsīnam mahādevam svayaṃbhuvam papraccha muni śārdūlaḥ durvāsāḥ tu mahā muniḥ bhagavaṃtam bhava udvignā edam āha ruta aṃjaliḥ bhagavan kena mucyate narāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva tathā vibho śvapāka mleccha mātaṃgāḥ śūkarāḥ pakṣi ghātakāḥ pāpa āśrayāḥ lolupāḥ ca havirdhakāḥ kanyānām dūṣakāḥ ca eva kula ghnāḥ strī napuṃsakāḥ mātṛtyāgī piṭatyāgī rāja ghnāḥ ca eva ye narāḥ para dra vya apahārīca yuddhe ca api parāṅmukhāḥ aśaktau aṅkuśaḥ ca eva śakti āvṛtti bhuja śvaye cāṃḍālāḥ matsya vaddhāśva agamyāgama neratāḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ sarva pāpeṣu ye narāḥ gacchan tena katham tāta pāpiṣṭhām gatim eva ca brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva tathā apare śvapāka amleccha mātaṃgāya ica anye pāpa karmiṇaḥ evam te dhyāninaḥ viprāḥ date pāpa kaṃkṣaṇāt pitṛ patnī bhrātṛ patnīm bhagi nīm gāvam eva ca dhyāninām śuddha buddhīnām dhyānena vidita ātmanām dhyānam ciṃtayamānasya ekacittena dhyāninaḥ ekena dhyāna yogena tat pāpam nirdahet kṣaṇāt pitṛ patnīm bhrātṛ patnīm bhaginīṃgāva me vaca saṃśayaḥ dhyāna hīnaḥ yaḥ tu nityam dṛḍha yuktaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ agni lokam vā yu lokam iṃdra lokam prajāpatiḥ viṣṇu loka aṃtaram gatvā brahma lokāt parām gatim iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām catustriṃśaḥ adhyā yaḥ durvāsāḥ uvāca kiṃca dhyānam sura śreṣṭha kaśva dhyātā ca nityaśas etat icchāmi aham śrotum tvad prasādāḥ dravīhi me aham vakṣyāmi tat sarva śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ mama oṃkāram paramam dhyānam yogam yuṃjīta yoga vid upaviśya āsanam tatra soma maṃḍalakam tathā padma maṃḍalakam ca eva svasti kaṃsam udāhṛtam rudra poṭhaṃcavacaṃcavajjadaṃḍoṃ nnataṃ tathā iti ete āsanāḥ proktāḥ nānā rūpa guṇa anvitāḥ eteṣām ekam āsthāya āsanam tu vicakṣaṇaḥ patiḥ bhūtvā rudra ādi lokān gacchati iti arthaḥ iti catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om namaḥ śivāya paṃcatriṃśattame adhyāye ladhu āhāra ujita krodha ekānte ca nirāmayaḥ śiṣṭa saṃsargava jitve darśana abhyāgamam tathā ciṃtaya īḍya āninaḥ nityam śāstra dṛṣṭe na karmaṇā ekāgra mānasaḥ bhūtvā utpattim pralayam tathā yuṃjīta sva śarīrasya yum jāna ūna ca hiṃsakaḥ yathā hi aham śarīrasya śukra śoṇita saṃbhavaḥ kim asmākam śarīra arthe anitye ca eva śarīrake majjā medas asthi saṃpūrṇa śirā jālena saṃvṛte śleṣma mūtra purīṣe pudurgaṃdha janma saṃbhave mamatvam hi śarīra ke prāṇāḥ tu rudra avijñeyāḥ avimuktam param smṛtam hita artham jaṃtuṣu āṃtaram śṛṇuyāt yogam yogaviyam varam sadā śrotram tvac cakṣuṣī jivhā nāsikā ca iti paṃcamī pṛthivī apaḥ tathā tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśa paṃcamāḥ mahābhūtāni kartavyam jñāna artha jñānam eva ca avyaktam parisaṃkhyātum prāṇāyāmaḥ tu dhāraṇā prāṇāyāmaiḥ vaśaṃkṛtvā sarvām iṃdriya vāhinīm tatas yuṃjīta medhāvī prāṇam cama nasā muniḥ pṛthak bhāvana tattvānām paśu ākuṃjīta mūrdhani eka tvam prāṇa manasaḥ riṃdriyāṇām samanvitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃ hitāyām durvāsa upanipad nāma paṃcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ātmanā a manasā iti paṃcatriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ prāṇa upānaḥ samānaḥ udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca tān hitvā vāyavaḥ paṃca dhārayaṃti ātmanā ātmani pāde ca eva ūru jaṃghā suśile vṛṣaṇayoḥ tathā pāyu upastha kaṭī vā avhoḥ hṛdaye pārśvayoḥ tathā vipule madhye pṛṣṭhe ca atha lalāṭayoḥ nābhi madhye śarīrasya viditam sūrya maṃḍalam jvālā mālā sahasā aiḥ tu āpyamāna ipu tejasā soma maṃḍalam adhyetu paramātmā abhitiṣṭhati asthi snāyu śirā māṃsa varjita a duḥkha varjitaḥ naca śyāmaḥ naca rakta una kṛṣṇaḥ naca pāṃḍuraḥ nāpiṃgala ūnapiṃgaḥ ca lohitona naśābalaḥ āditya varṇa puruṣam satam vidyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ īśvaraḥ ca bhavaḥ ca eva cityaḥ kartā asa kīrtyate śuddha sphaṭika varṇa ābhaḥ dṛśyate na ca cakṣuṣā krīḍā artha sṛjate lokān khyāti arthe ca maheśvaraḥ lokeṣu krīḍate nityam vālaḥ krīḍanakaiḥ iva thā patram sarva vyāptam hi taṃtubhiḥ jagat kṛtsram hitiṣṭhati sūrya iraśmiḥ yayā atyeṣa sarva tejāṃsi dhāraya n evam tena tathā vyānam śarīram paramātmanā paramātmā iti vijñeyaḥ jñāna abhyāsena bho dvija abhyāsāt paśyate sarvam paramā ātmānam ātmani imam yoga vidhiḥ utvā śṭaṇu tattvam manīṣiṇaḥ daśa prāṇa vahā nāḍyaḥ dehi deha iṣu saṃsthitāḥ catasraḥ vastu vijñeyāt decanā āḍhyā auca pārśvayoḥ ūrdhvam tu caturaḥ jñeyāḥ nāḍyaḥ tu parikīrtitāḥ nāḍīnām tu sahasrāṇi dvāsaptatiḥ iti padma saṃkāśa saṃsthānam hṛdayam tatra dṛśyate sūkṣmaḥ hi puruṣaḥ jñeyaḥ parātmā hṛdisaṃsthitaḥ śuddha sphaṭika varṇa ābham nirguṇam śā tvam savaga iṣu sarva gāmī tīrtha sraṣṭā dhātā ca prayuktavān prasūtaḥ pra thita abhāvānām traṣṭā āhartā aprasavitā adharma utsukaḥ tat eva agniḥ tat ādityaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ durvāsāḥ uvāca jñāpayāmi punar deva prasādam kuru śam kara kīdṛśaḥ tha bhavet dehe ṣaṣ aṃgaḥ yogaḥ ucyate prāṇāyāmaḥ tathā dhyānam dhāraṇā yogaḥ ucyate prāṇasya grahaṇam nityam prāṇāyāmaḥ saḥ ucyate oṃkāram manasā adhyāyet ekāgre manasā a smaran dhyānena tu sadā yogī dhyāna saṃvitta tā paraḥ sarveṣām idriyāṇām tu viṣayāṇām tathā eva ca pratipacya aharam kṛtvā a pratyāhāraḥ saḥ ucyate daśānām iṃdriyāṇām tu oṃkāra prīta mānasaḥ paṃcamam brahmacarya caitya iti ete niyamāḥ smṛtāḥ akrodhaḥ guru śuśrūṣā śaucam saṃtoṣam ṛ ya vat ete tu niyamāḥ paṃca vijñeyāḥ brahma vādiṣu ṣaṣ aṃgaḥ yogaḥ iti eṣa śuddhe vijñānā ucyate sa gacchet paramam sthānam śāśvatam dam avyayam ati śūnyam tu yasya arthe śarīram kīrtitam budhaiḥ sa śarīraḥ saḥ ucyate jñānam niraṃjanam ca eva avyaktam triguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ draṣṭā asaṣṭā casapitā amantā boddhā tathā eva ca puruṣam śāśvatam sūkṣmam draṣṭavyam dhyāna cakṣuṣā avyaktam triguṇam bhadrapuruṣa śvātra śāśvataḥ paṃcaviṃśatī tu vijñeyam īśam īśāḥ nam avyayam saṃbhūtim ca vināśam ca bhāva abhāvau tathā eva ca yaḥ tu vetti naraḥ prājñaḥ sarve draṣṭā aṣṭaviṃśakaḥ paṃcaviṃśaka tattvāni jñāyaṃte tu sadā naraiḥ paṃcaviśat tadā jñeyam īśānam avyayam param puruṣaḥ saṃca ditvā ca jñātvā ca sa gacchet paramām gatim saḥ evam paṃcaviṃśatikaḥ ṣaḍūiṃśakaḥ tathā eva ca ūnaviṃśatikam vidyāt tatva jñāna artha ciṃtakaḥ viṃśakam tu tat ājñātvā amṛta tvāya kalpate caturviṃśa gṛhaṃyogaḥ eṣa vai paṃcaviṃśakaḥ ṣaṣ śitiḥ tathā ājñe yā adhyakṣaḥ saptaviṃśakaḥ aṣṭaviṃśakaḥ puruṣaḥ triṃśat puruṣa lokadhṛk yam viditvā na śocaṃti tam śivam kathayāmi te om kāram paramam devam paṃ ca āyatana vāsinam durvāsāḥ uvāca katham jñeyam hi bhagavat mātra akṣara vivarjitam śṛṇuvi śarīram hita da brahma yat jñātvā a mucyate yatiḥ prathamā vai dvitīyā ca vijñeyā akṣara mālinī tṛtīyā animiṣā ca eva vijñeyā yoga citakaiḥ pipīḍitā ardha mātrā vai vijñeyā aguṇa varjitā ca eva ca eva akāraḥ uvaidyu tāca eva aukāra ukṣara gāminī makāraḥ nimiṣa anāma praśāṃtaṃtupipīḍitā kāraḥ tu umā ajñeya apraśāṃtam śāśvatam dhruvam om samudāharet vijñāna ākhyāta da ajñeya anityam akṣara gā sūtra nidarśanaiḥ iṣukāraḥ iva āsaktaḥ yathā agnim na tu paśyati tādṛśam bhāvayet rahmata dāviṃdati tatparam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām durvāsa upaniṣatsu saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ idam śarīram vipra indra sarva deva mayam śṛṇu viṣṇuḥ tu pāde vijñeyaḥ jaṃghayoḥ marutaḥ tathā jānubhyām aśvinau jñeyau ūrubhyām varuṇaḥ tathā om namaḥ śivāya sarva deva mayam vai aṃte samudrā vipra iṃdra udare paṃca deva tāḥ romakūpe dharmaḥ eva mūrdhya ādityaḥ na saṃśayaḥ saṃdhi sama ṛṣayaḥ jñeyāḥ cakṣubhyam sūryaḥ eva ca śrotrāṇi ca diśaḥ sarvā a vijñeyā a brahma vādibhiḥ nu vostu parvata ajñeyā lalāṭe vasavaḥ tathā śivaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ vijñeyaḥ nityam eva pratiṣṭhitaḥ aparāṃteyamaḥ ca eva tathā vedhāḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ pārśvayoḥ śubhe prāṇagatiḥ kaṃṭhe bhavaṃti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ etat jñātvā ca paramām gatim durvāsāḥ uvāca ete proktāḥ śarīrasya adevatāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tathā prāṇa āhutim katham bhaṃte vṛṣabhadhvaja mahādevaḥ uvāca prāṇa upānaḥ samāna śvaḥ udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca iti ete vāyavaḥ paṃca śarīra ica pratiṣṭhitāḥ sāvitrī caturaḥ vedāḥ sa paḍaṃga padakramāḥ oṣadhi aśva vanaspatyaḥ soma bhāskara mārutāḥ tena annena tu tṛpyaṃti yat prāṇe juvati dvijāḥ tena nāgāḥ samudra aśva saritaḥ sāgarāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ pitaraḥ ca eva sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ samāne juhute yaḥ tu tṛtīyām āhutim dijaḥ aśvinau marutaḥ viṣṇuḥ varuṇaḥ ca yamaḥ tathā prajāpatiḥ kubera śva sarve deva gaṇāḥ tathā tena aham cabhavaḥ bhaunaṃdī gaṇeśvaraḥ umā brahma api vipra iṃdra manaḥprāṇāḥ tathā eva ca vyāne vai juhuta iyān tu paṃcamī mā āhutim dvi jaḥ sapta loka aśva brahmāṃḍāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ bhavaḥ rudraḥ om namaḥ śivāya ū evam tu satatam viprāḥ juhute praṇave nave lipyate brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ yat iva a paṭhet veda aham etam puruṣam mahāṃtam āditya varṇa tamasaḥ parastāt viṣam hālāhalam pītvā anadhruvam mṛtyum āpnuyāt etam evam idam jñātvā amṛta tvam avāpnuyāt iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām durvāsa upaniṣatsu aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca yat tvayā uktam bhagavatā asāṃkhya yoga viśārada yoga nāḍīm imān tra śrotum icchāmi tat vratam praṇamya śirasā devam akṣayam bhuvana īśvaram kātyāyanīm namaskṛtvā rudra patnīm viśeṣataḥ pārameṣṭhyam idam jñānam nāḍī saṃcāra saṃsthitam viśvamūrtiḥ yadā śrīmān dehasyaḥ anantā raśmayaḥ tasya jagat deha āśritāḥ tathā yoga nāḍīḥ pravakṣyāmi thṛdaya sthānam ā śritāḥ pūrva dakṣiṇa paśu ārddha auttarām mūrtim āśritāḥ adhastāt deva nāḍyaḥ tu tāsām varṇān nibodha me pīta lohita kṛṣṇa aśrvaḥ uttarāḥ pāṃḍu piṃgalāḥ pūrvāḥ śvetāḥ tathā nāḍyaḥ dakṣiṇāḥ kṛṣṇa piṃgalāḥ tu kṛṣṇā nāḍyaḥ tu coditāḥ saṃsthāna saṃśritāḥ śatam eka uttaram nāḍīm upāsate ca yoginaḥ sarva aśvatāḥ samutsṛjya brahma nābhi nāḍībhiḥ krīḍā moha visarjanam ṣaṇṇavatyaḥ sahasrāṇi nāḍīnām hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ paṃca prāṇa ādyāḥ parikī titāḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ sthitāḥ nāḍyaḥ tāsām paṃca jalāḥ iti paścima uttara nāḍyoḥ tu udānam ca uttarāṇi ca adhastāyāḥ samāśritāḥ dviguṇam tu praviṣṭāḥ tu hṛdaya anaṃtaraṃ tatāḥ etat nāḍī pramāṇam tu viśvam yatra pratiṣṭhitam u ktāḥ caturbhiḥ saṃyuktam aṇoḥ aṇīyānāḍī iti adhastāt sa tu viśvakarmaṇā tena eva nāḍhī antara saṃcareṇa śuddhasya nāḍi di mūrdhni lakṣayet parāpara jñāna nidhāna bhūtāḥ paṃca indriyāḥ saṃyuktā paṃca karmabhiḥ iṃdriyaiḥ sarve te hṛdi saṃvaddha āyogena hṛdi pādayoḥ nāḍī sahasrāṇām guṇān eva catuṣṭayam tāḥ ca mūtra vahā nāḍī ekī bhūtātu miśritā retasā asaṃprasūyam te mūtram ca eva tathā eva ca brahmanāḍīmukheyasya manasā athṛdicā īśvaram trīṇi ca asthi sahasrāṇi varṇa sṛṣṭiḥ prakīrtitā snāyūnām sahasrāṇi param saṃvatsaram smṛtam sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataraḥ bhāvaḥ yam viditvā an ayujyate soma sūrya aṃśubhiḥ pītam padmam ca eva sa viṃdati tatra upari nayanti eva yoginām mūrdhniśāyinām jñānena vijñāya nivṛtta kalmaṣāḥ abhitvā sthitim trahma vidaḥ prayām ti sanatkumāreṇa idam tu nāḍī saṃcāra sūcitam yoga śāstram idam puṇyam mokṣa śāstram su niśvitam brahma ādyaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ gatam yoga śāstram viniścitam puṇyāt puṇyataraṃsi etat pavi pāpa nāśanam pramucyate nāḍī madhya gatam viśvam śudhyate pitṛ mātṛ jam go mūtram saptame pāpam dahate ca aṣṭame tathā tena apiśraṅgyā nāḍī mūrdhni adhastāt vi niḥsṛtā maṃtavyaḥ yena viśvam pūrvāḥ ta iti aditi sthati tad manaḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ tāvat saṃcita yet ugram yāvatā a tad mataḥ mataḥ nāḍī sūkṣmeṇa mārgeṇa aurdhvayā ati uttarāyaṇam tābhyām adhastāt yat kāryam tat gatam tasya saṃsmṛtam vidhānam ca eva nāḍyāḥ tu śarīreyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ snāyuḥ trīṇi sahasrāṇi sarvāḥ tā nābhi jāḥ smṛtāḥ ṣaṇṇavatyaḥ saha khāṇiśirāṇām hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ te vaiśivāni mārgāṇi viśvaḥ yatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ sarva nāḍīḥ parityajya brahmanāḍīm samāśrayet durgāṇi tārayet nauḥ iva arṇavam eka nāḍī nirālam vātālu madhye śiraḥ gatā sā nāḍī yoga yuktānām mokṣa dāsa ādi vaṃga tā śukra majjā vasā medaḥ kapham pittam śarīrayoḥ śirāṃsi tasya srotāṃsi ekaikam śukra raṃdhrayoḥ dhūta pāpa ādi vayāṃti mūrdhnibhitvātam īśvaram dhyāyaḥ devaiḥ sa divyaiḥ ṛṣayaḥ samagrāḥ brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca maheśvaraḥ ca vāyuḥ yamaḥ agniḥ varuṇaḥ śaśāṃkaḥ sarvān nirīkṣya eva divam prayāṃti guṇaiḥ tuvaṃtaḥ api mukha ābhimukhyaiḥ dhyāyaṃti gāyaṃti ca pūjayaṃti iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tathā ca oṃkāra devasya mahābhāgyam vadasva me śṛṇu vyāsa paraṃgutyam rahasyam yogam uttamam param padam tat aham saṃpravakṣyāmi iyat mayā tu śrutam purā pārvatyā asahasam vādam devadevasya śūlinaḥ tīrtha upaniṣadam puṇyam mokṣa dam sarva dehinām kathayāmāsa deveśaḥ rahasyam jñānam uttamam sva puram citayāmāsa saḥ u vimukta gaṇādhipaḥ vārāṇasīm vinā deva ūna ratim prāpya kutracid uvāca vākyam vara daḥ jagannātha pinākadhṛk yena kāryeṇa suśro śṛṇu siddhāṃtānām ca sarveṣām smṛtīnām ca eva suṃdari caturdaśānām bhuvanānām yaśva sāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ātma jñānam paraṃgulyam yat jñātvā mokṣam aśnute saḥ yaḥ devī sthitaḥ sākṣāt drāvāse svayam prabhuḥ tridhā sthānam tri bhoktāram tri bhojyam ca tathā aparam yatayā uśva param vidyāt sijyam te t bhāvam param āsthitāḥ om kāram paramam brahma paramam ca viduḥ budhāḥ paṃca brahma samāyuktam paṃca āyatana vāsinām ye rakṣyaṃti śivam tatra te drakṣyaṃti paraṃpadam brāhmaṇāḥ tava muṃcati veda vedāṃga pāragāḥ yatayaḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ ye ca anye veda saṃsthitāḥ nānā liṃga dhara a vipra veda śāstra parāyaṇāḥ gṛhasthāḥ ca eva yatayaḥ tasmāt tīrthaupāsa kāḥ ekadaṃḍāḥ tridaṃḍāḥ ca ye śaivāḥ pāśupata ayeca kapāla vrata cāriṇaḥ upāsate camām nityam mūkam ca vratam āsthitāḥ karma bhedena teṣām tu sarveṣām āsthitā iti aham vibhajāmi param sthānam tat mokṣam paramam padam śmaśānam taṃtra nityam sannihitā devaḥ jaṃtūnām ca eva tārakaḥ tasyām puryāḥ vyavasthānāt prakhyātā amevimuktatā avyakta liṃgam bhitvā eva tathā saṃsāra bhīrubhiḥ tatra viśveśvaram dṛṣṭvā saṃsāre na patet punar viśveśvaram cakāram etad sāram prakīrtayet siddhakṣetram tapaḥkṣetram yathā vārāṇasī mune sparśana adarśanāt tasya kṛtārthā mānavā bhuvi tāraṇam sarva jaṃtūnām nānā pāpasya nāśanam saṃdhyā upāsitā bhavati sakṛtvā daśa māsakṛt stutā patiḥ vārāṇasyām mahā puṇyam kasya vāsaḥ na rocate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ pūrṇabhadra sutaḥ śrīmān āsīt yakṣa pratāpavān tadā āsīta namaskāraḥ tad bhaktasya parāyaṇaḥ āsīnaḥ ca śayānaḥ ca gacchanti ṣṭhan anuvrajan bhuṃjāna uvā apidhāvan arūpam eva anuciṃtayan tasya evam yukta manasaḥ pūrṇabhadraḥ pitā bravīt nahi yakṣa kulīnānām evam vṛttiḥ bhavet suta vai svabhāvāt krūra cetasaḥ ka vyādāḥ ca eva kiṃtatra hiṃsā śīlāḥ ca putraka na eva kārya ānata īvṛtiḥ evam dṛṣṭvā mahātmanām om namaḥ śivāya daṃḍapāṇiḥ abhūt deva pra vam eva asati ananya bhāvena śaraṇam gacchati saḥ bhāva pradhānā paṃcamī svayaṃbhuvā yathā dṛṣṭvā tyaktavān mahite bhavet āśrama aṃtara jam karma na kuryāt gṛhiṇaḥ tatas deva tvam nodhi mārgeṣu mānuṣyam jātim eva ca na mayā vihitam tasya karma tat na atra saṃśayaḥ iti evam uktvā putraṃtu pūrṇabhadraḥ pratāpavān vārāṇasīṃsam āsādya tapaḥ tepe mahā ātmavān śeṣaḥ śuṣka kāṣṭha upala upamaḥ tyaktvā gotra kṛtām vṛttim tathā a jāti kṛtāḥ tatas śubhe ārādhayan ye yogi īśam gokarṇa devam īśvaram saṃniyamya iṃdriya grāmam vā atiṣṭhata niścalaḥ sahasram ekam varṣāṇām divyam saṃnyativarttata vālmīkena samākrāṃtaḥ bhakṣyamāṇaḥ pipīlakaiḥ rājasūcī mukhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ vidhyamānaḥ tathā eva ca vaikuṃda śaṃkheṃ bhaḥ etasmin antare devī vijñāpayati śaṃkaram udyānam punar evā idam draṣṭum icchā mita vara iti vijñāpitaḥ devaḥ pārvatyā parameśvaraḥ śarvaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame nirjagāma ca deve śaḥ pārvatyāḥ saha śaṃkaraḥ udyānam darśayāmāsa devyāḥ devaḥ pinākadhṛk vijñāṣayati vyajijñapat prajvāla nānā druma gulma śobhitam latā pratāna avanatam manoramam virūḍha puṣpaiḥ paritas sugaṃdhitam su puṣpitaiḥ kam aśoka puṃnāga vanaiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ dvi repha mālā ākula saṃcayaiḥ kvacid kvacid praphulla aṃbuja reṇu bhūṣitaiḥ vihaṃgamaiḥ śvāru phala praṇādibhiḥ kvacid ca kāraṃḍa varāḥ vana āditam kvacid ca matta ali kula ākulīkṛtam mahā kalābhiḥ śraṃmara aṃganābhiḥ niṣevitam cāru sugaṃdhi puṣpitam pragīta vidyādhara cāraṇaṃca pravṛtta nṛtya anugata apsaraḥ gaṇam prahṛṣṭa nā nāvidha pakṣi sevitam pramatta hārīta kula upamoditam mṭaga iṃdra nānā ākula mānasaiḥ kvacid gajaiḥ kvacid daddha kadaṃba kaṃmṭagaiḥ praphula nānāvidha cāru paṃkajaiḥ saraḥ taḍāgaiḥ upaśobhitam kvacid nibiḍa nicula nīlam nīlakaṃṭha abhivāsam mada mudita vihaṃga bāta nāda abhirāmam kusumita taru śākhā ālīna matta dvirephena iva kisalaya śākhā śobhitam prāṃta śākham kvacid ca cāru vīrudham kvacid latā āliṃgita cāru vakṣam kvacid viśāla alasa gāminībhiḥ niṣevitam kiṃpuruṣa aṃganābhiḥ pārāvata dhvani nikūjita cāru śṛṃgaiḥ akarṣaiḥ sita manohara cāru rūpaiḥ nīlaiḥ puṣpa stabaka tarala prāṃta śākhaiḥ aśokaiḥ matta ali trāta gīta śruti sukha janakaiḥ bhā sita antam manojñaiḥ haṃsānām pakṣa vāta pracalita kamala su accha vistīrṇa toyam toyānām tīra jāta pravikaca kadalī vāṭa nṛtyan mayūram māyūraiḥ pakṣa caṃdraiḥ kvacid api patitaiḥ aṃjitam kṣmā pradeśam deśe deśe mudita vilasat matta hārīta nṛtyam kṛṣṇābhiḥ kvacid api kiṃnara aṃganābhiḥ kṣīrābhiḥ sa madhupa pīta vṛkṣa khaṃḍam saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacid upa lipta karṇa puṣpaiḥ āvāsaiḥ parivata pādapam munīnām āśrāṃta utpala nicitaiḥ kvacid viśālaiḥ svīkartum sarala mahīruhaiḥ upetam phulla priyaṃgu taru maṃjari sakta bhṛṃgam bhṛṃga āvalī sarali tārdha kadaṃba puṣpam gulma aṃtara prasṛta tīra mṭa gī samūham vallī latā tanubhṛtām apavarga daṃtam caṃdra aṃśu jāla dhavalaiḥ tilakaiḥ manojñaiḥ siṃdūra kuṃkuṃma kusuṃbha nibhaiḥ aśākaiḥ cāmīkara pratisumaiḥ nava karṇikāraiḥ phulla araviṃda pada ci tra viśāla śākhaiḥ kvacid sakāśaiḥ śobhāṭyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ācita bhū talam puṃnāga iṣu dija gaṇa virutam rakta aśoka staba kata ralitam sakala bhuvana kartā āloka nāthaḥ tadānīm tuhina śikhara saṃvāsya ṛdha niṣṭhaiḥ gaṇeśaiḥ vividha taru viśālam matta dṛṣṭa anya puṣṭaiḥ upavana taru ramyam darśayāmā sa devyāḥ udyānam darśitam deva śobhayā aparayā ayutam a sadā vārāṇasī mama sarveṣām eva jaṃtūnām hetuḥ mokṣasya sarvadā asmi siddhāḥ sadā devi madīyam tratam āśritāḥ nānā liṃga dharāḥ nityam mama loka abhikāṃkṣiṇaḥ abhyasyaṃti param yogam yukta ātmānaḥ jita iṃdriyāḥ nānā vasa samākīrṇe haga rājite kamala utpala puṣpa ādyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte apsaraḥ gaṇa gaṃdharvaiḥ sadā saṃśobhite śubhe rocate me sadā vāsaḥ yena kāryeṇa tat śṛṇu yathāmokṣam iha āpnoti brahma ādayaḥ vijānaṃti ye ca siddhāḥ mumukṣavaḥ na atas priyataram kṣetram tasmāt me harate manaḥ mahā kṣetram idam tasmāt avimuktam iti smṛtam saṃha mattāḥ dṛṣṭa aśvā anya puṣṭāḥ kokilāḥ yatra devyāḥ devyai prayāgāt api tīrtha agryāt idam eva mahat smṛtam jaigīṣavyaḥ sata siddhi yogataḥ sa mahā tapāḥ māhātmyam tat vakti āmama bhāvanāt jaigīṣavyaḥ mahā śreṣṭhaḥ yoginām jñānam icchati dhyāyata iti atra mām nityam yogāt nirvāpyate bhṛśam kaivalyam paramam yā ti devānām api durlabham ātmanaḥ ca eva sāyujyam īpsitam sthānam eva ca kuveraḥ sa mahāyakṣaḥ tathā sarva arpita triyaḥ kṣetrasya vaṃdanā deva gaṇa īśa tvam avāpa ha parāśara sutaḥ yogī ṛṣiḥ vyāsaḥ mahā tapāḥ brahmā āca ṛṣibhiḥ sārddham viṣṇuḥ vāyuḥ divākaraḥ upāsane mahātmānaḥ sarveṣām iha suvrate siddhāḥ channa rūpa ama hā vratāḥ alaṃkāra purīm enām mad prasādāt avāpsyasi tena evam pūrvatas kṛtvā catur varṇa samākulām sphīta aṃjanapada ākīrṇā abhūtvā ca vasatim naraḥ tatas prabhṛti cārvagiyeyekṣetra nivāsinaḥ gṛhiṇa āliṃginaḥ vāpi mad bhakta amad parāyaṇāḥ mad prasāda āgamiṣyanti mo kṣam parama durlabham iha kṣetre mṭataḥ saḥ pi saṃsāre na punar viśet sattva stha avijita iṃdriyāḥ vibhāvitāḥ deha bhaṃgam samāsādya dhīmaṃtaḥ saṃga varjitāḥ gatāḥ eva param mokṣam prasādāt mama suvratāḥ janma aṃtara sahasreṣu yum jan yogī samāpnuyāt etat eva param jñānam etat eva param śivam vārāṇasī tu bhuvana traya sāra bhūtā masadāgiri rāja putri atra āgata a vividha duṣkṛta kāriṇaḥ api pāpa kṣaya addirajasaḥ pratibhāṃti martyāḥ yasmin ṭatāḥ tanubhṛtaḥ padam āpnuvaṃti mūrkha āgamena rahi tān ahi saṃśayaḥ utra tare devā devīm prāha giri indrajām dātum prasādam yakṣāya vara bhaktāya bhāvitam jagāma yakṣaḥ yatra āste kṛśaḥ dhamanisaṃtataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā praṇatam bhaktyā harikeśam vṛṣadhvajaḥ divyam cakṣuḥ adāt tasmai yena apaśyata śaṃkaram apaśyat sa gaṇam devam vṛṣa yuktam umāpatim sāmagryam ca śarīrasya tad jvaraḥ atas sa labdhvā tuvaram śarīreṇa akṣatena tu pādayoḥ praṇataḥ tasthauḥ hatvā śirasi ca aṃjalim uvāca atha tathā ca enam vara dosmi iti coditaḥ yadā ayena tvām iti śeṣaḥ udbhūma saṃbhramau karmaṇī iti ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om anna da tvam ca lokānām gāṇapatyam tathā akṣayam avimukta vane sthānam paśyeyam sarvadā yadā bhaviṣyasi gaṇādhyakṣaḥ vara daḥ sarva pūjitaḥ a jeya śvā api sarveṣām yoga aiśvarya samanvitaḥ anna daḥ ca api lokebhyaḥ kṣetrapālaḥ bhaviṣyasi tryakṣa śvadaṃḍa pāṇi śva mahā yogī tathā eva ca evam ca bhagavān tatra yakṣam kṛtvā gaṇeśvaram jagāma vāsadeva īśaḥ rudra āvāsam sureśvaraḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām daṃḍa pāṇi vara pradāne ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ paṃcāyatanam uttamam purākalpe dvijaśreṣṭha tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu carate tatra maṃḍūkī paṃcāyatanam uttamam paṃcatvam āgatā a brahman kālena kaṃtinā aṃjasā jāti sma ra tvam saṃprāptā rājñaḥ sumanasogṛhe yauvanam tu yadā yāta atadā rājā sa vismayaḥ dātu kāmaḥ tad dārā jāta yāca vinivāritaḥ vairāgyam manasā āgatvā vārāṇasyām upāgatā oṃkāram dṛṣṭavān devam paṃcāyatana vāsinam maṃḍukī ca api tatra eva siddhi ca evam upāgatā āsīt pratāpa mukuṭaḥ rājā a parama dhārmikaḥ kālena agacchata aśaśvat rājā aputram tam uktavān dāra saṃgrahaṇam putra tva yā kāryam ca śāśvatam mayā an aśakyate kartum tava ājñā paripālanam rājā uvāca mā nimajjīḥ kulam sahitam pituḥ ādeśam śrutvā nṛpa sutaḥ balī prāha saṃsmṛtya paurāṇīm saṃsārasya a vici tra tām śṛṇutā ata vaḥ comati aṃta tva vākyam sa hetukam mayā a janma sahasrāṇi jarā mṛtyu śatāni ca prāptāni dāra saṃyoga viyogāni ca sarvaśas tṛṇa gulma latā vallī sarīsṛpam mṛga dvijāḥ paśu strī puruṣāyā aniprāpta anigatayā umayā gaṇāḥ kiṃnara gaṃdharva bidyādhara mahoragāḥ yakṣa gutyaka rakṣāṃsi dānava apsarasaḥ tathā tatra īśvara īśvara tvam ca prāpnaṃta āta punar punar sṛṣṭaḥ tu bahuśas sṛṣṭau saṃhāre ca api saṃhṛtaḥ viḍaṃbanā hrā akṣaraḥ tu bhavet mṛtyuḥ asa raṃ brahma śāśvatam a tarkyamānau bhūtāni yojayetām asaṃśayam bhittvā aśarīram bhūtānām ahiṃsām prati padyate labdhvā āvāpṛthivīm sarvāṃsaha sthāvara jaṃgamām mā iva niśvinuyāt iti śeṣaḥ tathā ca abhimāna abhāvavataḥ vaiṣayika sukha abhāvāt viṣaya arjanam vyartham iti bhāvaḥ kāma ātmānam iti kāmena viṣaya icchayā akarmaṇā śārīreṇa nanudhyānena kurvati iti śeṣaḥ amṛtaḥ dravye tu mamatā yasya mṛtyoḥ vaśye savartate vīkṣāṃtarāṇām śatrūṇām svabhāvāya asi ame matiḥ kāma ātmānam praśaṃsaṃti loke kāma ātmanaḥ janāḥ tīrtha a niveda adhyayanam kācid asti pravartanā kecid tapa śva kāmena karmaṇā avāmṭata utsukaḥ tatas aham kāmaye nityam paṃcāyatanam īśvaram avimukte sthita devam om kāram paramam padam kathayāmi samāsena tīrtha māhātmyam u ttamam bhūdeva gaṃdharva mahoragāṇām vidyādharāṇām khaga kinnarāṇām jātaḥ asmi aham vai śyakule ivi śuddhe tatas mama abhūt acalā ca bhaktiḥ śarve śive śaṃkare tripura ghne vrata upavāsaiḥ vividhaiḥ stava aiśva saṃtoṣitaḥ śūla śita astra dhārī evam hi su mahat kālam bhramataḥ tīrtha kāraṇāt oṃkāram dṛṣṭavān tatra paṃca āyatana vāsinam rudra āvāsa kṛta sthānam devadevasya ca agratas rātrijāgaraṇam tatra vaiśākhe ca kṛtam mayā tat sarvam camayā dṛṣṭam deva gaṃdharva kiṃnaraiḥ tena eva karmaṇā ajātaḥ bhavataḥ uham gṛheśubhe tatra yāsyāmi aham śīghram racitaḥ yaḥ mayā aṃjaliḥ oṃkāra īśvara devasya prasādena mayā pitaḥ prādurbhūtam mahā jñānam durlabham yat suraiḥ api saṃsāre ca prapaśyāmi ātmānam prakṛteḥ param oṃkāram niṣkalam brahma paṃcāyatana vāsinam drakṣyāmi śaṃkaram devam yam dṛṣṭvā anaḥ udbhavaḥ punar rājā uvāca jātismara tvam saṃprāpyau dvigna mānasaḥ yaham saṃsāre ca sadā puṃsām vairāgyam jāyate punar priya apriyāṇi sarvāṇi nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkṛtiḥ tyakta karmāṇi sarvāṇi ātma śuddhāni dhārayet kṛtvā api kṣetra saṃnyāsam avimuktam upāsakāḥ śāṃta a dāṃtāḥ jita krodhāḥ titikṣā parama āyudhāḥ ātmani ātmānam ādhāya oṃkāra īśvara sarvagaṃ sarva bhūta iṣu ca ātmānam dviyāḥ sadbhāva bhāvitāḥ viśaṃti paramam deva moṃkāram paramam padam evam uktaḥ tadā rājā oṃkāram manasā a smaran rājyebhiḥ abhiṣecayāmāsa putram ca eva kanīyasam saṃsmaran pūrva caritam tatas nirvedam āgataḥ praṇamya manasā devam paṃcāyatana vāsinam oṃkāram paramam trahma vārāṇasyām upāgatam pradakṣiṇām prakurute oṃkāra devam īśvaram deva deva arādhayantau deveśam paṃcāyatanam īśvaram maṃdeva moṃkāram parameśvaram vyāsaḥ uvāca kīdṛśam ca vartanābhyām kṛrta deva sya śūlinaḥ yasya ca uccāra mātreṇa ātmā a saṃprakaṭībhavet rahasya yogam uttamam oṃkāra jam śiva padam nādim ajam avyayam svayaṃbhuvam anirdeśyam kāraṇam paramam vibhum paṃca daivatam oṃkāram māma kāma tvāt nirvāṇa mokṣaḥ eva nirbhayam nirmalam nityam nirapekṣam anāśrayam namaskṛtya mahādevam viśuddham jñāna nirmalam śivam sarva ātmakam sūkṣmam anādi paṃca daivatam ātma adhika upaviṣayam stutam ācāra varjitam śabda avakāśa rahitam bahma nirvāṇa kevalam śaṃkā viśeṣa nirmuktam vidyā patita mocanam niṣkramya ca ātmanā ātmānam prakaṭam jñāna dīpakam nitya avakāśa rahitam śabda a śabda ādi a gaḥ caram sakṛt vistīrṇa vipulam devadevam sura ātmakam anispaṃdam mahātmānam nirānaṃda avalokanam svabhāvam bhāvanā agra atyam bhāva atītam su lakṣaṇam vākya apavāda rahitam niṣprapaṃca ātmakam śivam jñāna jñeya avalokasya hetum parama kāraṇam anāhatam sarva gatam śabda ādi guṇa saṃbhavam śabdabrahma gatam śāṃtam śabda śabda antam mā āspadam anādim acyutam divyam pramāṇa atīta gocaram adhas śva ūrdhva gatam nityam jīva ākhyam hetu sam sthitam hṛd ādi dvādaśānta stham prāṇa apāna udaya aṣṭakam niṣkalaṃka ātmakam vibhum svara ādi vyaṃjana atītam varṇa ādi parivarjitam vācām avācya viṣayam oṃkārāt ūrdhva rūpiṇam niḥśabda niścalam saumya deha atītam parātparam bhūta avagāha rahitam niḥśabdam ekadhā āsthitam aciṃtyam paramam sūkṣmam paṃcataṃtra ādi saṃvṛtam aprameyam ananta akṣam asayam kāmarūpiṇam prabhavam sarva bhūtānām bīja aṃkura samudbhavam vyāpakam sarva kāma ākhyam akṣaram paramam mahat sthūla sūkṣma vibhāgasya vyakta avyaktam sanātanam mahābhūtam mahākāyam śivam nirvāṇa bhairavam śaraṇyam devam īśāna moṃkāram śiva rūpiṇam devadevam mahādevam kaṃṭaṣa dhvajam sadāśivam virūpākṣam śūla hastam jaṭā dharam vārāṇasyām sthitam deva moṃkāram paramam padam bhāva kam sarva jaṃtūnām namasyāmi namaḥ namaḥ vanhi bhāskara saṃkāśam sūrya koṭi sama prabham tu atra tu atra tadā ekadā oṃkāra nirdiṣṭa stotram śaṃbhoḥ paṭhiṣyati avimuktemahākṣetre sarvātman nā abhisaṃskṛtaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ upi ya divā paṭhet veda aham etam puruṣam mahāṃtam āditya varṇa tamasaḥ parastāt tam eva viditvā an abhavet mṛtyuḥ na anyaḥ paṃthāḥ vidyatehi janānām tadā ca oṃkāra devasya śakyam māhātmyam īritum māhātmyam oṃkāra hata eka deśam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām oṃkāreśvaravarṇanam nāma dvicatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca natṛbhim adhigacchāmi oṃkārasya kathāṃparām śṭaṇu vyāsa kathām divyām paurāṇīm veda saṃmitām śaṃbhogirimutā devī bhāryā kālī iti viśrutā a tyartha dayitā sādhvī śīla vṛtta guṇa anvitā sadā saṃdhyā pūrvā paścima aṃca oṃkāre saṃsthitaḥ haraḥ nṛtyamānāḥ sthitāḥ sarve gīta vāditra saṃvṛtāḥ śata varṣa sahasreṇa sveda bhūtāḥ gaṇāḥ tathā pra ta bhūtāḥ tathā devāt sṛṣṭān anṛtuḥ uttamam śva pade pade tam tādṛśam atho dṛṣṭvā gaurī vacanam abravīt kim virūpa akṣan nṛtyaḥ yaḥ mama vismaya kārakaḥ anekaiḥ bahuṣu sthānaiḥ dṛṣṭam nṛtyam mayā purā kailāsena eva saṃdṛṣṭam kadācid tu mayā purā kāraṇam katham yatu adya yadi anugraha bhāgaḥ asmin sthāne oṃkāra āyatane svam gulena mahā tmanā viśiṣṭam kāraṇam metra sthāne girisute śṛṇu sākṣikaḥ parikīrtitaḥ etat atra ayam trahma paṃcāsyam saṃsthitam prabhum paṃca paṃca sthi paṃca āyatana vāsinam tena nṛtyāmi aham devi parama ānaṃdam āsthitaḥ brahmāṃḍa udara varti ini tīrthāni giriśa udbhave teṣām atyadhikam sthānam paṃca āyatanam uttamam mama ca api adhikā aprītiḥ yena kāryeṇa tat śṛṇu saḥ yaḥ sthāne paredevi maṃtavyaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ pratyakṣam jñātavān bhadre puruṣasya catur bhujaḥ trinetram śūla hastam ca lalāṭa akṣam vṛṣadhvajam dra kṣyaṃti mānavāḥ pūrva paṃca āyatana saṃsthitāḥ śiva lokasya saṃcāram rahasyam sarva jaṃtūnām paṃcāyatanam uttamam narāṇām anya buddhīnām viṣaya ākrāṃta cetasām antar bhūtam tu saṃsthānam veda śāstra bahiṣkṛtāḥ śāṃta a dāṃta ajita krodhāḥ paṃcāyatana pūjayā sadbhāva bhāvitāḥ sarve drakṣyaṃti parameśvaram yaiḥ tu janma aṃtare devi purā ārādhitā iti aham sthānam avimuktam param padam brahmāṃḍa udara madhye cayāni tīrthāni suvrate vārāṇasyām gamiṣyaṃti vaiśākhasya caturdaśīm drakṣaṃti paramam devam paṃcāyatana vāsinam pūjayā a śama dama ādi sādhana saṃpannā bhavati iti āha om om namaḥ devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca eva rudrāḥ pāśupata āśvaye parivārya sthitāḥ sarve oṃkāra īśam tu suvrate yasmin akṣetre svayaṃbhū śru asthitaḥ pūrveṇa keśavaḥ rudrāṇām ca eva koṭiḥ tu kāśī purī eva saṃsthitā dhyāyamānā ca oṃkāra sthitā tasya eva dakṣiṇe vāmadevaḥ ca sāvarṇiḥ aghoraḥ kapilaḥ pare dhyāyamānāḥ tu oṃkāram paṃcāyatana vāsinam sapta koṭyaḥ tu maṃtrāṇām sarveṣām tapasā adhikaḥ evam madīyam śāśvatam śubham rakṣaṃti satatam paṃcāyatana vāsinam oṃkāra darśanāt eva gatim prāpnoti durlabhām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām oṃkāranirṇayaḥ nāma trayaścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ asmin sthāne purāvṛttam tadi ha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu rathaṃtare purā kalpe rājā āsīt puṣpavāhanaḥ nāmnā lokeṣu vikhyātaḥ tejasā sūrya sannibhaḥ tapasā tasya tuṣṭena devadevena śaṃbhunā kamalam kāṃcanam dattam yathā kāma gamam mune ca yatheṣṭam vicaran sadā kalpa ādau saptadvī peṣutasya puṣkara vāsinaḥ mucyate puṣpavāhanam iti āhuḥ tasmāt tam deva dānavāḥ patnī catasya a pratimāna rūpā nārī sahasraiḥ abhitas bhimānyā nāmnā acala avaṇyavatībabhūva sā a pārvatī ceṣṭatamā bhavasya tasya ātmajānām ayutam vabhūva dharma ātmanām agya dhanurdharāṇām saḥ api āgatam vīkṣya muni pravīram pracetasam vākyam idam babhāṣe kasmai mama adya pūjā jātā ca sarva viditā mama suṃdarī iyam bhāryā mā alpa tapasā eva su toṣitena dattam mā mā ambuja gṛhaṃcasu dhīra dhātrā yasmin praviṣṭam api koṭi śatam nṛpāṇām sa amātya kuṃjara sthauva dhanāvatānām muniḥ api avocata bhava aṃtaritām pṛthivīpate nanu niśamya ka thām abhūt anāvṛṣṭiḥ atīva raudrā kadācid āhāram aviṃdatā kṣudh pīḍitena bhramatā na kiṃcid āsāditam vanya phala ādi sadyas athā abhyapaśyat mahat aṃbuja āḍhyam sarovaram paṃka parīta rodhaḥ tad mūlya lābhāya puram sa mastam bhrāṃtam tadā aśeṣam abhūt tadānīm upaviṣṭaḥ tvam ekasmin sa bhāryā bhavatām a gaṇe rudra āvāse tu saṃsthāya tvayā rātrau mahā śrutiḥ tatra dṛṣṭaḥ tvayā devaḥ divya āśvarya vibhūtimān om kāra paramam bahma deva gaṃdharva kiṃnaraiḥ dhyāyamānaḥ param brahma oṃkāra ākhyam tu īśvaram tvayā adya avagatam sarva paṃca āyatana darśanāt bhaktiḥ ca eva tadā jātā a sāpatyasya nareśvara kim ebhiḥ kamalaiḥ kārya varaṃśaṃsuḥ alam kṛtaḥ niveditāḥ tathā puṣpāḥ paṃcāyatana vāsine dīyamānam ca devāya suvarṇasya śatam param na gṛhītam tatas kṣetre tu a mahātmanā prabhāte ca tvayā tasmin dṛṣṭaḥ śaṃsuḥ yadṛcchayā āścaryam paramam matvā tasmin āyatane sthitaḥ karmaṇā tena rāja iṃdra iyam vyuṣṭiḥ tava ā gatā sa bhavān lubdhakaḥ jātaḥ sa patnīkaḥ nareśvaraḥ puṣpa anukalpanāt tasmāt śaṃkarasya ca pūjanāt iyam vyuṣṭiḥ ta thā jātā paṃcāyatana pūjanāt oṃkāra īśvara māhātmyāt alpena tapasā nṛpa sam tuṣṭa stava rāja iṃdra brahmarūpīcaḥ īśvaraḥ tasmāt rakṣaskha rāja iṃdra puṣkara tvam mahī tale avimuktam samāsādya kārra śaraṇam traja prasādāt tasya devasya draṣṭāsi padam īśvaram iti uktaḥ satu rājāvaitena eva tu mahā ṛṣiṇā sarva gātraḥ tuharpāḥ viṣṭaḥ tam abravīt janmāṃtaram tvayā ākhyātam trahmaṇām kula vardhana saṃsāre tvad samaiḥ saṃgaḥ puṇya bhārāt tu jāyate evam prasādya tam vipram rājā atu kṛta niścayaḥ sa patnīkaḥ jagāma āśu vārāṇasyām mahā mune śaṃbhoḥ priyatame deśe paṃcāyatana mukkiṃde dakṣiṇām mūrtim āsthāya om kāraḥ tatra saṃsthitaḥ durlabham ca para sthānam mānuṣaiḥ akṛtātmabhiḥ akṛtātmabhiḥ akṛta sukṛta saṃbhāraiḥ rudra āvāsa iti vikhyātam puṇya dam sarva dehinām rudra āvāse kṛta snānaḥ paṃcāyatana vāsinam drakṣyāmi īśvaram devam yam dṛṣṭavān odbhavaḥ punar kali kalmaṣa bhūtaiḥ tu yeṣām na upagatā amatiḥ teṣām dṛśyam ca gamyam ca tat sthānam śaśimaulinaḥ tīrtham ca sthāpitam vyā tra daitya dānava nāyakaiḥ aṃtar dhyāna śataiḥ nityam pūjyate parameśvaraḥ tatra gatvā āturaḥ rājarṣiḥ paramam bhāvam āsthitaḥ ārā dhayānaḥ deveśam paṃcāyatanam īśvaram śāṃta ākāram vinirnatya jñāna dīpena īśvaram dṛṣṭvā avāsatuḥ rājarṣiḥ oṃkāram paramam padam tena vyāptam idam viśvam girā iva paramātmanā vārāṇasyām tu om kāram paṃcāyatana saṃsthitam yad darśanāt nara āloke vijñāna aiśvarya bhājanāḥ dānānām durlabham dānam vratānām durlabham param sarvatra durlabham sthānam iti āha bhagavān śivaḥ bhaktyā paramayā yuktāḥ mahādevam viśaṃti ca pūjayiṣyaṃti ye tatra sarva bhāvena śaṃkaram vijñeyāḥ te gaṇābhadre mānuṣī prakṛti sthitāḥ vārāṇasyām tu ye kecid tīrthāni āyatanāni ca teṣām ca eva tu sarveṣām oṃkāram prathamam smṛtam oṃkāra darśanāt devi sarvān dṛṣṭān asaṃśayaḥ uvāca devi paśya idam udyānam nirmitam purā sahadevyā atatovyāsa vārāṇasyām vṛṣadhvajaḥ deva udyānaṃ hi didṛkṣuḥ bhagavān tat samaṃtataḥ pūrvasmin tu asi ge bhāge devaḥ devyāḥ parātparaḥ udyānam darśayāmāsa nānā kinnara nāditam nānā vṛkṣa samākīrṇa nānā ku suma śobhitam nānā vṛkṣa samākīrṇa nānā pakṣi vināditam caṃpaka aśoka puṃnāga priyaṃgu śata saṃkulam saṃyuktam sarvatas sa tad udyānam āsādya devīm prāha jagatpatiḥ paśya devi vimāna sthā kinnarām śra manorame pārijātaka khaṃḍāni tathā kalpadrumāṇi ca mama loke caye vṛkṣāḥ viṣṇu loke caye śubhe iyam vārāṇasī devī śiva lokam samāśritā tiṣṭhate loka īśaḥ brahmā kamala saṃbhavaḥ parivārya sthitāḥ sarvāḥ oṃkāram ca ādi mukti dam ūrdhvam goloka saṃsthānam gavām ghāsaḥ svayaṃbhuvaiḥ gavayatra saṃvarṇānām payaḥ mūrdhni samāpatat tatas mayā ūrdhvatas dṛṣṭa āgāvaḥ tāḥ somapa anugāḥ tatas tau īkṣitāḥ tatra bhīta amāvaḥ tadā abhavan tejasām amama nirdagdha ana eka varṇa amṛpā āditāḥ gāvaḥ pūrvam imāḥ devi āsa nu kapila vaṃśa jāḥ na eka varṇāḥ tathābhūtāḥ yat etāḥ prekṣita āmayā tam vaiśaraṇya tām gatvā amām eva loka mātaraḥ āśritāḥ saḥ mama āgatya soma utpattim samāyayuḥ prasādayitvā atāgāvaḥ brahmā amām abravīt tatas na vināśam yathā yāṃti tathā kuru sura arcita goprekṣakeśvaram gatvā a dṛṣṭvā ca abhyarcya mānavaḥ tatas tāvī kṣyamāṇā astu prasanne suvrata imayi nhade siṃcitum ārebhe śāṃtāḥ sthira carāḥ tatas yathā bhakta ahitāḥ sarva abrahmaṇā api mahātmanā dhanyāḥ pūjyāḥ ca mānyāḥ ca bhaviṣyathamam ājñayā kapilāka dama aśvaryam tadā prabhṛti kathyate atrā api svayam eva aham vṛpadhvaja eti smṛtaḥ sāṃnidhyam kṛtavān devi satām vaidṛśya tām gataḥ devānām api durlabham śāṃti artha dharma lokānām sarva sam jātam idam etat manoharam gaccheyam aham īśa iti upaśām sthitaḥ tadā śivaḥ bhūtvā sthitaḥ uham ca puṇyam asya api darśanam atra āhma ṇānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā brahmaṇā ca api saṃgṛtya viṣṇunā āsthāpitaḥ punar tam dṛṣṭvā brahmaṇā viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvigna cetasā samānīta mā idam liṃgam kasmāt sthāpitavān asi tam uvāca punar viṣṇuḥ brahmāṇam kupita analam naṃkaḥ jannaraḥ sthāpayāmāsa vidhivat bhaktyā aparamayā ayutaḥ devadevam mahādevam prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā tatas ham sarva devānām paśyatām tatra tatra ca mānana arthaṃhitābhyām ca sūkṣmaḥ bhūtvā sva līlayā lokānām sarva netra gaḥ evam devi tatas viṣṇu brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ aśakyā sā gatiḥ tasya yoginām ca eva śāśvatī asmin api sthitāḥ daityāḥ sarve te deva kaṃṭakāḥ vyāghra rūpam samāsthāya nirdagdhāḥ tejasā āmayā vyāghreśvaraḥ tatas khyātaḥ nityam tatra aham āsthitaḥ na punar durgatim yāṃti dṛṣṭvā imam vyāghram īśvaram tava ājñayā aṃbikā ica atratasya idam kadama āsthitam nirvāṇa nāma vikhyātam sura asura nama skṛtam dṛṣṭvā imam manujaḥ satyam paśu pāśaiḥ vimucyate ādau atra aham māsa agra prasthitaḥ gaṇapaiḥ saha jyeṣṭhasthānam idam tasmāt etat me puṇya darśanam dṛṣṭvā tat amalam liṃgam jyeṣṭhasthāne samāsthitam āsamaṃtāt tu deva īśi liṃgāni sthāpitāni ca dṛṣṭvā tat niyata āmaya de iha bhed guṇaḥ bhavet mahādeva iti te sarve dhyāyamānāḥ sura uttamāḥ vārāṇasyām tatas devi devānām mānitaḥ bhavam kṣetram vārāṇasī puṇyā muktidāsā bhaviṣyati avimukteśvaram mām vaiyotra drakṣyati mānavaḥ prāṇāḥ mama priyam idam sthānam jñātvā liṃgam pratiṣṭhitam śaileśvaram iti khyātam dṛśyatām idam āsthitam dṛṣṭvā eva śailajam devim amalokam avāpnuyāt purā vārāṇasī ca iyam puṇya bhāgā pramodinī kṣetra āgatam alaṃkṛtya jān havyā saha saṃgatā varaṇānām a tatra eva gaṃgā asi śvasarit varā sthāpi tat saṃgam etābhyām brahmaṇā āliṃgam uttamam saṃgameśvaram tris arcayet saṃgameśānam tasya janma gatam punar idam atra adbhutam kṣetram nivāsam yoginām param kṣetra madhye ca yatra aham sva yam bhūtvā samāsthitaḥ siddhānām sthānam iti evam madīya trata cāriṇām yogi nām mokṣa lipsānām janma mṛtyūn aśocati sthāpitam liṃgam etat ca śukreṇa bhṛgu sūnunā nāmnā aśukreśvaram puṇyam sarva siddhaiḥ purā arcitam kaḥ sāditāḥ māritāḥ yasya liṃgāni yaiḥ sthāpitāni ligāni sambandha sāmānya vivakṣāyām ṣaṣṭhī ka dṛṣṭvā īṃ mānavaḥ sadyas muktaḥ syāt sarva kilviṣaiḥ purā jaṃbuka rūpeṇa pratiṣiddha āmayā tetu gomāyu vadha śaṃkitāḥ mayā a jaṃbuka rūpeṇa sādi tāḥ dānavāḥ purā mama ājñayā punar taiḥ tu liṃgāni sthāpitāni ca yasya liṃgāni puṇyāni sarva kāma pradāni tu gaṃbhīreśvara vikhyātam liṃgam sūryeṇa sthāpitam kalpeśivam mahā puṇyam liṃgam yama bhaya apaham yamena sthāpitam bhadre dṛṣṭvā avaita sya mokṣaṇam īśena sthāpitam liṃgam yasmāt gatvā ca krīḍhayā yaśva imam devam īśānam dṛṣṭvā āvām abhyarcya mānavaḥ īśānaḥ tatra tat tasmāt param sura namaskṛtam evam etāni puṇyāni saṃti sthānāni suvrate kathitāni mahā kṣetre gutyaka stham idam śṛṇu krośam krośam catur dikṣu kṣetram etat prakīrtitam yojanam vidhi kṣetrasya mṛtyu kāle amṛta pradam gaṇa tvam labhate dṛṣṭvā svayam mokṣam avāpsyati gāṇapatyam tatas yāti gatiḥ sāmuktiḥ uttamā tatas mahālayaḥ yasmāt kedārāt muktim āpnuyāt vyāsaḥ uvāca śilādasya ātmajam pu tram prayuṃjānam pracakratuḥ ārādhya sarva kalyāṇam jagatpatim aniṃditam vyāsaḥ uvāca katham nandī samutpannaḥ katham ārādhya śaṃkaram samāna tvam agāt śam bhoḥ pratīhāra tvam eva ca abhūt ṛṣiḥ sadharma ātmā śilādaḥ nāma vīryavān apaśyam laṃbamānān svān niraye asati sat dijaḥ ārādhaya mahādevam putra artham dvisattama yaḥ smad saṃtāraṇe śaktaḥ sate putram pradā syati teṣām vākyam tatas śrutvā jagāma śaraṇam śivam tat ṛṣṭvā somam īśānam praṇataḥ pādayoḥ gataḥ harṣa gadgadayā avācā tuṣṭāva vibudha īśvaram khaṣṭre sureśānām brahmaṇaḥ pataye namaḥ kāma aṃga nāśanāya eva yoga saṃbhava hetave kaṇiśa ādi arjanam śilam iti yādavaḥ ṛṣiṇām pataye nityam devānām pataye namaḥ devānām pataye ca eva yoginām pataye namaḥ vara dāya ca bhaktānām namaḥ sarvagatāya ca tanmātra iṃdriya bhūtānām vikārāṇām gaṇaiḥ saha prakṛteḥ pataye nityam pūjyāya apara gāmine īśvarāya namaḥ nityam yoga gamyā yaḥ raṃhase saṃsāra utpatti nāśāya sarva kāma pradāya ca avaśyāya namaḥ nityam namaḥ bhasma aṃga dhāriṇe sūrya anala ambuja akṣāya ardha caṃdra dharāya ca yasmāt uktaḥ tam eva asya jagataḥ sthiti nāśayoḥ aśaraṇyasya deveśa tvattaḥ ca śaraṇa arthinaḥ vara daḥ asmi iti tam prāha śilām mu ni sattamam tha vā co co aṃtaradhīyata aṃtarhitavān ṛṣiḥ śilādaḥ sītāyām lāṅgalapaddhatau yaḥ stotram etat akhilam paṭhati dvijanmā a prātar śuciḥ niyamavān dvijasattamānām tam bahma rākṣasa piśācaka bhūta saṃgha ahiṃsaṃtinaḥ dvipa da pannaga pūtanāḥ ca uvāca devadeveśam vācā a saṃsajjamānayā gate tasmin mahādeve ṛṣiḥ parama pūjitaḥ svam āśramam upāgamya ṛṣibhyaḥ kathayan tatas taiḥ bhṛśam sam stutaḥ ca eva kālena muni sattamaḥ sa didṛkṣuḥ yajña bhūmi lāṃgalena ca karṣatām tasya tu utkarṣamāṇasya sītāyām samupasthitaḥ saṃva rtaka anala prakhyaḥ kumāraḥ pratyadṛśyata sa tam dṛṣṭvā tadā udbhūtam kumāram dīpta tejasam rākṣasaḥ yam iti jñātvā abhayāt na upasasāra ha upāsarpata dīna ātmā avāta tāta iti saḥ vavīt tatas vāyuḥ tad ākāśe śilā ī prāhasatvaram sālaṃkāyana putraḥ teyāḥ usaudevena śaṃbhunā tasmāt naṃdī iti nāmnā ayam bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ na taḥsa vāyu vacanāt nam dinam pariṣasvaje gṛhītvā ācā āśramam nītaḥ naṃdīśaḥ tuṣṭi vardhanaḥ cūḍā upanayana ādīni karmāṇi apicakāḥ raha kṛtvā ca adhyāpayāmāsa vedān sa aṃga padakramān āyurvedam dhanurvedam gāṃdharva śāstram uttamam śilpāni ca eva sarvāṇi nimitta jñānam eva ca bhūta grāma cikitsāṃca mātṝṇām caritam ca yat bhujaṃgānām ca sarveṣām yat kiṃcid pariceṣṭitam sat ācāram dharmaśāstram ālakṣya dṛṣṭvā sarva śāstram sat ācāram aṣṭa śaivya ākaraṇāni ca tathā eva ca purāṇāni itihāsam aśeṣatas ciṃtanam mātṛ tatvam mahā maṃtram yoginām śāstram uttamam paṃcabhiḥ divasaiḥ vyāsa parijñānam aśeṣatas dakṣaḥ śuciḥ adīna ātma apri yava aganasūyakaḥ maṃsam anuprāptau śilādasya mahā ojasau tau abhyarcya yathānyāyam śilādaḥ su mahā tapāḥ tau ālakṣya sukha āsīnau āsane parama arcite abhijñau sarva jaṃtūnām sarva lāke carācare uvāca guṇa sapannaḥ same vaṃśa vivardhanaḥ samāḥ na āyata saṃtuṣṭaḥ putram naṃdinam acyutam tayoḥ pāde sva śirasā apātayaṃtam aniṃditam prāyuktām dharma nitya tām guru śuśrūṣaṇe bhāvam lokān ca eva tathā akṣayān śilādaḥ tau tathā alakṣyaḥ āśiṣa devayoḥ tayoḥ vissṛjya naṃdi naṃbhītaḥ saḥ pṛcchat ṛṣi sattamau śilādaḥ uvāca tapovaṃtau ṛṣī satyau gati jñau sarva dehinām mitrāvaruṇau ūcatuḥ tava eṣa tanayaḥ tāta aṣṭa āyuḥ pūrva dharmataḥ adya ārabhya aṣṭame varṣe jīvitum na bhaviṣyati tatas sa śoka saṃtaptaḥ nyapatat bhuvi duḥkhitaḥ kā kī vilalāpa ha svaram śrutvā su śubhaḥ kaṃdamānam ca tam dṛṣṭvā pitaram duḥkhitam bhṛśam naṃdī uvāca kena tvam tāta duḥkhena vepamānaḥ ca rodiṣi duḥkham te kutas dbhūtam jñātum icchāmi tatvataḥ śilādaḥ uvāca putra tvam kila varṣeṇa jīvitam saṃprahāsyasi ūcatuḥ tādṛśam sarva tatas mām duḥkha mā āviśat anyaṃhino catur vidhau natau anṛta bhāṣiṇau tena aham putra śokena bhṛśam pīḍita mānasaḥ naṃdī uvāca devaḥ vā a dānavaḥ uvāpi yamaḥ uvāpi kadācana śilādaḥ uvāca kiṃtapaḥ kim parijñā samāśritaḥ yena tvam dāruṇam mṛtyum vaṃcayiṣyasi putraka naṃdī uvāca cayiṣyena viyayā mahādevena nāthena mṛtyuṃjeṣyāminā anyathā drakṣyāmi śaṃkaram devam sa me mṛtyum vijeṣyati śilādaḥ uvāca mahādevaḥ purā a dṛṣṭaḥ labdhaḥ tvam me yatas sutaḥ bha vān tu varṣeṇa ekena katham drakṣyati śaṃkaram varṣeṇa kiṃtapaḥ putra śakyam kartu vṛṣadhvajāt kāteśaktiḥ mahābhāga yena si naṃyu uvāca na atatapasā devaḥ dṛśyate na ca vidyayā śuddhena manasā abhaktyā dṛśyate parameśvaraḥ aham eva ca jānāmi yena drakṣyāmi śaṃkaram tvayā a visṛṣṭaḥ gacchāmi acireṇa trilocanam sutaṃtumām a mataḥ na hiṃsā vā ayātesyāt iti tāta vrajāmi aham tiṣṭhatam vā āśayānam vā ādhāvantam patitam tathā sahasrāṇi yama koṭi śatāni ca abhidravaṃti saṃkruddhāḥ daṃḍa pāśa uyata āyudhāḥ yena drakṣyāmi tam aham eva jānāmi iti anvayaḥ daṇḍa iti daṇḍa pāśa ādīni udyatāni āyudhāni yaiḥ tathā uktāḥ tatra api nā anyathā tāta bhayam tvam me kariṣyasi avatīrya jala itāta bhāva śuddhim sa mā āsthitaḥ drakṣyāmi iva raṃ nātham devam mṛtyu haram param nam mṛtyu kālaḥ yāmyaḥ uvā kariṣyati mama avyathām tam evam vādinam matvā bruvāṇam śuddhayā girā vyasa jayat adīna ātmā rucchrāt putram mahā tapāḥ praṇamya sa pituḥ pādauśirasā ca mahā yaśāḥ pradakṣiṇam samāvṛtya saṃpratastheti ni śvitam namaskārya pituḥ pādau sa didṛkṣuḥ udāra dhīḥ dhyāyate manasā devam praṇata ārti haram haram iti śrī śiva mahā purāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām catuścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ nirgataḥ atha tad ānaṃdī jagāḥ ma saritām varām bhuvanām iti vikhyātām sarva loka sukha āvahām tām praviśya tatas dhīmān ekāgraḥ hradi saṃsthitaḥ jajā pasatadānaṃdī rudra parama kāraṇam koṭiḥ ekā yadā japtā tadā devaḥ tutoṣa tat āgatya āha bhagavān gṛheśarvaḥ kapardadhṛk uvāca praṇataḥ bhūyas prayata ātmā tadā eva ha dvitīyām taptum icchāmi ṭiṃ parama kāraṇa jajāpa koṭi manyāṃtu rudram eva anuciṃtayan dvitīyāyām tatas kāṭyām saṃpūrṇāya vṛṣadhvajaḥ anyān ca bhagavan koṭiṃṭatīyām api jāpitum uktvā jagāma deveśaḥ devyā saha mahā dyutiḥ tatas tṛtīyām tatra e va koṭim anyām jajāpa ha yuga aṃta āditya saṃkāśam tatas samabhavat dapuḥ taptāṃkoṭyām tṛtīyāyām ajvalat vidyayā saha sataṃkareṇa saṃgṛtya auddhṛtyaśirasā tathā saṃspṛśam śva agra hastena naṃdinam kāmam atravī tu naṃdī uvāca japeyam kāṭim anyām yam yam hiraṇuṣe kāmam te tuṣṭāva parameśānam jarā śoka vināśanam namaḥ kāma aṃga nāśāya trailokya hananāya ca namaḥ kāla ugra daṃḍāya ugra daṃḍāya vai namaḥ namaḥ nīlaśikhaṃḍāya sahasra śirase namaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādāya sarvatas akṣi mukhāya ca sarvatas śrutaye ca eva sarvam ādṛtya tiṣṭhate namaḥ caṃdra arka netrāya yogīśāya ajitāya ca pinākapāṇaye ca eva śūla mudgara pāṇaye namaḥ triśūla hastāya ugra daṃḍa dharāya ca namaḥ deva adhipataye rudrāṇām pataye namaḥ ādityānām capataye vasūnām pataye namaḥ dhyāninā dhyāyamānā yad dhyānibhiḥ saṃstutāya ca mṛtyave kāladaṃḍāya yamāya ca mahātmane avitre sarva devānām dharma āyāne ka netriṇe umā ruva iṃdra rūpāya tathā nārāyaṇāya ca lalāṭa aṃkita netrāya tata ūrdhva jananāya ca mṛtyu pāśa ugra hastāḥ ya nakṣatra āloka sūtriṇam viṣṇu deha ardha saṃsthāya tasmin śva vara dāya ca sarva bhūtāya saṃjñāya sarva bhūta aṃnukaṃpine aṃtarbhūta adhivāsāya prāṇinām jīvanāya ca vāce ca vāgmine ca eva sūkṣma āyatanave namaḥ sampāda kāya prāṇa sva rūpa ayavā namaḥ te apaśave nityam kṣetrajñāya viṭāya ca viṣṇave loka kartre ca prajānām pataye namaḥ brāhmaṇāya viśuddhāya tathā durvāsase namaḥ śilpine śilpa nāśāya viduṣe viśvakarmaṇe pulahāya pulastyāyaka tva āvhānāya tāpine bhūtāya bhūtanāthāya kūṣmāṃḍa pataye namaḥ avaśyāya api avadhyāya ajarāya amarāya ca akṣayāya avyayāya eva tathā apratihatāya ca anāthasyāya sarveṣām tathā eva puṇya rūpiṇe sūkṣmebhyaḥ ca ati sūkṣmāya sarvagāḥ yamahātmane na viṣṇu tvam na deva tvam na api iṃdra tvam ca kāmaye icchāmi aham viśvanātha saṃsārāt vinivartanam draṣṭum icchāmi yogena eṣa me dīyatām varaḥ tvam nogatiḥ purādeva tvam vā anāthāyanam mahat tvayā a tyaktasya ca eva aste vināśaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ anyām gatim na paśyāmi paśyāmi ātyaṃtikam sukham paśyāmi sarva loka īśa saṃsāra mati dustaram pratīccha mām mahādevaḥ epa medīyatām varaḥ yā edam prātar utthāya paṭhet avimanāḥ naraḥ caturdaśyām viśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇaḥ uvā āyatiḥ tathā yaḥ tu imam śṛṇuyāt nityam śrāvayet vā dvijottamaḥ mahīyate pūjām labhate iti paṃcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om namaḥ śivāya nandīśa ghora tapasā asam saḥ aśvamedha phalam prāpya rudra loke mahīyate stavam pāpa praṇāśanam eṣa maṃtra japaḥ ca eva saṃsāra vinivartakaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām paṃcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ pādayoḥ śirasā ānatam karābhyām saṃmukhābhyām tu saṃgṛtya bhuvane śvaraḥ uvāca jagatām nāthaḥ vacasā atoṣayan śvatam nirīkṣya gaṇapān sarvān ma hādevaḥ avadat punar vyayaḥ ca evasa pitāsa suhṛd janaḥ ye saṃdṛṣṭāḥ snigdha bhāvam gata āśvaye mama iṣṭaḥ gaṇapaḥ ca eva mad vīryaḥ mad parākramaḥ mama pārśva gataḥ sadā mad rūpaḥ ca eva bhavitā mahā yoga bala anvi taḥ ṛddhi yuktam sahat dīpam kṣīrodam amṛta ākaram kuśeśaya mayīm mālām svayaṃbhūḥ ā tmanaḥ śubhām āvabandha mahādevānam dinedeva rūpiṇe bhaukaṃṭha avasaktayā tryakṣaḥ daśa bhujaḥ śrīmān dvitīyā eva śaṃkaraḥ śrama śva ayam atyartha tapasā tava bhāvitaḥ samaṃtā yojanam kṣetram divya siddhi pradāyakam siddha cāraṇasam kīrṇam apsaraḥ gaṇa sevitam siddha kṣetram param gutyam bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā yat kiṃcid kurute naraḥ a śubham vā aśubham vā atra sarva bhavati bhasmasāt japamānasya ataulyam vai rudrāṇām tat bhaviṣyati tatas japyam śrutam vāri gṛhītvā āhāra nirmalam uktvā ānaṃdībhavaḥ ceti visasarja mahā tapāḥ sā atadā divyatas yāca puṇya āmāna jana aśubhā haṃsa kāraṃḍava ākīrṇa a cakravāka upaśobhitā strī rūpa dhāriṇī ca eva prāṃjaliḥ śirasā ānatā padma utpala dala ābhākṣī mahādevam upasthitā mahādevaḥ uvāca yasmāt yajña udakā devi pravṛttā tvam śubha ānane tasmāt yajña udakānām abhaviṣyasi sarit varā kuryāt śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ prabhuḥ sātam āghrāya śirasi pāṇibhyām parimārjatī putra premṇā abhiṣiṃcaṃtī srotobhiḥ tanu jaiḥ tathā payasā śaṃkha gau reṇa devadevī nirīkṣatī tāni srotāṃsi trīṇi syāt śrotrebhyaḥ patitā nadī naṃdī trisrota saṃpuṇyatitas tām anvavīkṣata naṃdī yaḥ parama harṣitaḥ yasmāt upapraṇādena pravṛttā āsām ahānadī tasmāt śivenakām tau ai uvāca vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ jāṃbūnada mayam citram sa devaḥ parama adbhutam mukuṭam ca dadau tasmai kuṃḍale vāṭata udbhave tam ta thā abhyarcitam vyomni dṛṣṭvā ameya prabhākaram deva ūpi rājyebhiḥ sicat na nādaśa tata guṇam yasmāt suvarṇāt niḥsṛtya nadīyam saṃpravartate tat suvarṇodakā nāmnā mahādevaḥ abhyabhāṣata jāṃbūnada mayāya prabhā tat ca jāṃbūnadam nāma jāpya īśvara samīpataḥ vikhyā tam phalam eteṣām yajña udānam mahātmanām tat ca jaṃbūnadam divyaṃdavam jāpya īśvaram cayaḥ tri rātra upoṣitaḥ gatvā snātvā abhyarcya ca śūlinam brāhmaṇān tarpayitvā acayatra tatra mṛtaḥ naraḥ naṃdīśvarasya anucaraḥ kṣīroda nilayaḥ bhavet nandīśvara samaḥ nityam yaḥ vyayaḥ same sadā asyāt guṇapaḥ variṣṭhaḥ tvayā asamaḥ kāṃta vapuḥ bhavet iti iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām naṃdīśvarotpattiḥ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ devaḥ nandīśvaram devam ca abhiṣicya vibhūṣitam iti ṣaṭcatvāriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ gaṇeśvarāṇām sarveṣām ki tattve manyase śubhe sata loka ādhipatya aṃca gaṇa īśānām tathā eva ca sarveṣām iti deveśa naṃdī pu tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ sura siddha gaṇa arcitaḥ prāc mukhaḥ sa gaṇeśaḥ vaibhūtvāt devaḥ maheśvaraḥ ciṃtayāmāsa sa gaṇā nūrudrān ca diśi vāsinaḥ evam ciṃtita mātrāḥ te gaṇādhyakṣāḥ mudā anvitāḥ ye sthitāḥ dakṣiṇām āśām paścimām uttarām tathā ca ūrdhvam adhas te tuśūla hasta aniṣaṃgiṇaḥ nīlakaṃṭha asita grīvāḥ śuddha prajvalana īkṣaṃṇāḥ samāgatāḥ tadā avyāsaye ṣāṃsaṃkhyāna vidyate brahmāṃḍa āvaraṇāḥ paṃca adhaurvyāt ayaḥ mune kapālī śaḥ viśoka śva śata netraḥ śata anilaḥ anaṃta rudrāḥ śata śas śata pādāḥ śata ānanāḥ saṃprāptāḥ sarva loka īśāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva mahā mune tatas karāla vadanaḥ bhṛkuṭī bhūpita ānanaḥ paṃca yojana vistīrṇaḥ dīrghataḥ tādṛś eva ca tatas catvāri iva pāṃḍuraḥ vṛtaḥ koṭi śatena eva sadṛśānām mahātmanām bhārabhūtiḥ iti khyātaḥ mahā yoga bala anvitaḥ somavarṣā iti vikhyātaḥ koṭīratha samāvṛtaḥ tādṛśānām gaṇādhyakṣaḥ devasya ca sthita ugratas aṃbā śivaḥ mahākāyaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ mahā balaḥ yugāṃta anala saṃkāśaḥ sthitaḥ sthira yaśaḥ balaḥ caṃdramauliḥ mahākāśaḥ catu bahuḥ vilohitaḥ eka pādaiḥ mahākāyaiḥ kṣaiḥ taiḥ śūla pāṇibhiḥ vṛtaḥ koṭi śatena eva sthāṇuḥ tatra abhyavartata sa pārṣadaḥ yam rudrasya sarva asura su pūjitaḥ idam gaṇapa nāma apataḥpurataḥ śuciḥ sahasra bāhu caraṇaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ sahasrapād tryakṣaḥ caṃdra kṛta āpīḍaḥ śiras mālā vibhūṣitaḥ caṃdramauliḥ mahākeśaḥ koṭiśas parivāritaḥ tatas parivṛtaḥ somaḥ ājagāma mahā balaḥ tatas param samīpe tam deva devam vara pradam caturvakaḥ mahā tejāḥ caturviṃśati lakṣaṇaiḥ sahasrabā durvyāttāsyaḥ mahādeva ardhavāhanaḥ karāla vadanaḥ ca eva śaṃku karṇaḥ mahā balaḥ asi pāṇiḥ mahā tejāḥ śata pādaḥ kṛśa udaraḥ koṭi śata inasaḥ āgāt tatas uparaḥ vyāsa gaṇapaḥ sa mahā balaḥ sarvatovadanaḥ śrīmān sarvatas pāṇi pādadhṛk aśanim dhārayan śubhām śataiḥ ṭataḥ tu koṭīnām aṣṭabhiḥ ca ātmanaḥ samaiḥ nikuṃbha eti vikhyātaḥ śatapādaḥ śatānanaḥ āgatā iti aparaḥ ca atra taḍitkeśaḥ mahā balaḥ daṃḍadhārī mahā cakraḥ śam kha kuṃda sama prabhaḥ tatas uparaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnām gaṇapaiḥ ṭataḥ sarpa mālā śataṃbiḥ śradā ājagāma mahā tapāḥ sarvajñāna mahā tejāḥ viśrutaḥ su mahā dyutiḥ tathā anyaḥ ca caṃdrāyudhaḥ mahātejāḥ cakrabāhuḥ kaṭā kaṭaḥ gaṇa koṭi śataiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ vataḥ samanudhā vati śaṃkukarṇaḥ abhyayāt ca eva gaṇa koṭyā mahā balaḥ naṃdikaḥ ca eva daśabhiḥ piṃgākṣaḥ aṣṭabhiḥ eva ca nāmnā aprasiddhaḥ aja pāda saṃmā eka pāda tvāt iti bhāvaḥ aśani vajyam koṭīnām aṣṭabhiḥ aṣṭakaḥ kaṭākaṭaḥ tad nāmakaḥ vināyakaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā kūṣmāṃḍaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ dhūmrakeśaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ patākī daśabhiḥ tathā śata muktā uṣṭādaśabhiḥ śata paṃcabhiḥ eva ca sahasra śīrṣaḥ ṣaṣ vigaṇa koṭi śataiḥ vṛtaḥ vīraḥ daśabhiḥ āyā kuṃbhakarṇaḥ tathā aṣṭabhiḥ viśvabalaḥ sahasreṇa manuḥ tasyāḥ śatena vai nāda īśaniḥ tathā aṣṭābhiḥ samabhiḥ caṃdravartanaḥ mahīdharaḥ sahasreṇa koṭinā aṃgaṇapaiḥ yutaḥ praṇava āditya mūrtiḥ vai koṭyā ca eva hiḥ kuṃbhaḥ ca paṃcadaśabhiḥ tathā saṃkocataḥ paraḥ eka pāda uṣṭaṣaṣṭyā acata thā sama śiraḥ gaṇaḥ mahābalaḥ ca daśabhiḥ apasmāra śva viśrutaḥ śvāpi nāma ājagāmaha koṭīnām ca sahasrāṇām śataiḥ viṃśatibhiḥ vṛtaḥ ājagmuḥ mahā yoga valāḥ nvitāḥ bhūta koṭi sahasreṇa pramathaiḥ koṭibhiḥ vṛtaḥ vīrabhadraḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyāḥ ūṣa kaśva mahā balaḥ megha saudāmanīnām anavatyā koṭibhiḥ vṛtaḥ prabhākaraḥ ca viṃśatyā ā vidyudbhiḥ tu mahā balaḥ mṛtyuḥ ca eva yamaḥ ca eva kālaḥ viṣadharaḥ tathā śatamā yaḥ mahā māyaḥ parvata ābharaṇaḥ tathā ekaśṛṃga abhivikhyātaḥ tathā ābhṛṃgiriṭi śvayaḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ gaṇapāḥ ca mahā balāḥ mukhena vādyāni tathā vādayantaḥ mudā anvitāḥ rathaiḥ nāgaiḥ hayaiḥ ca eva ṛkṣa markaṭa vāhanāḥ vimāna iṣu tathā ārūḍhāḥ nānā rūpa dharāḥ pare ekīkṛtya tad ākāśaṃsa kiṃnara mahā uragam bherī śaṃkha mṭadam gaiśva paṇava ānaka gomukhaiḥ bherī gaṃbhīra sat nādaiḥ nānā ḍamaru ḍiṃḍimaiḥ vādyamānaiḥ mahā ghoraiḥ ājagmuḥ yatra śaṃkaraḥ munibhiḥ vyāsa saṃsiddhaiḥ vṛtāḥ sarve samaṃtataḥ ṛgvedaḥ dakṣiṇe bhāge divya kuṃḍala bhūṣitaḥ mavet aśva nānā rūpa dharaḥ śubhaḥ sadā itihā sa purāṇāni nānā rūpa dharāṇi ca devadevaḥ mahādevaḥ yajña rūpa dharaḥ śubhaḥ dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇam devam mahādevaḥ bravīt tadā vācā agaṃbhīrayā ataṃtu sa devam loka bhāvanam śṛṇu viṣṇo vacomatyam yat da kṣyāmi sureśvara yat ite ca priyam kṛṣṇa abhiṣekam kuruṣva ame prahasya ca mahādevam tataḥ nārāyaṇaḥ bravīt tathā vibho devānām api devaḥ tvam pramāṇam tu na saṃśayaḥ rāvata ārūḍhaḥ ājagāma śiva antikam vasubhiḥ mārutaiḥ ca eva prāṇi vāsān mahā balaiḥ te viśvakarma ādya vicitra dehāḥ viśveśam eka akṣaram avyayam ca iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe naṃdi upākhyāne saptacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sarva deva īśvara īśvaram om namaḥ śivāya ājñāpayavaca umama kiṃsāgarān śoṣayāmaḥ pāṭayāmaḥ su parvatān hanma etāḥ diśaḥ kasya adya vyasanam ghoram kariṣyāmaḥ tava ājñayā tān tathāvādinaḥ sarvān satatam bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca devaḥ saṃpūjya gaṇa andraḥ maheśvaraḥ śṛṇudhvam yatkṛte pūrvam iha āhūtāḥ jagat hitāḥ śrutvā ca praṇata ātmānaḥ kurudhvam tat aśaṃkitāḥ naṃdīśvaraḥ yaṃputraḥ ūnaḥ sarveṣām īśvara īśvaraḥ priyaḥ gaṇāgraṇīḥ devaiḥ kriyatām vacanāt mama saināpatya abhiṣiṃcadhvam mahāgaṇapati patim adya prabhṛti yuṣmākam mayam nandīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ evam ukte bhagavatā rudrāṇī gaṇakāḥ śubhāḥ āsanam meru saṃkāśam śubhaṃsam upakalpayan śātakuṃbha mayam ca api varam cāmīkara prabha m muktā dāma nibham ca eva maṇi ratna vibhūṣitam staṃbhaiḥ vaidūrya mayaiḥ kiṃkiṇī jāla saṃkulam caturaṃgaka saṃyuktam maṃḍapam viśvatomukham tasmin saṃsthāpya deveśam abhyaṣiṃcanta naṃdinam keyūram kuṃḍale ca eva mukuṭam hāram eva ca svayaṃharaḥ ṛṣayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca enam pitāmaha purogamāḥ namaḥ kūṣmāṃḍa rāgāya vajja udyata karāya ca sālaṃkāyana putrāya halamārga utthitāya ca śaṃkhāḥ iti ādi vādya nāmāni vāṃśikā vaṃśa vādanam śīlam yeṣām goviṣāṇikāḥ rudra bhaktāya devāya namaḥ te jalaśāyine namaḥ gaṇādhipataye mahā yogi īśvarāya ca daṃḍaghaṃṭāyacaṃḍāya ekādaśaśatāya ca akṣayāya amṭatāya eva ajarāya avyayāya ca paśūnām pataye ca eva rudra rūpa dharāya ca namaḥ prabala veśāya sarvajñāyai jitāya ca kirīṭine kuṃḍaline mahā parigha bāhave prāṃjaliḥ praṇataḥ bhūtvā jaya śabdam cakāra ha tatas sarvāṇi bhūtāni brahmā śakraḥ tathā eva ca ḍiṃḍima dhenukāḥ ca eva mardana aśva saha sraśas tatas śaṃkha aśrva bherī aśva mardala aśva sahasraśas karkarā goviṣāṇikāḥ avādayanta gaṇapāḥ sa yakṣa asura pannagāḥ namaḥ naṃdīśvarāya iti yaḥ kṛtvā stutim ācaret tasya kūṣmāṃḍarājebhyaḥ na bhayam vidyate kvacid prabhāteyaḥ paṭhet nityam svayam vai bhāva saṃyutaḥ naṃdīśvaram ye praṇamam ti nityam prasanna sarva idriya śuddha satvāḥ te deva devasya sadā ati pūjyāḥ iṣṭa a viśiṣṭa aśva gaṇāḥ bhavanti iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām naṃdīśvarābhiṣekaḥ nāma aṣṭācatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas tān āga tān devān devānām adhipaḥ haraḥ mārutān prāha saṃgrātya kanyā artha sat patiḥ prabhuḥ mārutāvaḥ mahābhāga amahāsatvā mahaujasaḥ āmaṃtrya nāmnātān devān sarvān śakra purogamān om namaḥ yuṣmākam prīti dā kanyā subhagā divya rūpiṇī dātum arhatha tām śuddhām devāḥ ūcuḥ yuṣmākam ca eva tasya āśva sarvasya jagataḥ sadā mānyaḥ parāvara īśāna yasya atvam sat asat guruḥ kaśyapaḥ pulahaḥ śrīmān marīci śvapitāmahaḥ pitā brahmācatasya apideva tvam prapitāmahaḥ satvam pitā yācitum arhasi īśvarā uvāca na aham aham ikalyāṇīm satyam vaḥ bhāṣitam vacaḥ kiṃtu loka hita arthāya munīnām ca īdṛśam tathā adattān na grahīṣyāmi eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ tad kṣaṇāt mana sidhyā deva varam tadā svayam hotā atu tatra āsīt brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ vatte ca pāṇigrahaṇe gaṃdharvāḥ saha cāraṇaiḥ nāra daḥ parvataḥ ca eva citrāsanaḥ sa pārṣadaḥ sarvāśvaḥ suruciḥ ca eva hāhā hūhūḥ tathā eva ca urvaśī ca eva raṃbhā ca ghṛtācī loka viśrutā anyāḥ ca apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ deva manoharam tatas sa sa tkṛta udvāhaḥ naṃdī gatvā mahātmanaḥ pādau vai vaṃde devasya tathā viṣṇoḥ jagatpateḥ punar devyāḥ sa vaivyāsa brahmaṇaḥ sa tathā punar śilādasya kule ca ayam śriyā aparamayā ayutaḥ īśvarā uvāca varam vṛṇīṣva putra tvam nuṣācā iyam tava priyā dadāmi tevaram tuṣṭyā manasā ayat abhīpsitam devyā saha aham nuṣṭā iti anvayaḥ iṣṭomam ā iti śeṣaḥ kāmagam icchāgāḥ naṃdīśvarā uvāca sadā kālam mahādeva bhava tuṣṭaḥ bhavodbhava sadā ahaṃtaṃvanaṃdīśa saṃtuṣṭaḥ tu gaṇeśvara me paramam vacaḥ sadā iṣṭa śva variṣṭha śva parama aiśvarya saṃyutaḥ mahā yogī mahā iṣvāsaḥ prapitā sapitāmahaḥ ajayaḥ ca eva jetāsya pūjyeśa śva mahābalaḥ bhaviṣyati gaṇādhyakṣaḥ yaṃtā gaṇapatiḥ dhruvam pitāmaha upite vatsaye ca anya nava vaṃśa jāḥ mad samīpam ga miṣyaṃti mayā a datta varāḥ tathā parvatam ca eva vaiśśrājam kāmagam sarva kāma dam tatas devī mahābhāgā anaṃdinam varadā travīt naṃdīśvarā uvāca pādayoḥ patitām dṛṣṭvā tuṣṭā devī tataḥ travīt nityam dhyāna parā āsya ātmā jñāna ca matiḥ mā devyāḥ aśva vacanam śrutvā trahma nārāyaṇau ubhau nārāyaṇam atha alokya brahmaṇā āsa hitam haraḥ uvāca sahita audava prasṛṣṭena aṃtarātmanā adya prabhṛti naṃdī śaḥ putrābhyām mānitaḥ sadā prabhuḥ ca eva hi devānām pratīhāraḥ ca me sadā deva rudrāḥ gaṇāḥ ca eva sarva deva priye samān aiśvarya camama akṣayyaṃbhavadbhiḥ anumoditam satatam bhavatām ca api apriyaḥ rudra gaṇāḥ ūcuḥ bhavān maṃtāca yaṃtāca gatiśva agatiḥ eva ca asmākam īśa sarveṣām devānām api ce śvaraḥ cariṣyatām harasya agre rudrāṇām rudra sattamaḥ ṛṣīṇām devatānām ca pramathānām tathā eva ca mahā balaḥ mahā yogī bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ asmākam bhava nāthasya nāyaka utha vināyakaḥ tvam vai mahāsena samaḥ surāṇām nārāyaṇena amara pū jitena jāpya īśvara niketaḥ ca jāpya īśvara vibhāvitaḥ tvam ca eva sarva dātā ca vara daḥ bhava dīkṣitaḥ uvāca vacanam sarva antakiṃkaravāṇi vaḥ evam ukta aśva gaṇapa arudra aśva bhāva bhāṣitam tān abruvan divya jñāna ajñānam devasya saṃnidhau tvam asmākam gaṇa adhyakṣa stutaḥ devena śūlinā asmābhiḥ śva abhiṣiktaḥ tu nāyakaḥ mokṣa dāyakaḥ sattvam śiśuḥ ca saumyaḥ ca guṇavān nirguṇaḥ api ca kṣamā śauca dama upetaḥ bhavān naḥ priya kṛt sadā evam uktaḥ tad ānaṃdī sarvān prabala mānitaḥ śirasi aṃjalim ādāya gaṇapān astuvat tadā aśvamedha avabhṛtha vat iti tasmāt yathā janaḥ kilbiṣāt mucyate tathā namaḥ sahasra rūpebhyaḥ śata rūpebhyaḥ eva ca namaḥ mārjāra rūpebhyaḥ kāla rūpebhyaḥ eva ca deva asura manuṣyāṇām āpyāyibhyaḥ namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ dbhyaḥ sarva devānām namaḥ sarva gatāḥ śubhāḥ namaḥ saumya giribhyaḥ aśva bhavaṃtu gaṇanāyakāḥ iti stutāḥ gaṇapatayaḥ mahā balāḥ śubhaiḥ vacobhiḥ sura siddha tatas akṣayam jñānam anuttamā gatiḥ yamaḥ nitya tām diśaṃtu sarvam sura īśvarāḥ yakṣa piśāca gutyakāḥ idam naṃdi kṛta stotram yaḥ vācayati nityaśas saṃdhyāyām aparasyām tu yat pāpam pūrvasya saṃtyajet ca api sarva rātram na saṃśayaḥ tatas te gaṇapāḥ sarve saṃyutāḥ tena dhīmatā visṛṣṭa aśva tathā ājagmuḥ praṇipatya vṛṣadhvajam deva aśva ṛṣayaḥ ca eva sadeva upi maheśvaraḥ īpsitam sahadevyā vai jagāma ākāśam avyayam abhiṣekam vivāham ca paṭhet vā āśrāvayet tathā brāhmaṇaḥ pāṭha toyāti naṃdīśvara salokatām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra sam ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ hitāyām naṃdivivāhaḥ nāma ekonapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kasmin deśe mahā puṇyam etadā khyānam uttamam vṛttam brahma purogānām kasmin kāle mahā dyute dhyāyaḥ om namaḥ śivāya ūnapaṃ yathāśrutam mayā a sarva vāyunā jagadātmanā kathyamānam dvi aja śreṣṭhāḥ śata varṣa sahasrike kaṃṭhasya deva deva syaśūlinaḥ tat aham kīrtayiṣyāmi śṭaṇu dhvam śaṃsita vratāḥ puṇya udyāneṣu tīrtheṣu devatāyataneṣu ca giri śṛṃgeṣu tuṃgeṣu śaṃkara upavaneṣu ca evam bhaktyā mahātmānam munayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma rūpābhiḥ gīrtti śva ātharvaṇa ādi bhiḥ ohūṃkāra namaskāraiḥ arcayaṃti sadāśivam pravṛtte jyotiṣām cakre madhyam prāpte divākare devatā niyata ātmānaḥ sarvetiṣṭham titāṃkalām prāṇinām jīvana udbhavaḥ namaḥ te nīlakaṃṭhāya eti uvāca sadāgatiḥ tam śrutvā abhāvi tātmānaḥ munayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ vālakhilya iti vikhyātāḥ pataṃga sahacāriṇaḥ aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇām ūrdhvaretaḥ sām bhojanāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ etat ruhyam pavitrāṇām puṇyam puṇyavatām vara nīlatākena kaṃṭhasya prakāreṇa avikāpateḥ yāvā eva acaḥ pravartate sarvāḥ tāḥ preritāḥ tvayā varṇa sthāne gatā iva vācaḥ nivartate vetti tāvat smṛtiḥ medhā samānaḥ yam tvam īśvara brūhi maṃgala saṃyuktām kathām pāpa praṇāśinīm śrutvā vācam tatas teṣām munīnām bhāvitātmanām pratyuvāca mahā tejāḥ vāyuḥ loka namaskṛtaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam ṛṣayaḥ viprāḥ veda vedāṃga pāragāḥ nīya śikṣāyām prasiddham vasiṣṭhaḥ nāma dharma ātmā mānasaḥ vai prajāpateḥ krauṃca jīvita harttāram gaurīṭa daya naṃdanam mahiṣa asura nārīṇām nayana aṃjana taskaram mahāsenam mahātmānam megha stanita niḥsvanam tam ānataḥ praharṣe ṇa bālakam su accha rūpiṇam brūhi maṃgala saṃyuktām kathām puṇyam jana priyām etat āptāya dāṃtāya bhaktāya brūhi pṛcchate śrutvā vākyam tatas tasya vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ pratyuvāca mahā tejāḥ daitya ariḥ pāvaka upamaḥ śrūyatām vadatām śreṣṭha ka thyamānam idam mayā umā utsaṃga upaviṣṭena yathāpūrva śrutam mayā pārvatyāḥ ca eva saṃvādam śarvasya ca mahātmanaḥ tat aham kīrtayi ṣyāmi tvad priya artham ahā mune taruṇa āditya saṃkāśe tapta kāṃcana bhūṣite vajña sphaṭika sopāne citra padṛ śilā tale jāṃbūnada maye divyena nānā dhātu vibhūṣite nānā druma latā ākīrṇe nityam puṣpa phala āśraye haṃsa kāraṃḍava ākīrṇe kinnaraiḥ upaśobhite jīvaṃjīvaka jātīnām virutaiḥ ca eva kūjite kokila ālāpa bahule siddha cāraṇa sevite vaṃśa vāditra nirghoṣaiḥ śrotra iṃdriya manoharaiḥ dolā alaṃvita saṃpāta sura saṃgha niṣevite dhvaja ālaṃbita dolānām ghaṃṭānām ninadāvate varṇa kī gha upa bahule nityam vyāpāra saṃkule krīḍā ceṣṭita vādyānām nirghoṣaiḥ pūrṇa kaṃdare deha varṇaiḥ vicitra aiśva prakrīḍita gaṇa īśvaraiḥ bila āḍha vadanaiḥ śva ugraiḥ kroṣṭu vānara mūrttibhiḥ vināyaka upaha viśeṣaḥ vaṃśa vāditra nirghoṣaiḥ a kṛtrimaiḥ kīcaka vanaiḥ varṇitam vai vāta pitta śleṣmaṇā avaiṣamya nimitte hasta jaṃdhaiḥ pralaṃba uṣṭhaiḥ sthūla jaṃ caiḥ tathā aparaiḥ gokarṇaiḥ ekakarṇaiḥ ca mahākarṇaiḥ akarṇakaiḥ eka pādaiḥ mahā pādaiḥ vahu pādaiḥ a pādaiḥ taḥ vicitra ratna aṃga vibhūṣaṇa ācita śilā tale hema maye manorame sukha upaviṣṭam madana aṃganāśanam uvāca vākyam giri rāja putrī bhagavan devadeveśa govṛṣa aṃkita vāhana tava kaṃṭhe mahādeva śvājata iṃbuda saṃnibham śubham śuddham nīlāṃjana caya upamam kim idam deva kaṃṭhe kāma aṃga nāśana hetuḥ kaḥ kāraṇam kiṃvā yena idam nīlam īśvara śrutvā a vākyam tatas tasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ pārvatī priyaḥ kathām maṃgala saṃyuktām kathayā māsa śaṃkaraḥ mathyamānā iṣṭate pūrvam kṣīroda isura dānavaiḥ agre samutthitam tasmāt viṣam kāla anala prabham ca mahā dyutiḥ kimarthā evai mahābhāga abhītāḥ audvigna mānasāḥ mayā aṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam bhavatām saṃpravartitam vimāna cāriṇaḥ sarve sarve svacchanda cāriṇaḥ prajāḥ karma vipākena śaktāḥ yūyam pravartitum yena yūyam samudvignāḥ mṛgāḥ siṃha arditāḥ iva abhavat megha saṃkāśam nīlāṃjana caya upamam prādurbhūtam viṣam ghoram saṃvarta agni sama prabham kālakūṭam iti khyātam vipam viṣama vega dhṛk tam dṛṣṭvā asura saṃgha aśrva daityāḥ ca eva varānane viṣaṇṇa vadanāḥ sarve tvām eva śaraṇam gatāḥ brahmā uvāca namaḥ tubhyam virūpākṣa namaḥ te divyacakṣuṣe sāṃkhyāya ca eva yogāḥ ya bhūta grāmāya vainamaḥ namaḥ trailokya nāthāya bhūtānām pataye namaḥ namaḥ surāri haṃtre ca soma sūrya agni cakṣuṣe madana aṃga vināśāya kālakālāya vai namaḥ kapardi nekarālāya śaṃkarāya harāya ca kapāline virūpāyam śivāya vara de namaḥ tripura ghne makha ghnāya maṃtrāṇāṃpataye namaḥ namaḥ kamala hastāya digvāsāya śikhaṃḍine agrāyaca eva ca ugrāyaviprāya ane kacakṣuṣe aciṃtyāya cacityāya ciṃtyā aciṃtyā yavainamaḥ bhaktānām ārtti nāśāya nārāyaṇa priyāya ca umā priyāya sarvāya naṃdiva analāya ca pakṣa māsa ardha māsāya ṛtu saṃvatsarāya ca bahurūpāya muṃḍāya daṃḍine ca savalkine ṛk yajuḥ sāma rūpāya puruṣāya īśvarāya ca loka akṣa ya nipātāya aiṃdrāya varuṇāya ca evam bhagavatā apūrva trahmaṇā aloka kartṛṇā da tvā a sumukhayā aprītyā avidyayā aham athā bravam bhagavan bhūta bhavya īśa bhūta adhipa mahā tapaḥ śrutvā vākyam tatas utra lā pratyuvāca ambuja īkṣaṇaḥ bhūta bhavya bhavat nātha śrūyatām kāraṇam mama abha vat megha saṃkāśam nīlāṃjana caya upamam prādurbhūtam viṣam ghoram saṃvarta agni sama prabham kāla mṛtyum iva udbhūtam yugāṃta āditya varcasam trailokyeṣu ādi sūrya ābha visphuraṃtam samaṃtataḥ bhītāḥ draṣṭum vṛṣabha vāhanam tam pivasva mahādeva lokānām hita kāmyayā yena abhyuddhata mātreṇa kṛtaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ janārdanaḥ bruvataḥ tuvarāḥ rohebrahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ bāḍham iti eva tat vākyam pratigṛtya varānane me mahā ghoram viṣam sura gaṇa ardanam kaṃṭha samabhirakṣam tu dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇa aṃbuja īkṣaṇe taṃdṛvā utpala patra akṣam viṣaṃkāla anala prabham takṣakam nāga rājānam lelihānam iva aparam tadā uvāca mahā tejā trahmā lokapitāmahaḥ śobha setvam mahādeva kaṃṭhe na anena suvrata paśyatām sura saṃghānām daityānām ca varānane yakṣa gaṃdharva nāgānām piśāca uraga rakṣasām tatas śrīkaṃṭha tām ama saṃpaśyamānāḥ sura daitya saṃgha adṛṣṭāḥ param vismayam āgata aśva tatas sura gaṇāḥ sarve sa yakṣa āraga rākṣasāḥ ūcuḥ prāṃjala yaḥ bhūtvā matta mātaṃga gāmini pṛthak vibhā ukta pralaye ca gomā iti idam uktvā vacanam sura iṃdrāḥ gatā vimānaiḥ anila ugra vegaiḥ ninādayaṃtaḥ vidi tām kathā śubhām vipaṃtasya varāroheḥ sthāvaram jaṃgamam cayat gātram prāpya ca su śroṇi kṣipram ca pratihanyate śamayati aśubham ghoram svam aṃca apakarṣati iti paṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ strīṇām vallabha tām yāti sabhāyām pārthivasya ca gacchati kṣemam adhvānam śarīrena asti tad bhayam śarīrabhede vakṣyāmi gatim tasya varānane hari śmaśruḥ nīlakaṃṭhaḥ śaśāṃka aṃkita mūrddhajaḥ naṃdi tulya balaḥ śrīmā naṃdi tulya parākramaḥ kṣatriśūlī vara vāhanaḥ vicarati akhilān siṅghaḥ sapta lokān mama ājñayā mama tulya balaḥ bhūtvā tiṣṭhati ābhūtasaṃplavam mama bhaktyā varārohe ye ca śṛṇvaṃti imāḥ navāḥ teṣām gatim pravakṣyāmi iha loke paratra ca pādam vāyat iva api ardha ślokam śloka ardham eva ca iti itihāsam girirāja putri mayā a su tuṣṭena jānane niveditam puṇya phala ādi yuktam svayam ca gītam caturānanena kathām imām puṇya phalā di yuktām nivadya devyāḥ śaśi baddha mūrdhajaḥ saha umayā aprabhuḥ jagāma kailāsa guhā aṃguha priyaḥ adhītya sarvaiḥ likhitam sa tad kṣaṇam jagāma ca āditya patham dvijottamāḥ iti śrī śivamahā vyāsaḥ uvāca icchāmi vettum purāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām nīlakaṃṭhastavaḥ nāma paṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ tathā eva muninā muni iṃdraḥ praśnam yathāvat kathayāṃcakāra dagdham yathā tat ripuram tathā tat śṭaṇuṣva putra iti yathā bruvan vacaḥ ādāya daityam saha tārakākṣam vidyutprabham viṣṇu sama prabhāvam te śīta kāla hima parvatasya agrīṣma ica paṃcajvalana abhitaptāḥ abhe payaḥ plāvita bhūmi bhāge ceruḥ tapaḥ prāk ṛṣayaḥ prayatnāt teṣām agāt dvi isama saha saṃtathā ayutam ca ugra tapaḥ sthitānām siṃhāḥ āditya tejaḥ pratimāna vīryāḥ babhūvuḥ āditya tapaḥ prakāśāḥ tam aṃtapaḥ vaḥ agha śata pramocanam varam tu idānīm vṛṇuta iha thṛṣṭāḥ taṃtrām jaliḥ bhūmi niviṣṭa jānuḥ mayaḥ sureśam praṇataḥ abhyuvāca dātum na śakyaḥ varaḥ eṣa tubhyam tasmāt varam sāṃtaram etat eva tvam putra yācasva tatas pradāsye cittam camā tad anujān yathā bhūt pūrṇa saha setu puram samānām saṃghībhavati ardha nimeṣa śrutvā tatas tat vacanam mayasya brahmā avaram tam hṛṣita aṃtarātmā dadau abhīvṛt danuja adhipāya da tvā varam ca sva puram jagāma tat etat puratrayam ati laukika śobhi manaḥ bhilaṣita nikhila vastu jāta kalpatarum nirmāya cadra aṃśu saṃsṛṣṭatama aiśvaramyaiḥ śīta anila āhlāda sukha praveśaiḥ muktā pravālaiḥ maṇi khaṃḍa citraiḥ ālaṃbitaiḥ citra taḍit prakāśaiḥ prāsāda paṃkti sthita ratna khaṃ ḍaiḥ mahā mahīdha yuti saṃnikāśaiḥ vāpībhiḥ ākrāṃta viśuddha bhābhiḥ praphulla nīlotpala saṃvatābhiḥ tad punnakha ābhinna payodharābhiḥ ākīrṇa rakta aṃta vilocanābhiḥ sa vrīḍa mīṣat capala īkṣaṇābhiḥ yoṣidbhiḥ ākīrṇam atīva reje puram dvitīyam rajata ālayam yat vidyutprabhāya asura rāj pradāya haimam tṛtīyam svayam eva divyam jagrāha rājā amaye ātmanā arthe adhi sthitam tat tripuram tadā abhūt sa maṃtribhiḥ taiḥ danu rāja siṃhaiḥ saha viprabhṛtyaiḥ matvā atu teṣām prasabham nipatya nānāvidha aśva kuratīva pīḍāḥ vanāni vaiśvāja puraḥsarāṇi saṃbhidya tāni ātta sumāni cakruḥ tepām atītaḥ samayām mahān alam prakurvata deva vināśanāni vattam yathā sarvam aśeṣam etat nyavedayan āśu pitāmahāya tān āha devaḥ kamalāsanaḥ tu sarvān su reśān pratisāṃtvayitvā mahā balāḥ te tripura asura iṃdra ahaṃtum na śakyāsu abalāt bhavadbhiḥ tasmāt yaviṣṇuḥ aham ca yuṣmān pragṛtya śaṃbhum śaraṇam prayāmaḥ gatiḥ sa dānaḥ śaśi bhṛt sureśaḥ sarvān balān dhakṣyati śūlapāṇiḥ tathā eva te tu pratipadya deva brahma arka śakra anila pāvaka āyāḥ kaiḥ lāsam āgamya sureśvaram na i dṛṣṭvā haram tuṣṭuvuḥ ādṛtāḥ te pūṣṇā eti pūṣṇaḥ udanta nāśanāya dakṣa yajña nāśe namaḥ tu caṃdra ardha jaṭā kalāpa kānti prabhā dyotita śekharāya sthitāya nityam himava girīṃde kailāsa vāsāya namaḥ sadā eva caṃdra arka śaka agni pitāmahānām khaṣṭre namaḥ deva vara īśvarāya sūkṣmāya nityam parameśvarāya nityam namaḥ sarga gatāya gātre namaḥ parāya atiparātmane paraḥśatam namaḥ śaṃkara saṃjñitāya soma anila arka jvalana ambu bhūmi vyoma ātmaka ardi sṛjate namaḥ astu pūṣṇena moṃ ta vināśa nāyaka kāma aṃga nāśāya namaḥ astu nityam namaḥ sṛje yajña surāsu rāṇām namaḥ tṛtīya īkṣaṇa dhāriṇe namaḥ śmaśāna vāsāyana maḥ sadā eva namaḥ astu daitya aṃga vināśanāya namaḥ sadā moha vināśanāya ajñāna nāśāya ca te namaḥ astu namaḥ sadā mokṣa vara pradāya namaḥ sadā cāmṭata saṃsthitāya namaḥ stu caṃḍa īśa vara pradātre yoga īśvarāṇām vara dāya tubhyam harāya śarvāya namaḥ namaḥ stu bhīmāya śaṃbho ca namaḥ sadā eva prasādyamānaḥ prasādam tuṣṭaḥ pareṣām tuvara pradāya evam ca teṣām stuvatām surāṇām troṃ draviṣṇu arka puraḥsarāṇām prītaḥ tayā stotra viśeṣa bhaktyā jagāda vākyam parama
