praṇamya parameśvaram uṃcha vat te hiraṇyasya naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ svayam eva prayātā aham dvijāt pūjām pratīcchitum māhātmyam tasya tat dṛṣṭvā brāhmaṇa sya tapasvinaḥ gata arha vismayam deva dvijāḥ śreṣṭhatamāḥ iti devebhyaḥ api garīyāṃsaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ iti me matiḥ sattvam nāśayate moham sacā agnau saṃpravartate vanhitejaḥ sa amātya ete mahā tmānaḥ dvijātayaḥ sarvatas prabhavantaḥ tena asti teṣām nivāraṇam mā yuktā dārjavam tu viśiṣyate asādhyam haṃti pāpa anisama tā moha baṃdhanam purā bhāgīrathī tīret dijaḥ parama dharma vid nāmnā ādānaruciḥ nāma oṃcha vṛttiḥ babhūvaha sarva vidyā vinīta ātmā sarva bhūta abhaya pradaḥ ṣaṣṭhe kāle tatas śnāti tasya idam vratam utamam babhūva atyartham aciṣmān arka anyoḥ api tejasā tasya evam tapasā avanhiḥ prītaḥ tuṣṭim agāt parām guru tuṣṭiḥ babhūva asya samīhita phala pradaḥ kadācid atha kālena ṣaṣṭhe kāle samāgate na apaśyat atithiṃkaṃcid tapasā ācasa kheditaḥ yadā an āsāditaḥ tena dina aṃte pi atithiḥ kvacid a prāpya eva tu tam kaṃcid upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ patnī ca asya mahābhāgā pati bhakti vrate sthitā yathā ca asyāḥ patiḥ cakra tathā eva api akarot sadā dvaṃdva samāvṛtaḥ tathā agniḥ tasya tam jñātvā aniścayam paramam mahat śvapāka sadṛśam rūpam vikṛtam kutsitam vahis vipra iṃdraḥ paryaṭan atithi īpsayā apaśyat ṛkṣa mūla stham ghoram vikṛta rūpiṇam śvapāka śīta saṃkṣubdham na ekatra vikrośatam catāta iti sacā apaśyat vijottamaḥ kṛpaṇam tam sadā a dṛṣṭvā svapam tat vijasattamaḥ śīta apanayana artha ca vanhi prajvālayan dvijaḥ viśītam vanhi saṃsargāt samāśvastam uvācasaḥ tam uvāca tatas udīnaḥ śvapākaḥ tapasāṃnidhim śvapākaḥ ham dvijaśreṣṭham atyam annam iva hi na aham saṃskṛtam āhartu yogya unnam iti ca atravīt tam evam vādinam dhyānāt jñātvā vahnim upasthitam provāca dvija śārdūla edam vai cana kovidaḥ na aham jātim tava arcābhiḥ pūjayāmi tava anagha ātmā vai sarvatas jyeṣṭhaḥ sarva prāṇiṣu ayam sthitaḥ ā tmā anantam aham bhadra pūjayāmi param śivam kṛmi kīṭa ādi sarpa iṣu śvapākeṣu dvijātiṣu yadā sarva gata utdi ātmā tadā akutsā kathaṃcana atra śloke bhuktvā asaṃskṛtam annam tvam pāvaya asmān anugrahāt evam uktaḥ dvijeṃdreṇa śvapākaḥ prītimān tadā gṛhaṃgataḥ saviprasyaviprāḥ nugraha lipsayā vimuktaḥ saha patnī yātu prāptavān amṛtam padam evam ārjava saṃpannaḥ bā hmaṇaḥ kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ na kiṃcid prāpnuyāt devi śubha aśubha param padam evam kathitam naga iṃdra tanaye māhātmyam atyuttamam śṛṇvan nityam idam paṭhan śva vidhivat siddhaḥ śuciḥ mānavaḥ puṇyam saukhyam atha api abhīpsita phalam tejaḥ valam prāpnuyāt ākhyāna me tat kathitam yathāvat mahā mahīdhā iṃdra sute dvijānām dṛṣṭa prabhāvā amamate dvijeṃdrāḥ mahā munīnām padam adhyavātsuḥ dvija māhātmyam ullikhya pārvatī parameśayoḥ babhūva ca evam saṃvādaḥ puṇyaḥ pāpa bhaya āvahaḥ yat ca anyat aṃbuda śyāma pārāśarya tapodhana śrotavyam manyase mattaḥ tat śṭaṇuṣva samāhitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāya tripaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca prāpya pāśupatam jñāḥ nam brahma ādyāḥ te sura uttamāḥ lebhire paramam tatvam jñānam ca api mahā dyute kīdṛśam vā abhava iti ogam jñānam pāśupatam śubham brahma ādyāḥ devatāḥ vyāsa dakṣa yajña mukhe purā śaṃkaram śaraṇam jagmu vīrabhadra bhaya arditāḥ gaṇa iṃdraiḥ abhiyuktāḥ te bhasmakūṭa ajire sthitaiḥ abhayante tathā raudrāḥ paśavaḥ dīkṣitāḥ iva bhasma rūṣita gātrāṇām śaṃkara vrata dhāriṇām sva yogam ca dadau teṣām tadā devaḥ umāpatiḥ sarvāsām mokṣa vidyānām yatra tvam iti ha ucyate dīkṣām pāśupatīm prāpya praviśaṃti maheśvaram na adharme ṇa vinā adharmaḥ na dharmeṇa vinā aśubham dahet soma kkṛtam vanhirim dhanam ca analam viduḥ kṛta akṛtam dahati agniḥ bhūyas soma samāhṛtaḥ bhasmanā a saṃcitāḥ sarve brahma ādyāḥ abhimāninaḥ bhasmanaḥ tejasā avīrya yasmāt pāvanam īśvaram ātmānam śaṃkaram nyasya yatusnānam bhasmanā ācaret prabhavanti surāḥ somāt pitaraḥ vanhi saṃbhavāḥ agnīṣoma ātmakam tasmāt jaga tsarvam pratiṣṭhitam tejasā tasya saṃsṛṣṭaḥ mucyate bhasmanā dvijaḥ sāṃkhyam vidyām tapaḥ ca eva tyaktvā adharma āśu avaidikān śīghram eva param yogam prāpya mucyati baṃdhanāt evam tra tam mahat prāpya śuḥ raḥ pāśupataḥ muniḥ bhāvaḥ trīṇi ambakāni netrāṇi yasya iti vigrahaḥ tamasā a śūnyam om itye idam māheśvaram jñānam gutyam paramam abhyaset jñeyam jñānam tathā ajñātā trayam dehe tathā sthitam ātma aya śvayathā vāsaḥ sthāna traya samanvitaḥ nāḍīṣu ca yathātdyātmā ātmani eva avatiṣṭhati sarvatas sarva bhūteṣu nigūḍhaḥ tiṣṭhate tathā na sevitum vinā jñānam samyak ātmā kathaṃcana rūpa śabda rasa atītam kaḥ tam vetti maheśvaram ta thā atyaham mahābhāga prasādāt ryaṃbakasya tu ātma jñāne para upāya kathayāmi tava anagha sūryaḥ ca caṃdramāḥ śuddham mahat ca vimala makṣaram param īśvaram sarva mātra guṇa atītam nirvikāram niraṃjanam bahis antar caram dīnam avikāram param dhruvam vijñānam paramam yat tat akṣaram brahma tat śṛṇu om iti ekākṣaram pūrva akṣaram tasmāt vinirgatam oṃkāraḥ brahma śasya te akāre tatra viṣṇuḥ syāt tukāre tu pitāmahaḥ makāraḥ bhagavān īśaḥ mātrāyām prakṛtiḥ smṛtā patnī rūpeṇa sā śaṃbhuṃbhuṃ jate prakṛtim punar brahma viṣṇū sthitau tau ca devau īśvara saṃjñitau saṃpad virūpam prakṛtiḥ sarva viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiḥ tau ā kramya maheśaḥ taṃ prakṛtiḥ tau guṇa ātmakau mahāvalaḥ vibhuḥ bhūtvā naktaṃsaṃhāram eva hi oṃkāram dhyāyataḥ yena atītya prakṛtim mune satama āditya mukta ātmā anṛta arthaḥ jāyate muniḥ na evaṃjanā vimārga sthāḥ śuddha hetu parāyaṇāḥ bhoktāram prakṛteḥ īśam param tattva iṣu saṃsthitam oṃkāram prakṛteḥ nityam tad madhye bhāsvaram svayam īśvaraḥ usau dadāti īśaḥ samuktaḥ paśubaṃdhanaiḥ na īśvarā a prakṛtiḥ khyātā guṇa karma ādi bhedinī bṛhat tvāt gṛhatī śyāmā viṣṇu tvāt vibhavā smṛtā sa abhimānā bhavet sṛṣṭiḥ bho ktāṃtasyā maheśvaraḥ aṣṭa bāhu tri pādā ca paṃca deha mukhī tathā jaganmātā smṛtā atyeṣā guṇatraya vikāra jā ubhe śubha aśubhe tasyām vidyā avidyā tathā ubhaya artha pramā yāgaḥ kriyā anuṣṭhānam eva ca nimittam bhavaneya anetārāḥ saṃkṣepataḥ tu amī īśvarāt jātaḥ oṃkāraḥ saca tasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ atas kṛtvā gaṃ yoginaḥ kapila ādayaḥ saḥ eva sarva yoga ātmā akāraṇam saca eva tu īśa bhojyau guṇa ātmānau ru tva viṣṇu pitāmahau saṃ sā ra tāḍanau mūḍhau sarva nitya samau ubhau īśvara itu bhavet vidvān adhyāna yoga parāyaṇaḥ yena asau īśvaraḥ bhinnaḥ yogena ātmani saṃsthitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām vibhūtiyogaḥ nāma catuṣpaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ātmā sūkṣmaḥ manaḥ buddhiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ guṇāḥ tathā bhūtāni iṃdriya saṃbhāraḥ tanmātrāṇi daśa anilāḥ ātma atatrasa jīvaḥ tu sumanaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ tat svapna stham iti prāhuḥ saṃsiddhāḥ śiva yoginaḥ jvālinī stimitā ca usrā vidyā vidyā viśālinī mālinī śaṃkarī ca eva sumitrā bodhinī tathā etāḥ daśa mahānāḍyaḥ jīve smin tāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ śayānam prati co huddhaḥ bhāvaiḥ bhāṣaiḥ samāhitaḥ śabda ādi viṣayebhyaḥ tu ātma sarva gatāḥ trayaḥ sadbhiḥ pūrva saṃyuktau jīvaḥ īkṣayate punar ahaṃkāraḥ manaḥ buddhiḥ bhāva śvatasraḥ deha jāḥ sahanā eva na tiṣṭhati vārayanti śarīriṇam te evam vihitāḥ sarve jīvaḥ ca eva tu paṃcamaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ cetaḥ saḥ eva saṃproktam saḥ eva puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ upya ja āraṃbha bhūtaḥ bhāskara saṃcaraḥ rasam ātma amahauṣadhyaḥ sa anugaḥ bhāva vistaraḥ ahaṃkāraḥ gata aśa śvamṭatyu duḥkham anāmayam kāma roṣa ja vā aduṣṭāḥ su dharmāḥ śrābhitāḥ samāḥ viṣṇuḥ buddhiḥ yathā kārya kāraṇam bhūmiḥ eva ca jñāna vairāgyam ākāśam rāja saṃbhāva vista raṃ jīva madhye sthitā a sūkṣma a vidhūma a pāvakaṃśikhā amṭatam sarva bhūtānām gatiḥ ca eva hisā parā madhye tasya agni saṃkāśaḥ jīvaḥ protaḥ ūna dṛśyate sarasā lohitā mukhyā protā rasavatī tathā vidhūmā ca amṭatā ca evanaṃdinī baśnuvistarā etāḥ sūkṣmatarāḥ nāḍyaḥ saṃbhidya daśa pāvakam paryaṭatisadāsomam bhūtādhāram payovatam satābhiḥ tarpitaḥ somaḥ sarva aṃtara sa mīpatas śabdāpayati vṛddhaḥ tām jīva madhya aṃga tām śivām tat eva amṛtam ākhyātam yat ca eva ātma dam uttamam tayā ayat ahi somasya śikhayā a kalpita āplavaḥ prājñaḥ sarva yoga sanvitaḥ yā a bhūta iṣu surā nāḍī sā suṣumnā pratiṣṭhitā bhāvāḥ kriyāḥ ghṛṇā para jugupsā kuśalaṃmokṣaḥ katham yogaḥ sādhanīyā etya āha sa hi iti gamana ādya āśvayebhāva amanasaḥ caivayā ghṛṇā kuryāt ahaṃkāraḥ tat jñātvā maraṇam tyajet nikṣipya ca kutas karma tad vinā kuśa laṃkutas yaime viṣayāḥ kiṃcid vidyāḥ bhoktā vanhiḥ smṛtaḥ teṣām tvacā na alpena bādhyate iti jñātvā atya jevitām sarva yoga rataḥ sadā dharma vāda kṣayam lokān icchāmām badhyate katham kriyayā a yoga viduṣaḥ śaṃkaram vratam āsthitāḥ gacchanti sva tanum tyaktvā abhitvā māyām paraṃpadam idam anyat param jñānam asya sūkṣmataram sphuṭam yoginaḥ yat na jānaṃti yata sūkṣmam parama uttamam muktvā a pāśupatān śuddhāni anna bhūteṣu vidyate manaḥ buddhiḥ ahaṃkāra aiṃdriyāṇi guṇaḥ kṣayam na spṛśaṃti sat ātmānam vikārāḥ tasyate bahis sadṛśyate ca bhagavān na tu prāyaḥ kathaṃcana sarva bhāva guṇānām antam acityam parameśvaram jñānena ye prapaśyaṃti yoginaḥ te parāmatāḥ chāyā eṣām dṛśyatā iyātu cakṣuḥ viṣayasam gatā kanīnī aṃta sthitiḥ vyāsa hetuḥ sarva śarīriṇām atra āste sasaraḥ jñātvā sūkṣmaḥ madhya gataḥ nayaḥ ti nāḍyaḥ jīva ica saṃsthitāḥ gāṃdhārī vijayā ca eva etāḥ prāṇa vahāḥ smṛtāḥ yute yogāt ayaḥ daśa ūṣmāṃtāḥ nāḍyaḥ nāgena saṃbhṛtāḥ sa prāṇaḥ bahis antar ca tarpayan havyavāhanaḥ vṛddhasya vārayet dāḥ puṃsā abalena ca nāḍī tu anyā suṣumnī iti soma vanhi svavasthitā na abhinibaddhāyām nābhi deśa tatāyām kūrmaḥ pūrva uktaḥ vāyuḥ tasmin śvāturake dehe kumāreca analam sthitāḥ śudhyate sāriṇī samāna dhyāna saṃyukta āraktam ātmā atra pūryate tadā avāyoḥ parovāyuḥ sacakūrmā iha ucyate nāḍyām nābhi nibaddhāyām natāyām tau pratiṣṭhitau dhare nāḍyām vāyuḥ alpāḥ tad ūrdhvatas adhastāt pāda sanaddhaḥ kūrmaḥ śirasi ca sthitaḥ yovāyuḥ devadatta ākhyaḥ kṛta kāryāya bodhinaḥ devadatta mahānāgalaka kūrma dhanaṃjayāḥ prāṇāḥ te mayi vikhyātāḥ cakra yoga abhipālinaḥ huta śeṣam pradiṣṭam vā somam tatra pratiṣṭhati somam vidhitsate yajñān na teṣām mukti lakṣaṇam dīptiḥ agniḥ smṛtāyām tu sravitaḥ ca atra yatrasā tarpaṇam parvaṇā tasya kaṇikāyām tadā smṛtam netre paśyati yat jyotiḥ tārā rūpam prakāśakam sa jīvaḥ sarva bhūtānām ātmānam ca samāsthitaḥ jyotiṣaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ sūkṣmam tatvam tat paramam smṛtam tat ca amṛtam samākhyātam jñāna labhyam tat ucyate tasmāt parataram vijñāna dā gatiḥ jñātvā evam saṃtyajet moham guṇatraya vikāra jam vimoham tyaja saṃsarga akriyāḥ kārya a vivarjitāḥ tam viśaṃti maheśānam īśvaram kṛta kāriṇī iti tatvam samākhyātam vyāsa māheśvaram tava ta brahma paripūrṇa tu nāma rūpaṃcana asti te iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāya piṃcapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca aho jñānam tvayā ākhyātam ajñāna vinivarttanam adya ahaṃgata saṃde ho mahādevam paraṃprati śaṃkarāt prakṛtiḥ jātau ahma viṣṇu śiva ātmakau jñātvā ṣaḍīśam īśānam mucyate sarva baṃdhanāt iti paṃcapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ niṣkalam sakalam jñātvā asayaḥ eva prakāśate tvad prasādāt aham tāta prāpta jñānā gatā śubhaḥ niḥsaṃdehaḥ abhavat śāṃtaḥ praṣṭavyam na anyat asti me tathā api jñāpayāmi idaṃtatvam ākhyātum arhasi evam vijñāna saṃpannaḥ prāptayaḥ gomuniḥ munim vinā kleśam tanum tyaktvā ayogī yoga bala anvitaḥ īśvara dhyāna saṃprāptam upāyam yoga lakṣaṇam kathayasva muni śreṣṭha praṣṭavyam nā anyat asti me evam uktaḥ sa śiṣyeṇa vyāsena su mahātmanā śṛṇu vyāsa param jñānam īśvara dhyāna kāraṇam sva icchayā yena mucyaṃte yoginaḥ jñāna tatparāḥ sva deham vighnavat yatktvā ṣaḍūiṃśena yama anu yāt saṃcaraṃti śarīriṇaḥ setuḥ tāsām tatānām tu kaṇikā madhyam āśritāḥ tam āśri tya tusā nāḍī bāhya pāda iṣu saṃsthitā smṛtā bhūyastuyā nāḍyaḥ tāḥ eka karam āśritāḥ niḥsamāne sahasrāṇi nāḍīnām paraḥ mātmani tāsām ekaikaśas bhedaḥ sūkṣma sūkṣmataraḥ smṛtaḥ tāsu saṃcarate prāṇaḥ karṇikā madhya saṃbhavaḥ tatra ātmā asūkṣma sam lakṣyaḥ prāk uktaḥ tiṣṭhati dvija vidyayā diśi paśyan tāḥ tam paśyet yogam āsthitaḥ tat tejaḥ sarva nāḍīṣu vibhaktam sarva dehinām tāḥ ca nāḍyaḥ manaḥ saṃgāt manaḥ kurvati viṣṭutam tat tejaḥ cakṣuḥ āhatya sarva nāḍī samāśritam vāyuḥ varṇa jayaḥ nāma yothṛdī hasphuret sadā trīṇi tasya mukhāni āhuḥ śiraḥ nābhiḥ tṛd eva hi ye pramāṇāḥ tava ākhyātāḥ vāyavaḥ kīrtitā mayā mukha anisthānāni prayogāt abhyāsāt yoginaḥ jīvāḥ iti saṃbaṃdhaḥ śārīram śarīra jam iti arthaḥ dhanaṃjayasya te sarve vaśagāḥ tad nibaṃdhanāḥ na vaśā āgaṃtum anyatra tasmin tiṣṭhati saṃsthitāḥ nābhibaṃdhanam āsādya nāḍī cakram samāśritāḥ dvitīyam karṇikāyām tu tṛtīyam tālu saṃsthitam vikāra param śūlam trividha utkrāṃtiḥ ucyate hṛdi śūlam param nāḍyām tāla paraśuḥ āsthitaḥ tāsu kehadi baddha śva padma nāḍyām niyojitaḥ bhānau viyojitam sarvam prāṇam eva vimuṃcati ākṣipya tritayam nāḍyām kaṇikāyām niyojanam yayā ajīvān abādhyam yoginaḥ tat idam śṭaṇu bālyaḥ śarīra jaḥ ca iti smṛtyuḥ dvividhaḥ ucyate matyuḥ iti khyātaḥ śārīram kāla jaḥ jarayā yuktaḥ roga jaḥ vyādhi saṃjñitaḥ yoga upāya rutaḥ yaśva yaśca kāla kṛtaḥ kṣayaḥ tayoḥ bheda adhikārau samāsatas yogam ākrāmataḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate śrotra saṃdhi jaḥ śabda sparśaḥ guṇa atītaḥ rūpa yogam vimuṃca ti udānaḥ nāma saṃyujya karṇikāyām viśaṃti hi indri yāṇi manaḥ yāṃti manaḥ prāṇa vinirgatam teṣu sarveṣu līneṣu prāṇa vāyum nipīḍayet pīḍyamānāḥ tatas sarve bhavati ekaśas tānilāḥ su saṃyuktam tatas sthānam tatas karma yad ātmakam ekasthā vāyavaḥ sarve pūrayaṃti dhanaṃjayam śeṣaḥ tadīya kūrma ādyāḥ jīvan tyaktvā sa tiṣṭhati eka kāla kṛtā atyeṣā sarva bhūta guṇa sthitiḥ samāsatas saṃkṣepataḥ yogam ākrāmataḥ yoga abhyāsinaḥ śabda yogāt śabda saṃbaṃdhāt anita ājīvitāḥ karaṇaiḥ kriyābhiḥ saha sukham kalyāṇam brahmabhiḥ sadyojāta ādibhiḥ niṣkalam nirguṇam churikām paraśvā piśūlam vā dhārayet muniḥ tatas sarve vilīyaṃte vikārāḥ karaṇaiḥ saha yadā anapaṃca vijñāyat daṣṭvā tu pariniṣṭhitaḥ paṃcabhiḥ brahmabhiḥ pūtaḥ bhasmanā a dīkṣitaḥ dvijaḥ śaṃkara eka manāḥ yogī jñānam etat avāpnute māheśvara bhimaṃyogam niṣkalam mukti kāraṇam yajñāt api na muṃcati vratam a prāpya śāṃkaram mahādeva paraḥ bhūtvā sarva jñānam avāpnuhi na eva amatyā aparam brahma anye viṃdaṃti yoginaḥ śiva yoginaḥ mahādevasya vakṣyāmi tat bhaktyā yena yāṃti hi iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām yogadhyāne ṣaṭpaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ t kumārā uvāca bhūta bhavya bhavānām ca saptānām ūrdhvatas sthitāḥ lokāḥ bhagavataḥ śaṃbhoḥ yatra āste satatam śivaḥ na asau tarka vinirdeśyaḥ lokāḥ tasmin pratiṣṭhitāḥ brahmāṃḍam sakalam tasmin śiva loke pratiṣṭhitam na asau naśyati saṃhāre dhruva sthānam surālayaḥ yatra aham sanaka ādyāḥ ca brahmā ca eva pitāmahaḥ om namaḥ śivāya yeṣu lokeṣu bhagavān saṃsthitaḥ girijāpatiḥ yakṛtaḥ yaḥ cakāla kṣaya āgataḥ tayoḥ bheda vikāra aṇiśṭaṇu vyāsa samāhitaḥ vālakhilya purogāśva siddhāśva kāpila ādayaḥ śiva yogam pariprāptāḥ sattva ādi guṇa varjitāḥ niṣkāma a niṣṭhita avyāsa se vamāna aśva īśvaram parama ātma aca bhāva usau para mosau manīṣiṇām kṣamā satyam dhṛtiḥ ca eva tapaḥ vairāgyam eva ca viṣṇu tvam ca vidhātṛ tvam ādya bodhaḥ maheśa tā atas param paraḥ divye paramāṇoḥ pade sthitaḥ manasaḥ prākṛtasya ādau tat tejaḥ saṃprakāśanaḥ mahāntaḥ sarvatas nityāḥ īśvarāt tat abhūt tadā tasmāt dijasya nirbhedaḥ kṣatrataḥ sa vibhuḥ smṛtaḥ prakṛtiḥ vaiṣṇavī pro ktā asā ca tasmāt vinirgatā amuṣya puratas brahma abrahmaṇaḥ śaṃkara ātmanaḥ yat sthānam vigraha īśasya īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ nāmnā aśiva puram vyāsa gatiḥ īśvara yoginām śatam śata sahasrāṇām yojanānām tat ucyate mahā maṃḍala saṃsthānam tad madhye vimalam śubham mahatā ajātarūpeṇa prākāreṇa sa veṣṭitaḥ śatam śata sahasrāṇām yojanānām yathādiśam divyā marāvatī bhūmiḥ sparśa mātra sukha āvahā vimala iṃdu vikāśāni vāla arka sadṛśāni ca mahā krada pramāṇa ani nānā vaidūrya sannibhāḥ gaṃdhavanti mahārhāṇi vinyastāni mahī tale iṃdranīla nikāśāni mahā maṇi nibhāni ca kvacid kṛṣṇāni raktāni divya gaṃdha vahāni ca utpatrāṇi samaṃta taḥ pure bhagavataḥ śaṃbhoḥ parivārya nivodha tāḥ varadā ca vareṇyā ca vara īśāḥ varavarṇini mahāpagā nānā kusuma saṃmiśra bahu tāni jala amṛtam na devāḥ anamuni iṃdra aśva na asurāḥ paśavaḥ na ca antar bhāva viśuddha āye sarvatas bhakti bhāvitāḥ meru śṛṃga pratīkāśaḥ dṛśyate ca punar punar prāsādaḥ ūna kṣapādiḥ tu kāmadaḥ kanaka āmayaḥ a nirīkṣyaḥ mahā lubdhaiḥ samaṃtāt pariśobhitaḥ vaiḍūrya vyoma saṃkāśaiḥ sphaṭikaiḥ caṃdra saprabhaiḥ pravālaiḥ arka saṃkāśaiḥ iṃdranīla mayaiḥ śubhaiḥ śikhiḥ asmi prakāśābhiḥ kvacid arka svarūpibhiḥ śobhi taṃtu patākābhiḥ virarāja sukha anilam śuśubheta tat puram divyam pādapaiḥ kā mada aiśvitam yathā eva kāṃcanaḥ meruḥ sarveṣām pravaraḥ mahān tatra viśveśvaraḥ sā kṣāt mahābhūta parigrahaḥ sadā aste sahitaḥ patyāṣaḍūiṃśaḥ sa parigrahaḥ lakṣmīḥ medhādhṛtiḥ ca eva śrīḥ kīrtiśva sarasvatī umayā mahitāḥ tatra modate loka mātaraḥ gaṇānām adhipāḥ tatra kuna vāmana rūpiṇaḥ kāmarūpa a mahā veśa a mahā yoga parāyaṇāḥ pramathānām mahātmānaḥ tatra tiṣṭhaṃti suvratāḥ mahākāleśvaraḥ tatra naṃdīśvara gaṇeśvarau gṛhīta paṭṭiśau divyau sadevau devapārśvagau devyāḥ pārśve sthite nityam asi haste mahā bale mahānādaḥ mahā nīśvara vāhanaḥ tatra āste megha saṃkāśaḥ gopatiḥ kāma rūpa dhṛk ghaṃṭā śakti dharaḥ śrīmān pitṛ pārśve vyavasthitaḥ śākhaḥ ca eva viśākha śva naigamī ca eva suvrata jagatpa teḥ śārdūlāḥ kāṃcanāḥ tatra siṃha aśva rajata prabhāḥ prājñānām maṇi tulyānām mahā yoga bala ojasām asaṃkhyātāḥ ttamaḥ sakala aṃkaḥ gṛheśasya de va deva jagat sṛjaḥ sarva bhāva arpita ātmānaḥ ye yogāḥ rudra tatparāḥ yatra tatra mṭatā vat sa teṣām tatra āspadam smṛtam ye ca māheśvara āvyāsa tiṣṭhate śaṃkara ālaye anye iye śaṃkare bhaktāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva samāhi taḥ ahaṃsanaṃdanaḥ ca eva sanaka śva sanātanaḥ dhātā brahmā āsatu jyeṣṭhaḥ nara nārāyaṇau api muniḥ hayaśiraḥ āyaśva yājñavalkya ādayaḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ śuka dharmāṇaḥ parama aiśvarya saṃyutāḥ tiṣṭhati īśvara mūla itu guṇa atītāḥ didṛkṣavaḥ māviśya prāpnuvaṃti āparāhnikam yaiḥ śva dṛṣṭāni vipra iṃdra hara sya āyatanāni tu mahākāleśvaraḥ ca eva gokarṇa śva tathā aśubhau ṣaṣ īśvaraḥ devaḥ śrīgirau vā maheśvaraḥ kārohane ca deveśaḥ mahākāle ca śaṃkaraḥ bhadreśa śva mahādevaḥ śabdakarṇa īśvaraḥ tathā mahākāleśvaraḥ ca eva gokarṇe ca tathā śubhau avimukte ca oṃkāram yaiśvadṛṣṭam mahā mune kāle jāpateḥ yogaḥ pāśupataḥ yasya mayā ate parikīrtitaḥ bhaktiḥ yeṣām tyam kṛtārthāḥ te nara uttamāḥ mṛtāḥ śiva pure vyāsa bhikṣā paṭṭiśa pāṇayaḥ naṃdīśa skaṃda saṃkāśāḥ yoga aiśvarya bala anvitāḥ rudrāḥ bhavanti vipra iṃdra sadā śaṃkara pārśva gāḥ sakalam ca eva jñātvā evam vijñāya parame śvaram bhaviṣya sica yogīca jñānasya asya prabhāvataḥ jñāna sitdhyā smṛtim prāpya brahmāṃḍa udbhava kāraṇe sthiti dharma nirodhānām vijñāna artham anusmṛtya caturdhā vikariṣyasi tvad kṛtāḥ prakariṣyanti tīrthakṛt tvam bhaviṣyasi tasmāt rataṃca saṃprāpya paśu pā śa vimocanam śaṃkara jñāna saṃpanna īśvara ilayam āpsyasi tad kṣaṇāt ca asya yogāḥ usau prādurbhūtaḥ mahā muneḥ abhivādya guruṃcyāsaḥ brahma putram mahā tapāḥ viveśa ca mahī talam evam sanatkumāraḥ tu pṛṣṭaḥ vyāsena dhīmatā muni iṃdra kathayāmāsa purāṇam śiva saṃbhavam śiva yoga dharam dhīram sarva jñāna arṇavam mahat tasmāt yūyam api prāpya vratam pāśu patam dvijāḥ veda artha smṛti saṃpannaḥ citāḥ cakre mahā dyutiḥ purāṇam prathamam prāha ślāghyam naṃdīśvara uddi jaḥ kṛtsnasya jagataḥ vidyāsu ādi kartā yathā haraḥ tathā sarva purāṇānām purāṇaḥ yaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ mṛtyu kālam anuprāpya nate śocaṃti janminaḥ śravaṇāt devadevasya sāyujyam dhāḥ raṇāt vibhoḥ ślāghyāt puṇyam umāpateḥ hi jagatām stotra anuvādam param devyāśvāḥ śaṃbhāva arpita sarva bhāva yam sevitaḥ sarve te jvalat arka vanhi vapuṣa ru yakṣāḥ śaśāṃka tviṣaḥ devasya anucarāḥ catu daśa vara a nirmukta sarva aśubhāḥ sarve harṣa samanvitāḥ śruta dhiyaḥ nānā guṇaiḥ anvitāḥ tata eha paramam prāpya yogam muni iṃdrāḥ parama parama naṃtam prāpya deva adhivāsam tripura haram imam ye jñātavaṃtaḥ prayatnāt gata kaluṣa cayāḥ te prāpnuvate ca mokṣam idam purāṇam paramam pavitram śuciḥ paṭhet yaḥ śṛṇuyāt ca yaḥ naraḥ pitṝṇām paṭhyamānam idam bhavet duṣṭa svapna ādi duṣkarma kali kalmaṣa nāśanam ślokam śloka arthā eva āsa māhitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām saptapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptā iyam saṃhitā bhāvanā eka vaśam devam bhavānī sahitam bhavam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitā samāptā
